# Changelog ‚Äî 2026-06

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): plugin‚Üîplugin dispatch + host-build capability (microkernel foundation F10)

Foundation cutover **F10** ‚Äî two reverse legs on `ExecutorService` (served on the SAME broker
`InvokeWithExecutor` already stands up): **plugin‚Üîplugin dispatch** + **host-build**. Both LIFT the existing
step-confined capabilities (the RunHostStep `ExternalPlugin` arm; the per-step Builder legs) into
class-generic reverse RPCs any plugin can call.

- `InvokeProvider(class, word, op, params, env)`: the host (which owns the registry) resolves another
  provider + Invokes it on the calling plugin's behalf ‚Äî threading the SAME venue executor into an
  OUT-OF-PROCESS target via `InvokeWithExecutor` (a fresh NESTED broker ‚Äî the generalization of the
  RunHostStep ExternalPlugin arm from OpExecute-only to any class/op), or a direct `Invoke` for an in-proc
  target. The shared-capability seam: a SHARED plugin (egress/k8s-gen/arbiter) is "a plugin others invoke".
- `HostBuild(kind, spec)`: the calling plugin requests a HOST-side build (the build ENGINE stays in core) ‚Äî
  the host runs the registered `hostBuilder` for `kind`. F10 registers `plugin-binary` (‚Üí `buildPluginBinary`);
  M13/M14 register `kustomize`/`image`.
- `plugin/proto`: `InvokeProvider`/`HostBuild` RPCs + messages on `ExecutorService`. `plugin_dispatch_reverse.go`:
  the host impls + the `hostBuilders` registry (`registerHostBuilder`/`hostBuilderFor`). `sdk/executor.go`:
  `Executor.InvokeProvider`/`HostBuild` clients. Reference `candy/plugin-example-dispatch`.

F10 is the dispatch + host-build MACHINERY (it moves NO subsystem); M13 (k8s-gen from-box), M14 (build
engine), M16 (egress ‚Äî every writer calls the egress plugin via InvokeProvider), M17 (arbiter) are consumers.

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green incl.
`TestPluginDispatch_InvokeProviderAndHostBuild` (the real `plugin-example-dispatch` plugin, served OOP +
driven via InvokeWithExecutor, calls back `InvokeProvider` to reach an OUT-OF-PROCESS peer over the NESTED
broker ‚Äî proving the HIGH-risk nested round-trip ‚Äî AND `HostBuild` to build a candy's plugin binary, asserting
both results); `task build:charly`; the `check-pod` disposable bed PASSES on the fresh rebuild (no-regression ‚Äî
the new RPCs on ExecutorService don't disturb existing reverse-channel flows).

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): plugin lifecycle phases + bootstrap pre-pass (microkernel foundation F9)

Foundation cutover **F9** ‚Äî ordered plugin lifecycle PHASES + a kernel bootstrap pre-pass, so
early-running capabilities (migrate, egress) can be plugins loaded at the right time. A capability
declares its phase (`sdk.Phase*`: `bootstrap ‚Üí schema ‚Üí load ‚Üí build ‚Üí runtime`, default `runtime`) over
Describe; the kernel invokes BOOTSTRAP-phase plugins on the RAW config bytes BEFORE config
validation/migration, so a bootstrap plugin (migrate, M15) can rewrite a stale config's bytes before the
schema gate rejects them.

- `sdk/phase.go`: the ordered phase vocabulary + `NormalizePhase`. `sdk/ops.go`: `OpBootstrap`.
- `ProvidedCapability.phase` (proto field 9 + sdk + the grpc/inproc provider carry via `buildUnit`/
  `buildUnitInProc` onto the `phaseCarrier`; `phaseOfProvider` defaults to runtime ‚Äî R3 with the F1-F7
  capability-flag pattern). `providerRegistry.providersInPhase`.
- `bootstrap_phase.go`: `runBootstrapPhase` (+ the injectable `runBootstrapPhaseWith`) ‚Äî enumerate
  PhaseBootstrap providers, invoke `OpBootstrap({config})`, thread the transformed bytes. Wired into
  `LoadUnified` BEFORE `gateSchemaVersion`. Re-entrancy-safe: bootstrap plugins are compiled-in (in-proc),
  so this never re-enters the validated-config load (the F4 connect-cycle avoided by construction).
- Reference `candy/plugin-example-bootstrap` (compiled-in, phase:bootstrap, OpBootstrap returns the bytes
  unchanged), added to `compiled_plugins:`.

F9 builds the phase machinery + bootstrap set (a no-op proof); it moves NOTHING. M15 moves migrate onto the
bootstrap phase, M16 moves egress onto a plugin (consumed via F10).

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green incl.
`TestBootstrapPhase_ExampleEnumeratedAndNoOp` (the compiled-in bootstrap plugin is enumerated in
PhaseBootstrap; `runBootstrapPhase` is a no-op) + `TestBootstrapPhase_TransformApplied` (the pre-pass
APPLIES a bootstrap plugin's transformed bytes ‚Äî the migrate path, via injection to avoid global-registry
pollution) + `TestPluginsGenReproducible`; `task build:charly`; the `check-pod` disposable bed PASSES on the
fresh rebuild (no-regression ‚Äî the bed's baked charly runs the bootstrap pre-pass on every LoadUnified with
the no-op compiled in). RCA mid-flight: a transforming test fake registered globally rewrote every later
test's config via the hot-path pre-pass ‚Äî fixed by the `runBootstrapPhaseWith` injection seam.

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): command compile-in ‚Äî the last class gains in-proc compiled-in placement (microkernel foundation F8)

Foundation cutover **F8** ‚Äî "make compile-in work for all six classes." The COMMAND class was the one hole:
its Kong CLI grammar is Go-not-serializable, so a command candy listed in `compiled_plugins:` would register
but never appear in the CLI. Closed via the dynamic-grammar + in-proc-dispatch bridge: `dispatchCommand`
(the dispatch entry, called from `main` after parse) routes a parsed dynamic command by PLACEMENT ‚Äî a
COMPILED-IN command candy (registered in-proc as an `inprocProvider`) dispatches IN-PROC via
`dispatchInProcCommand` ‚Üí `Invoke(OpRun, {"args":[‚Ä¶]})` (the candy's handler runs in charly's own process,
native stdio); an out-of-process one keeps `dispatchExternalCommand`/`syscall.Exec`. The dynamic Kong grammar
(`externalCommandHolder`, pass-through `Args`) is identical for both placements ‚Äî only the dispatch transport
differs (the command half of placement-invisibility). The other five classes already compile in via the
class-agnostic `buildUnitInProc` (verb/kind compiled-in today; step/deploy/builder ride the same machinery).

- `provider_command_external.go`: `dispatchCommand` + `dispatchInProcCommand` (route by placement, R3 with
  the existing `dispatchExternalCommand`); `main.go`'s post-parse dispatch calls `dispatchCommand`.
- `candy/plugin-example-command`: converted to the dual-placement importable pattern (root package
  `examplecommand` with `NewProvider`/`NewMeta` + `Invoke(OpRun)` + `Describe` advertising
  `command:examplecommand`; a `cmd/serve` `sdk.Main(‚Ä¶, CliMain)` shim; both call one shared `runCommand`),
  added to `compiled_plugins:` (regenerated `plugins_generated.go` + `go.work`).

Scope: F8 closes the all-six-class compile-in mandate (command was the last). The full inclusion-surface
CONSOLIDATION (merging the dwindling in-charly-module `providers:` manifest + emptying the 38
`registerDedicatedBuiltin` builtins into `compiled_plugins:`, then deleting those hardcoded paths) completes
WITH the M-series, which moves those builtins onto this now-class-complete surface ‚Äî they cannot be deleted
before the builtins become candies.

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green incl.
`TestCommandCompileIn_ExampleCommandInProc` (the compiled-in command registers in-proc as an `inprocProvider`,
not a `*grpcProvider`/static `CommandProvider`) + `TestPluginsGenReproducible` (regen drift) +
`TestCommandSeam_*`; `task build:charly`; the live `charly examplecommand hello f8-world` prints
`hello f8-world` via the compiled-in in-proc dispatch; the `check-pod` disposable bed PASSES on the fresh
rebuild (no-regression ‚Äî the bed's baked charly includes the compiled-in command).

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî fix(charly): a `run: plugin: <step-word>` (class:step) validates as a deploy act (box-validate gap surfaced during F7)

`charly box validate` rejected a `run: plugin: <step-word>` step whose word is a class:STEP plugin (F3's
external step KIND) with "verb 'plugin' cannot act in build/deploy context ‚Äî runtime-only": `opActsInBuildDeploy`
(`checkspec.go`) only recognized class:VERB plugin words (`ResolveVerb`/`isDeclaredExternalVerb`), not class:step.
A class:step lowers to an `externalStep` that ACTS at deploy (`compileActOp`), so it IS a valid deploy act.
Latent since F3 (its R10 used check-pod + e2e, never main-repo `charly box validate`), surfaced during F7.

- `checkspec.go` `opActsInBuildDeploy`: a `plugin:` word resolving to a ClassStep provider ‚Äî or declared as an
  external step (the not-connected standalone-validate path) ‚Äî acts in build/deploy.
- `plugin_prescan.go`: `declaredExternalStep` + `registerDeclaredExternalStep` + `isDeclaredExternalStep`;
  `registerExternalVerbsFromCandies` now registers class:step words alongside class:verb (the post-scan
  declaration that lets standalone `charly box validate` recognize a not-yet-connected step plugin).
- `candy/plugin-example-stepkind`: the demonstration `run: plugin: examplestepkind` step gains
  `context: [deploy]` (it executes at deploy, not build).

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green; `task build:charly`; `charly box
validate` on the main repo PASSES (the stepkind rejection is gone); the `check-pod` disposable bed PASSES
(no-regression of the validation path).

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): generic host-adapter seam + wired OpValidate (microkernel foundation F7)

Foundation cutover **F7** (closes gaps C7 + C8). Two cleanly-separable parts in one cutover:

**C7 ‚Äî generic host-adapter registration.** The host's out-of-band out-calls to a plugin (a verb word in
NO plan step) now share ONE connect seam. `connectPluginByWord` gains a `connectPluginByWordRef(class,
word, extraRef)` variant (an optional canonical candy ref ‚Üí `ResolveOpts.ExtraCandyRefs`, for a project
whose closure references the plugin candy nowhere ‚Äî a `box/<distro>` VM bed). `vm_plugin_client.go`'s
bespoke `ensureVmPluginConnected` (a `sync.Once` two-pass) and `k8s_plugin.go`'s bare `ResolveVerb("kube")`
are DELETED and routed through the seam (R3); `connectBakedPlugin`'s registry-resolve-first check makes it
idempotent, so the `sync.Once` was redundant. `credential_plugin.go` already used it (the reference).

**C8 ‚Äî wire OpValidate (was a dead constant).** A `class:kind` plugin can now serve a DEEP validation check
beyond the static CUE input-def gate: declare `ProvidedCapability.Validates = true` and the host dispatches
`Invoke(OpValidate)` at load, surfacing error-severity `spec.Diagnostics` as a load failure. New:
`spec.Diagnostics`/`spec.Diagnostic` wire types, the `validates` capability flag (proto field 8 + sdk + the
grpc/inproc provider carry + the `validatingKindCarrier` interface ‚Äî R3 parity), and the dispatch in
`runPluginKind`. `candy/plugin-example-kind` extended to serve OpValidate (rejects the sentinel
`marker: INVALID`).

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green incl.
`TestExternalKind_OpValidateRejectsInvalidBody` (a `marker: INVALID` body fails the load via the plugin's
OpValidate Diagnostics) + `TestExternalKind_PrescanConnectDecode` (a valid marker still loads ‚Äî no
regression with Validates on) + `TestCandyCUESchema_Corpus`; `task build:charly`; a live `charly vm list`
(C7 ‚Äî drives `invokeVmPluginEnv` through the new `connectPluginByWordRef` path against real libvirt) + the
`check-pod` disposable bed PASS on the fresh rebuild (no-regression). R5 grep self-test:
`ensureVmPluginConnected`/`vmPluginLoadOnce` return only CHANGELOG history; the 4 sibling comments that
referenced the deleted pattern were swept to `connectPluginByWordRef`.

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): substrate-lifecycle + preresolver over gRPC ‚Äî a deploy plugin brings its own host-side venue lifecycle (microkernel foundation F6)

Foundation cutover **F6** (closes gap C5). An external deploy-substrate plugin can now bring its OWN
host-side venue LIFECYCLE (PrepareVenue/Start/Stop/Status/Logs/Shell/Rebuild/PostApply/PostTeardown/
ArtifactKey/TeardownExecutor) AND a host-side PRERESOLVE step ‚Äî served host‚Üíplugin over the existing
`Provider.Invoke` with new Op selectors (no new gRPC service). The KEY decouple: a live `DeployExecutor`
cannot cross the wire, so `OpPrepareVenue`/`OpTeardownExecutor` return a self-contained
`spec.VenueDescriptor` the HOST re-materializes into a real `ShellExecutor`/`SSHExecutor` independently
(after the lifecycle Invoke returns), then serves THAT over the existing `ExecutorService` to the
deploy-walk plugin ‚Äî so the lifecycle plugin never holds the broker across the walk.

- `sdk/ops.go`: +the lifecycle Op selectors + `OpPreresolve`. `spec/deploy_wire.go`: +`VenueDescriptor`.
- `ProvidedCapability` gains `lifecycle` + `preresolve` (proto fields 6/7 + `sdk.ProvidedCapability` +
  the grpc-provider carry, populated in `buildUnit` for a `class:deploy` capability).
- `substrate_lifecycle_grpc.go`: `grpcSubstrateLifecycle` implements the in-core `substrateLifecycle`
  by Invoking the plugin + re-materializing the descriptor (`venueFromDescriptor`). `deploy_preresolve.go`:
  `wireDeployPreresolver` (Invokes `OpPreresolve`). Both registered idempotently at plugin-load
  (`registerPluginSubstrateLifecycle`/`registerPluginDeployPreresolver`, never shadowing a compiled-in
  pod/vm/k8s/android hook); both registries `sync.RWMutex`-guarded for the load-time mutation.
  `externalDeployTarget` is UNCHANGED ‚Äî it already calls only through the `substrateLifecycle` /
  `deployPreresolver` seams (R3).
- Reference plugin `candy/plugin-example-lifecycle` (out-of-process-only).

F6 SERVES the lifecycle channel; pod/vm stay compiled-in. M4 (later) MOVES the pod/vm lifecycle (+ the
`vmshared` render engine) into candies ‚Äî the dep-shed F6 enables.

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green incl.
`TestSubstrateLifecycle_PrepareVenueDescriptorRoundTrip` (builds the real `plugin-example-lifecycle` OOP,
`RegisterPluginProviders` wires the lifecycle + preresolver, `grpcSubstrateLifecycle.PrepareVenue`
re-materializes the shell descriptor into a `ShellExecutor` with venue `local`, the wire preresolver
returns the round-tripped marker) + `TestCandyCUESchema_Corpus`; `task build:charly`; the `check-pod`
disposable bed PASSES on the fresh rebuild (no-regression ‚Äî pod's compiled-in lifecycle still drives
through the now-mutex-guarded `substrateLifecycleFor`). The host-local descriptor round-trip is the fast
RDD spike; the live SSH-descriptor + auto-boot path is exercised by M4's `check-k3s-vm` when vm moves.

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): structural-kind tree-decode channel ‚Äî a plugin kind folds into uf.Bundle (microkernel foundation F5)

Foundation cutover **F5** (closes gap C2b). A class:kind plugin can now decode a STRUCTURAL entity ‚Äî its
`OpLoad` returns a `spec.Deploy` (BundleNode) member tree the host folds into `uf.Bundle`, the SAME map a
builtin pod/group/candy decoder populates in-proc (`buildBundleNodeInto`) ‚Äî so the entity participates in
deploy/check exactly like a builtin (the folded member goes through the SAME `validateDeploy`). This makes
`uf.Bundle` consumable FROM PLUGIN OUTPUT, the channel M3 reuses to externalize the seven builtin structural
kind decoders (pod/vm/k8s/local/android/group/candy). Builds on F4's flat decode (a FLAT kind still lands
its opaque body in `uf.PluginKinds`).

- `ProvidedCapability` gains `structural` (proto field 5 + `sdk.ProvidedCapability.Structural` + the
  `structuralKindCarrier` on the grpc/inproc provider, populated in `buildUnit`/`buildUnitInProc` for a
  ClassKind capability ‚Äî dual-placement parity, R3).
- `runPluginKind` (`provider_kind_invoke.go`): a structural kind json-unmarshals its `OpLoad` reply into a
  `BundleNode` and folds it into `uf.Bundle[name]`; a flat kind keeps the F4 `uf.PluginKinds` path.
- Reference plugin `candy/plugin-example-structkind` (out-of-process-only ‚Äî the witness that a plugin the
  loader was not built with can contribute a `uf.Bundle` member tree over the wire).

F5 ships the structural decode CHANNEL (the plugin RETURNS a member tree; the host folds it). Per-kind
authored-input threading is wired in M3 as each builtin kind is externalized.

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green incl.
`TestExternalStructKind_StructuralDecode` (stages the real `plugin-example-structkind` OOP, `LoadUnified`s a
`kind: examplestructkind` entity, asserts its plugin-built member folds into `uf.Bundle[‚Ä¶].Members[‚Ä¶]` with
`Target=pod` surviving the wire AND NOT also landing in `uf.PluginKinds`) + `TestCandyCUESchema_Corpus`;
`task build:charly`; the `check-pod` disposable bed PASSES on the fresh rebuild (no-regression ‚Äî builtin
kind decoding unaffected). The folded member passing the SAME `validateDeploy` as a builtin (the box-required
error during development) proved identical treatment.

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): parse-time external-KIND prescan + re-entrancy-safe pre-load connect (microkernel foundation F4)

Foundation cutover **F4** (closes gap C2a). A `kind: <plugin-word>` entity whose serving plugin is NOT
compiled in now parses + decodes during load ‚Äî the kind analogue of the deploy-substrate / command
prescans (R3). Unlike a deploy substrate (which defers to the bundle builder) or a command (lazy-connect
on invocation), a kind must DECODE its body during load (`runPluginKind`), so the serving plugin is
connected BEFORE decode ‚Äî and that connect re-loads the project (which contains the kind node), a genuine
circularity broken by a defer + a re-entrancy guard.

- `plugin_prescan.go`: `declaredKind` + `registerDeclaredKind` + `recognizedKind` (= connected OR
  pre-scanned) + `declaredKindWords`; `prescanPluginManifest` gains a `ClassKind` arm.
- `node_parse.go` `classifyDisc`: `ResolveKind` ‚Üí `recognizedKind` (a declared-but-unconnected kind word
  classifies as an entity).
- `connectDeclaredKindPlugins` (called at the depth-0 loader hook after the prescan): host-builds +
  connects the declared kind plugins before `mergeUnifiedDocs`. Re-entrancy-GUARDED (`inKindConnectPass`)
  ‚Äî the connect's nested `LoadConfig`/`ScanAllCandy` ‚Üí `LoadUnified` re-loads the SAME root, where the
  nested pass skips the connect AND `normalizeNodeInto` DEFERS (skips, no error) the not-yet-connected
  kind node; the OUTER pass then has the provider registered + decodes. A declared kind whose provider
  never connects is a LOUD `normalizeNodeInto` error (never a silent drop).
- Reference plugin `candy/plugin-example-kind` (out-of-process-only ‚Äî the witness that the loader can
  recognize + connect a kind it was not built with). No CUE change: `#NodeDoc` already admits a non-core
  discriminator opaquely (the 9 compiled-in plugin kinds prove it).

F4 is parse-time recognition + connect for a FLAT external kind body; the structural (nested-child)
kind tree-decode channel is F5.

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green incl.
`TestExternalKind_PrescanConnectDecode` (stages the real `plugin-example-kind` OOP, `LoadUnified`s a
`kind: examplekind` entity whose plugin is NOT compiled in, asserts it decodes into
`uf.PluginKinds["examplekind"]` with the body round-tripped ‚Äî the test COMPLETING is the
no-infinite-recursion proof) + `TestCandyCUESchema_Corpus`; `task build:charly`; the `check-pod`
disposable bed PASSES on the fresh rebuild (no-regression ‚Äî the loader still loads the builtin kinds).

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): external (plugin-contributed) install-step KIND ‚Äî opaque `external:<word>` + declared StepContract (microkernel foundation F3)

Foundation cutover **F3** (closes gap C1). A plugin can now CONTRIBUTE a first-class install-step
KIND, carried OPAQUELY through the InstallPlan IR as `external:<word>` with a plugin-DECLARED
Scope/Venue/Gate contract ‚Äî the generalization `ExternalPluginStep` is not (that wraps a `class:verb`
op in the ONE fixed `ExternalPlugin` kind with a Go-fixed contract). The reverse-channel EXECUTION
plumbing is REUSED wholesale (R3): the new `externalStep`'s host dispatch funnels through the SAME
`OpExecute`-to-the-serving-plugin path `ExternalPluginStep` uses (`executeExternalStep` ‚Üí
`invokeStepExecute`), and teardown ops are recorded dynamically from the reply (record-and-replay).

- `kit.StepContract` over Describe: `ProvidedCapability` gains `step_contract` (proto + SDK); a
  `class:step` plugin declares `{scope, venue, gate}`; `buildUnit` / `buildUnitInProc` carry it onto the
  grpc/inproc provider (`stepContractCarrier`, dual-placement parity).
- `externalStep` IR type (`Kind()=="external:"+word`, opaque `Payload`, stored declared contract,
  dynamic `reverseOps`); `InstallStepView` gains an opaque `Payload` and treats Scope/Venue/Gate as
  AUTHORITATIVE for an external kind (the advisory‚Üíauthoritative flip ‚Äî the host cannot recompute a
  contract it has no concrete Go step for).
- OPEN DEFAULT ARMS: `kit.WalkPlans` + `RunHostStep` route any `external:<word>` (by the
  `isExternalStepKind` prefix) with NO per-word case; `compileActOp` lowers a `run: plugin: <word>` whose
  word is a `class:step` provider to an `externalStep`. The closed `allStepKinds` / bijection deliberately
  ignore the `external:` prefix.
- Reference plugin `candy/plugin-example-stepkind` (the `class:step` companion of the verb-/deploy-class
  examples).

This is the carrier **M2** reuses to externalize the builtin step kinds (the compiler will emit
`external:system-packages` etc. with a built payload).

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green incl.
`TestExternalStepKind_EndToEnd` (builds the example `class:step` plugin OUT-OF-PROCESS, decodes its
StepContract from Describe, `compileActOp` lowers a `run: plugin: examplestepkind` op ‚Üí `externalStep`,
the opaque view round-trips, and `RunHostStep`'s open default arm dispatches `OpExecute` so the plugin
writes its marker on a real shell venue ‚Äî payload round-tripped, dynamic teardown op recorded) +
`TestCandyCUESchema_Corpus` (the example candy validates); `task build:charly`; the `check-pod` disposable
bed PASSES on the fresh rebuild (no-regression ‚Äî the builtin step kinds + IR walk unaffected).

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): CheckContextService reverse channel ‚Äî host-coupled kit check verbs are out-of-process-capable (microkernel foundation F2)

Foundation cutover **F2**. The host-coupled check-verb kit (`charly/plugin/kit`) was COMPILED-IN-ONLY
because `kit.CheckContext` exposed host-side legs the wire could not carry. F2 serves them over a new
**`CheckContextService`** gRPC reverse channel (`charly/plugin/proto/plugin.proto`), served on the SAME
go-plugin broker as `ExecutorService` (`grpcProvider.InvokeWithExecutor` gains a `*checkContextReverseServer`
arg; `invokeVerbProvider` wires it). Two class-generic RPCs (the Uniform API Invariant ‚Äî never per-verb):
`HTTPDo` (the host issues the request from its OWN network namespace with the per-request TLS/redirect/CA
policy ‚Äî an `*http.Client` cannot cross the wire, so the REQUEST crosses and the host dials) and
`AddBackground`. The scalar legs (`Mode`/`Box`/`Instance`/`Distros`/`DialTimeout`) ride the env_json
`CheckEnv` snapshot (new `DialTimeoutNs`).

- `kit.CheckContext`: `HTTPClient() *http.Client` ‚Üí `HTTPDo(ctx, HTTPRequest) (HTTPResponse, error)` (the
  only leg that could not cross). `httpClientFor` + the request execution relocated host-side into the
  shared `charly/check_http.go:doHTTPRequest` ‚Äî the ONE path both the in-proc `runnerCheckContext.HTTPDo`
  and the out-of-process `CheckContextService.HTTPDo` use (R3); deleted from `candy/plugin-http`.
- SDK: `sdk.ServeCheckVerb` wraps a `kit.CheckVerbProvider` as a pb.ProviderServer whose Invoke
  reconstructs an `sdkCheckContext` from the broker (ONE dial ‚Äî go-plugin pairs one Dial per
  AcceptAndServe id, so both services multiplex on the single conn) + the env snapshot, then runs RunVerb.
  A kit candy's `cmd/serve` is a one-line shim; `candy/plugin-port` + `candy/plugin-http` gain one
  (dual-placement, ZERO authoring change).

PLACEMENT: port/http (and the other kit verbs) stay COMPILED-IN by default ‚Äî they are UNIVERSAL verbs
(used by ~every candy's checks, composed by no image), so their serving candy is not in any bed's image
closure; flipping them OOP-by-default needs the universal-verb loader work that belongs to M1 ("14 kit
candies servable OOP"). F2 delivers the MECHANISM that makes them OOP-CAPABLE; M1 flips the non-universal
ones. (RDD discovery: a check-pod flip surfaced the universal-verb loading gap ‚Äî the bed corrected the
plan's assumption that the flip "just works".)

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build`/`go vet`/`go test ./...` green incl. the new
`TestKitVerbOutOfProcess_HTTPDoEndToEnd` (builds candy/plugin-http OUT-OF-PROCESS, dials `cc.HTTPDo` over
the reverse channel to a real httptest server ‚Äî status+body matched on success, mismatch failed; the RDD
highest-risk HTTP-over-RPC leg proven byte-correct) + `TestDoHTTPRequest` (host-vantage status/body/
insecure-TLS/timeout/redirect) + the existing deploy reverse-channel e2e; `task build:charly`; the
`check-pod` disposable bed PASSES on the fresh rebuild (no-regression: port/http dispatch in-proc through
the new HTTPDo interface). The in-proc port/http verb tests relocated to
`candy/plugin-{port,http}/plugin_test.go` (RunVerb vs a fake kit.CheckContext).

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly): generic verb-preresolver registry + opaque CheckEnv.Substrate (microkernel foundation F1)

Foundation cutover **F1** of the full-externalization program. The hardcoded per-verb
host-side endpoint preresolution ‚Äî the typed `CheckEnv.{Cdp,Vnc,Mcp,Spice}` fields plus the
fixed five-preresolver call block inside `invokeVerbProvider` ‚Äî is replaced by a GENERIC
registry: `registerVerbPreresolver(word, fn)` (`verb_preresolve.go`) + a single opaque
`CheckEnv.Substrate json.RawMessage`. This is the check-verb analogue of the proven
`registerDeployPreresolver` + `DeployVenue.Substrate` deploy seam. `invokeVerbProvider` now runs
ONE registry lookup with no per-verb branch (the Uniform API Invariant ‚Äî the per-plugin data
channel is opaque JSON, never a per-verb typed field); the four endpoint verbs (cdp/vnc/mcp/spice)
register thin wrappers (`verb_preresolve_wrappers.go`) that marshal their resolved `*Env` into
`CheckEnv.Substrate` ‚Äî each plugin decodes it into its own endpoint type, so NO candy go.mod
changed (the host‚Üîplugin boundary was already pure JSON) ‚Äî and `kube` registers one that rewrites
the op's resolved cluster context. A new host-resolved verb now adds a preresolver + a Substrate
decode in its plugin, with zero core dispatch edit.

**Blocking pre-existing fix surfaced by F1's R10 (R2):** `checkLocalTarget` (`check_venue.go`)
misrouted a `pod` deploy to the HOST venue because `isExternalDeploySubstrate("pod")` became true
when pod externalized (commit `7a38cc3a`) ‚Äî so `resolveCheckVenue` returned `Kind=host` and
`resolveCheckEndpoint` returned the RAW container port (`127.0.0.1:9222`), making cdp/vnc/spice dial
the container port on host loopback instead of the published host port. Masked while pod beds used
fixed `H:C == 9222:9222` ports; surfaced once they moved to auto-allocated host ports. Fix: a `pod`
is NEVER host-routed (it has a real CONTAINER venue) ‚Äî the `entry.Target != "pod"` guard. New
regression test `TestCheckLocalTarget_PodNotHostRoutedWhenExternal` registers pod as a runtime
external substrate and asserts it is not host-routed (proven to FAIL without the guard).

R10 (fully tested and validated): `go build` + `go vet` + `go test ./...` green; `task build:charly`;
the four matching disposable beds all PASS on the fresh-rebuild gate ‚Äî `check-k3s-vm` (kube, 6 steps),
`check-arch-vm` (spice, 13 steps), and `check-sway-browser-vnc-pod` (cdp/vnc/mcp/wl/dbus/record,
**154 passed / 0 failed** after the pod-venue fix); the goss / no-preresolver verbs unaffected. (The
`record: start` "already active" seen mid-RCA was stale tmux-session state accumulated across iterative
debug runs, cleared by `charly remove --purge` ‚Äî confirmed not a code bug by the clean run.)

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî fix(charly): REMOTE add_candy `copy:` step on a pod overlay ‚Äî stage the candy source

The add_candy-on-pod fix's flagged immediate-next follow-up. A REMOTE (@github) add_candy with a `copy:` (or
`cmd: --mount`) step on a pod overlay FAILED ‚Äî `buildOverlay` never staged the remote candy's source tree to
`.build/_candy/<name>.<version>/` (only the FULL build's `Generator.Generate` ‚Üí `createRemoteCandyCopies` did). The
just-landed write:-only marker passed because `emitWrite`'s bare COPY reads the staged inline file directly (no
scratch stage); a `copy:` step emits `COPY --from=<candy>` against the per-candy `FROM scratch AS <candy>` stage,
forcing buildah to build it ‚Üí missing `.build/_candy/...` source. Fix (R3): `buildOverlay` now calls
`Generator.createRemoteCandyCopies()` ‚Äî the SAME staging the full build uses (LOCAL candies a no-op). The
check-addcandy-pod bed + the pod-addcandy-marker candy gained a `copy:` step (copied.dat ‚Üí /etc/pod-addcandy-copied
+ a runtime check), so the bed now covers `write:` AND `copy:` on a remote add_candy.

R10 (fully tested and validated): `charly check run check-addcandy-pod` PASS (box/fedora, disposable) ‚Äî BOTH
`addcandy-marker-deployed` (write:) AND `addcandy-copied-deployed` (copy:) checks pass inside the running container.
`TestPodOverlayStagesRemoteCandySource` proven to FAIL without the fix. `go test ./...` green.

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî fix(charly): add_candy on a pod now builds + deterministically deploys the overlay (3 latent bugs)

A pod deploy declaring `add_candy:` was never exercised (boxes baked candies to avoid it); the new
`check-addcandy-pod` bed (box/fedora, deploy-key ‚âÝ image-name, a marker file asserted INSIDE the running
container) surfaced THREE latent bugs in the pod overlay build+deploy path, all fixed here:

- **Bug 1 (candy lookup):** OCITarget's bare-name `Generator.Candies[name]` lookup missed a REMOTE add_candy
  candy keyed under its qualified `candyMapKey` (a remote candy's `.Name` ‚âÝ its map key). New shared
  `Generator.candyByName` (exact-key, then `.Name` fallback) routes all 5 bare-name lookup sites
  (build_target_oci.go lookupCandy + 4 deploy_target_pod.go sites ‚Äî R3), also fixing the same latent mismatch
  for service/copy/security steps. PrepareVenue threads `ExtraCandyRefs` (collectOverlayCandies) so the add_candy
  candy is scanned into the overlay Generator.
- **Bug 2 (inline staging):** the overlay OCITarget left `ContextRelPrefix` empty, so a `write:` step's inline
  COPY resolved `_inline/<candy>/<hash>` against the project root instead of the overlay build dir (a UNIVERSAL
  bug ‚Äî local add_candy `write:` was broken too). New `overlayOCITarget(buildDir)` sets BuildDir AND ContextRelPrefix.
- **Bug 3 (deploy resolution ‚Äî the documented quirk):** the overlay BUILT but `charly config` resolved the BASE
  image (not the `<deploy-key>` overlay alias) via a CalVer-sort race. Fixed authoritatively: PrepareVenue persists
  the built overlay ref into a new `resolved_image:` host-state field (charly/schema/deploy.cue + `task cue:gen`),
  and `resolveDeployRef` consumes it by deploy-key at both config_image.go sites, bypassing the race
  (LocalImageExists fallback for plain pods / post-`bundle del`). Swept the two now-fixed CHANGELOG quirk claims (R1/R5).

R10 (fully tested and validated): `charly check run check-addcandy-pod` PASS (box/fedora, disposable) ‚Äî the
@github add_candy overlay builds, bakes `/etc/pod-addcandy-marker`, and the marker is PRESENT inside the running
container (overlay deterministically deployed); `update` + `feature-run-rebuild` pass (the Rebuild gate re-persists
the ref). Each bug has a hermetic regression test proven to FAIL without its fix
(TestOCITargetLookupCandyRemoteQualifiedKey, TestPodOverlayInlineCopyResolvesUnderContext,
TestResolveDeployRefPrefersPersistedOverlay). `go test ./...` green (incl. TestGenReproducible).

KNOWN follow-up (R2-separable ‚Üí immediate-next cutover): a REMOTE add_candy with a `copy:` step still needs
`.build/_candy` source staging in the overlay build (non-blocking ‚Äî the write:-only marker doesn't exercise it).

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî fix(charly): add `charly vm scp` ‚Äî the VM credential-sync leg was a dead invocation

check_synccreds_cmd.go invoked `charly vm scp` which never existed (after the command-class-out-of-process
cutover it resolved to `charly __vm scp` ‚Üí Kong unknown-command ‚Üí nonzero exit), so the VM leg of the
check-runner credential sync (an iterate.sandbox resolving to a kind:vm deploy) failed at runtime ‚Äî latent,
since all repo iterate: sandboxes are pods. `cp-box` is images-only (podman save|load), never arbitrary files.
Fix: added a real `charly vm scp <vm> <src> <dst>` subcommand (charly/vm_scp.go ‚Äî VmScpCmd + scpToVm), the
arbitrary-file analogue of cp-box ‚Äî resolves the guest endpoint via the managed charly-<name> ssh alias
(sshParamsForVm, as cp-box/vm-ssh do), tilde-resolves dst against the guest $HOME, and delivers the file
USER-owned via SSHExecutor.PutFile (the bed-proven scp-into-guest primitive). check_synccreds' VM leg now
calls scpToVm IN-PROCESS (R3, mirroring the pod leg's direct podman cp), honoring the source mode + dst tilde.

R10 (fully tested and validated): live on a disposable arch VM ‚Äî `charly vm scp arch <file> '~/scp-probe.json'`
‚Üí the file landed at /home/arch/scp-probe.json (tilde-resolved), owner `arch` (USER-owned, not root), correct
content; VM torn down. go test ./... green (5 new tests: tilde-resolution, absolute-dst, mode-override,
directory-source rejection, Kong arg-parsing).

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî fix(charly): reap orphaned plugin processes ‚Äî client Kill-on-exit + server parent-watch

A plugin-process leak accumulated ~6,000 orphaned `<plugin> __plugin serve` go-plugin servers across DAYS
(etimes 77h, 78k system threads ‚Üí `fatal: newosproc / failed to create OS thread (errno=11)` that nearly
broke a check-bed R10). RCA (vs vendored go-plugin v1.8.0): the server has NO parent-death detection (Serve
blocks on doneCh, closed ONLY by the client's Kill‚ÜíShutdown RPC), AND the host never called client.Kill() on
exit (providerRegistry.Close() was test-only). Two-pronged fix:

- **Client reaping (every exit path):** reapPlugins() (= providerRegistry.Close()) wired three ways since
  os.Exit skips defers ‚Äî a RegisterShutdownHook on the EXISTING InstallSignalHandler (R3, no second
  signal.Notify) + a defer + an explicit call after dispatch (covers the os.Exit error paths). New
  vmshared.RegisterShutdownHook/runShutdownHooks + the package-main alias.
- **Server self-terminate (crash/SIGKILL backstop):** charly/plugin/sdk/parentwatch.go ‚Äî watchParentDeath()
  records os.Getppid() at startup, polls every 2s, os.Exit(0) when the parent dies (reparented). Called at
  the top of Serve() so EVERY plugin (external + in-charly `__plugin serve`) gets it. go-plugin v1.8.0 has
  no parent-watch to re-enable, so this ADDS one.
- **C6 await-unlock preserved:** the watch fires ONLY on actual parent DEATH (getppid is stable while the
  parent lives), so a live host awaiting an unbounded credential unlock is never disturbed ‚Äî proven by
  TestCredentialAwaitUnlock_ExternalEndToEnd.
- **R1/R5:** swept the false "server auto-exits when the host disconnects (no orphan)" claim across sdk.go /
  plugin_transport.go / plugin_cmd.go / provider_registry.go.

R10 (fully tested and validated): clean baseline ‚Üí `charly check run check-exampledeploy` PASS ‚Üí ZERO orphans
after (prong 1 ‚Äî charly reaped on exit, vs the prior leak); SIGKILL a live plugin's parent ‚Üí the orphan
self-exited after 2s (prong 2 ‚Äî the parent-watch). `go test ./...` green (new: TestParentWatch_FiresOnParentDeath
/ _QuietWhileParentLives, TestShutdownHooks_RunRegistered, TestReapPlugins_ClosesRegisteredPluginClients).

### 2026-06-30 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize the four detection-builders (cargo/npm/pixi/aur) ‚Üí candy/plugin-builder-{cargo,npm,pixi,aur} via a builder-IR-over-RPC seam

The four detection-builders' DEPLOY-TIME IR shim leaves charly's core ‚Äî they are now external
out-of-process plugin candies. RDD against the live tree corrected the premise: the four
`plugin_builder_*.go` files never held the build-time multi-stage (that is the embedded
`builder:` vocabulary, `emitBuilderStages`) nor the host-side execution (`builder_venue.go`); they
held ONLY the in-proc `BuilderProvider` IR shim ‚Äî `CollectContext` + `Reverse` (+ a DEAD
`StagingMount`). The proven `external_builder:`+`OpResolve` mechanism covers a DIFFERENT concern
(explicit build-time multi-stage), so this builds a NEW builder-IR-over-RPC seam for the deploy-time
legs while keeping the build engine core (the operator's vm/pod principle).

- **Two new builder-class ops** (`charly/plugin/sdk/ops.go`, aliased in `provider.go`):
  `OpCollectContext` (per-candy stage-context keys) + `OpReverse` (that step's teardown ops). Wire
  types in `charly/spec/deploy_wire.go`: `BuilderCollectInput`/`BuilderCollectReply` +
  `BuilderReverseInput`/`BuilderReverseReply`.
- **Compiler-purity build PRE-PASS** (`charly/builder_preresolve.go`, mirroring
  `deploy_preresolve.go`): `preresolveBuilderContexts` RPCs each externalized builder's
  `OpCollectContext`+`OpReverse` HOST-SIDE, BEFORE the pure `BuildDeployPlan` compile, and stashes
  the result on `HostContext.BuilderContext`. The pure compiler READS pre-populated data and NEVER
  dials a plugin ‚Äî locked by `TestBuildDeployPlan_BuilderPurity_NoPluginRPC` (connects no plugin,
  must still compile). Wired at the 3 `bundle_add_cmd.go` compile sites via `preresolveBuildersInto`.
- **`BuilderStep.Reverse()` is now a PURE getter** of the new `PreResolvedReverse` field (set by
  `compileBuilderSteps`), carried across the wire on `InstallStepView.ReverseOps` and restored by
  `stepFromView` ‚Äî so RunHostStep's host-side `st.Reverse()` echoes the stashed ops with no RPC.
- **Shared logic in `charly/plugin/kit/builder.go` (R3)**: `BuilderCollectContext` + `BuilderReverse`,
  the single source for all four builders' deploy-time IR (the per-builder reverse-op KIND moved
  out-of-process), dispatched by word. Covered by `plugin/kit/builder_test.go`.
- **Detection stays core + PRECISELY scoped, on-demand** (`candyNeedsBuilder` unchanged ‚Äî no
  `external_builder:` forced onto the ~39 consumer candies). New `provider_builder_external.go`
  (`externalizedBuilders` / `externalBuilderPlugins` / `externalBuilderPluginRef`, mirroring the
  deploy-substrate sets). The build PRE-PASS detects EXACTLY the builders the deploy's resolved
  closure triggers via `detectExternalizedBuilders` ‚Äî applying the SAME distro/build-format gate
  `candyNeedsBuilder` applies, so a fedora deploy NEVER connects aur and a pixi-only deploy connects
  ONLY pixi ‚Äî and `ensureBuildersConnected` build-connects only those, by their canonical ref, the
  same on-demand scoped pattern as `ensureVmPluginConnected`. `collectReferencedPluginWords` does NOT
  surface builder words (that over-built unrelated builder plugins across a whole-box scan ‚Äî aur on a
  fedora pod deploy ‚Äî and amplified host thread pressure); a pure pod deploy (no `add_candy`) connects
  nothing (its multi-stage is baked at build via the vocabulary). Gated by
  `TestDetectExternalizedBuilders_ScopedAndDistroGated`.
- **R5 deletes** `plugin_builder_{cargo,npm,pixi,aur}.go`, `provider_builder.go` (the in-proc
  `BuilderProvider`/`BuilderStager` interfaces + `builderProviderFor`/`builderStagerFor`), the dead
  `StagingMount`/`builtinBuilderBase`/`pixiDefaultEnvName`, and `builder_builtins.go`. The build
  engine (`emitBuilderStages`/`buildStageContext`/the runtime-env‚Üílabel contract), the host-side
  executor (`builder_venue.go`/`runVenueBuilderStep`/`renderBuilderScript`), and the `BuilderStep` IR
  STAY core. `TestDedicatedProviders_*` updated; new `TestExternalizedBuilders_NoInProcProvider`
  asserts no compiled-in builder remains.

### 2026-06-29 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize the `pod` deploy substrate ‚Üí candy/plugin-deploy-pod (the last substrate; pod = vm's shape)

The DEFAULT, highest-traffic deploy substrate leaves charly's core ‚Äî ALL FIVE substrates
(local/vm/pod/k8s/android) are now external plugins. The earlier "pod is irreducible" reading was
WRONG: vm already keeps its build engine (libvirt/qemu disk build) core and runs it host-side in
PrepareVenue, externalizing fine ‚Äî a container image is identical, so pod externalizes the SAME way
(operator: "if building a VM works via an external plugin, a container should too"). The build engine
(PodDeployTarget/OCITarget/Generator) STAYS core, called in-process host-side; nothing crosses gRPC.

- **podSubstrateLifecycle** (charly/pod_deploy_lifecycle.go) implements the Design A substrateLifecycle
  hook: PrepareVenue lifts the old PodUnifiedTarget.Add body verbatim (NewGenerator + resolve ResolvedBox
  + OCITarget overlay build + prepareCandySecrets + PodDeployTarget.Emit), builds the overlay HOST-SIDE
  (exactly as vmSubstrateLifecycle.PrepareVenue builds the VM disk), then returns a host-local
  ShellExecutor so the generic plugin walk is a clean no-op. Start/Stop/Status/Logs/Shell shell to the
  CLI; Rebuild = box build + check box + bundle add + stop + config + start (the `charly update` gate);
  PostTeardown = charly remove + drop the <name>-overlay images (keep-image-gated).
- **candy/plugin-deploy-pod** serves deploy:pod (thin ‚Äî its Invoke returns an empty DeployReply; the
  overlay was baked host-side, walking add_candy steps on the host venue would be wrong). `pod` joined
  externalizedDeploySubstrates + externalDeploySubstratePlugins.
- **substrateLifecycle interface change:** PrepareVenue gained `plans []*InstallPlan` (pod consumes them
  to build the overlay; vm ignores them ‚Äî it walks them in-guest), PostTeardown gained `keepImage bool`
  (pod honors --keep-image; vm ignores).
- **The one fork the vm precedent didn't cover (fixed):** the bed runner classified EVERY external
  substrate as isInPlace (skip config/start) ‚Äî correct for local/android/k8s (no container lifecycle),
  fatal for pod (it builds+runs a container). New R3 helper `bedExternalInPlace(target) =
  isExternalDeploySubstrate(target) && target != "pod"` at the 3 classification sites drives pod through
  the DEFAULT build‚Üíconfig‚Üístart‚Üícheck-live‚Üíremove path (only bundle add's overlay build routes through
  pod's external machinery).
- **R5 deletes:** plugin_deploy_pod.go (podTarget), unified_targets_pod.go (PodUnifiedTarget) +
  dispatch/test. PodDeployTarget RETAINED as pod's core overlay-build engine (the vm-keeps-libvirt
  principle). `git grep` of the removed identifiers ‚Üí CHANGELOG only across superproject + plugins.

R10 (fully tested and validated): `charly check run check-pod` PASS run 2026.180.2113 (box/fedora,
disposable) ‚Äî the externalized deploy:pod built the fedora overlay host-side, deployed, passed
check-live + feature-run, AND `update` + `feature-run-rebuild` passed (the Design A Rebuild = the
`charly update` gate). The substrateLifecycle interface + external-deploy signatures changed, so the
cross-cutting beds re-verified GREEN: check-arch-vm (vm ‚Äî the changed interface), check-exampledeploy +
check-local (the external-deploy/bed-runner paths). `go test ./...` green (new pod_deploy_lifecycle_test.go
mirroring the vm tests + the Rebuild stale-verb guard).

### 2026-06-29 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize the `vm` deploy substrate ‚Üí candy/plugin-deploy-vm (Design A: the substrate-LIFECYCLE hook framework)

The last entangled deploy substrate leaves charly's core. vm has a real substrate LIFECYCLE
(Start/Stop/Status/Logs/Shell/Rebuild) that local/android/k8s lack, so the bare externalDeployTarget can't
serve it (its Rebuild only re-runs bundle-add, but `charly update <vm-bed>` ‚Äî the R10 gate ‚Äî must
destroy+create+start the domain). Design A generalizes the framework: a per-substrate **`substrateLifecycle`**
hook (charly/deploy_substrate_lifecycle.go) ‚Äî the walk is the plugin, the lifecycle is a registered host-side
hook. This generalizes for pod next.

- **candy/plugin-deploy-vm** serves `deploy:vm`, running the shared `charly/plugin/kit.WalkPlans` over the
  guest SSHExecutor (a near-clone of plugin-deploy-local). `vm` joined `externalizedDeploySubstrates`.
- **`vmSubstrateLifecycle`** (charly/vm_deploy_lifecycle.go) implements the hook: `PrepareVenue` (resolve the
  kind:vm entity, ssh-config stanza, auto-boot, WaitForSSH/CloudInit/PackageLock, EnsureCharlyInGuest, build
  the guest executor, persist VmDeployState), `PostApply` (nested pod-in-guest), `TeardownExecutor`/`PostTeardown`,
  and `Start/Stop/Status/Logs/Shell/Rebuild` shelling to the `charly vm` family (Rebuild = destroy+build+create+
  start+bundle-add ‚Äî the `charly update` Rebuild gate). externalDeployTarget consults the hook.
- **RebootStep** now routes through RunHostStep (the host reboots the guest + waits for boot_id on a rebootable
  venue; skip-and-note on a host venue) ‚Äî kit no longer silently drops it (it would have dropped kernel-driver
  guest reboots).
- **The guest ledger is preserved (R2/R5 fidelity):** `recordVenueLedger` writes the deploy + per-candy layer
  records THROUGH the executor into the guest (`~/.config/opencharly/{deploys,layers}`), restoring the in-proc
  VmDeployTarget's self-contained `*Via(t.Exec)` design (the host-side computeDeployID record stays for `bundle del`).
  **Root-cause fix that unblocked it:** `SSHExecutor.PutFile` ALWAYS ran under sudo (ignoring `ownerRoot`), so
  user-scoped env.d writes created `~/.config/opencharly` root-owned and the user-scoped ledger write failed
  Permission-denied; PutFile now honors `ownerRoot` (RunUser for user files ‚Äî R3 parity with ShellExecutor.PutFile,
  unit-locked via `sshInstallScript`).
- **Latent local-externalization regressions (211c2dab) surfaced + fixed here (R2):** dotted/nested deploy
  plugin discovery (`deployNodePluginContext`‚Üí`resolveDeployNodeByPath` recurses nested children + auto-injects
  the substrate-plugin candy ref), the nested executor honoring `opts.ParentExec` (a nested target:local-in-vm
  child runs in the guest), and `--verify` deferral for a lifecycle substrate.
- **R5 deletes:** deploy_target_vm.go, unified_targets_vm.go, plugin_deploy_vm.go, the EmitVM half of
  StepProvider (+ all 13 arms), EnsureManagedBlock(Via), buildVmReverseRunner, findVmDeployRecord. `git grep` of
  the removed identifiers ‚Üí CHANGELOG only across the superproject + the plugins + box/arch skill/bed sweeps.

Arch VM, FRESH VM) ‚Äî the externalized `deploy:vm` deployed the arch-host layers + a nested target:local child

fresh-rebuild gate). `go test ./...` green (new unit tests: sshInstallScript privilege, recordVenueLedger
guest-write, resolveDeployNodeByPath, the substrate-lifecycle dispatch, RebootStep-via-RunHostStep).

### 2026-06-29 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize the `local` deploy substrate ‚Üí candy/plugin-deploy-local; generalize the build channel to RunHostStep (5 host-engine step kinds)

The highest-impact deploy substrate (the default `target: local`) leaves charly's core, via the F1
substrate-kind seam + F2/F3 ‚Äî completing the reverse-channel contract for EVERY step kind. Per the operator
directive "make EVERYTHING a plugin": a charly composed with plugin-deploy-local deploys `target: local`;
the in-proc LocalDeployTarget is gone.

- **RunBuildStep ‚Üí RunHostStep (generalized; R5 rename + proto regen):** the host-served reverse RPC now
  drives ALL host-engine-dependent step kinds an external deploy plugin can't execute itself ‚Äî BuilderStep +
  LocalPkgInstallStep (from F3) + SystemPackagesStep (host renders via DistroConfig from the reverse server's
  buildEngineContext) + act-verb OpStep (host registry resolveProvisionScript) + ExternalPluginStep (host
  registry + broker dispatch of a NESTED plugin). The plugin owns the walk ordering; the host owns the
  engine/registry. The ExternalPluginStep reentrancy (a second reverse server on the nested plugin's own
  broker, inside the deploy plugin's RunHostStep) is live-proven by check-local.
- **kit.WalkPlans (charly/plugin/kit):** the shared out-of-process walk ‚Äî plugin-renderable kinds
  (Op/File/ShellHook+managed-block/ShellSnippet/Service*/RepoChange) via the F2 Executor legs; the 5
  host-engine kinds via RunHostStep. Pure render helpers moved to kit; package main re-exports via
  kit_aliases.go so VmDeployTarget shares the ONE render copy (R3). Consumed by plugin-deploy-local +
  plugin-example-deploy.
- **Reverse-op fidelity:** InstallStepView gains `ReverseOps`; `stepToView` computes `step.Reverse()`
  host-side, and `externalDeployTarget.apply` captures the two deploy-time-stateful kinds on the live venue
  before `wireView` (probe `systemctl is-enabled` ‚Üí ServicePackaged.PriorEnabled; resolve env.d path ‚Üí
  ShellHook.EnvFile). `Reverse()` logic stays ONCE in package main (R3); the plugin echoes the ops.
- **R5 deletes:** LocalDeployTarget, LocalUnifiedTarget, unified_targets_local.go, plugin_deploy_local.go,
  LocalDeployTarget.execBuilder, the 13 EmitLocal step-provider methods + the interface method; surviving
  shared helpers relocated to deploy_host_helpers.go. New candy/plugin-deploy-local serves deploy:local;
  ResolveTarget picks the executor via rootExecutorForDeployNode (Shell for host:local, SSH for
  host:user@machine). `git grep` of the removed identifiers ‚Üí CHANGELOG only (incl. the plugins skill sweep).

R10 (fully tested and validated): BOTH beds GREEN on a fresh rebuild ‚Äî `charly check run check-local` PASS
run 2026.180.1353 (Op-write + act-verb OpStep [RunHostStep] + the ExternalPluginStep reentrancy on the live
host) AND `charly check run check-exampledeploy` PASS run 2026.180.1352 (Builder/LocalPkg/ShellHook/File/
PutFile). `go test ./...` green incl. TestRunHostStep_Dispatch (all 5 arms), TestWalkPlans_PerKindDispatch,
TestStepToView_CapturesReverseOps.

Follow-ups (each its own immediate-next cutover): (1) a deploy-class baked-plugin lazy-connect so a packaged
charly resolves `target: local` offline/instantly ‚Äî today it resolves on-demand via loadDeployPlugins (the
proven android/k8s model); the per-plugin bake is INERT for the deploy class (discoverBakedPluginWords
handles only verb/command). (2) live SystemPackages/ServicePackaged RunHostStep coverage on a DISPOSABLE
local bed (a container/VM local target) ‚Äî those arms are unit + dispatch tested here but not live-exercised,
since a live `target: local` test mutates the operator host.

### 2026-06-29 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: F3 ‚Äî the build channel (host-served RunBuildStep reverse RPC; an external deploy plugin drives the core build engine)

The exact analog of F2: F2 made the host SERVE the executor so an external deploy plugin drives venue ops;
F3 makes the host SERVE the build engine so the plugin drives BUILD ops (builder + localpkg steps) ‚Äî the
two step kinds F2's RunSystem/PutFile legs cannot execute because they run the HOST build engine
(`BuilderRun`/`buildLocalPkgOnHost`/`EnsureImagePresent` ‚Üí `charly box build`). The build engine STAYS the
irreducible core; F3 only EXPOSES the existing machinery via an RPC the plugin drives, so the plugin owns the
full deploy walk. Unblocks externalizing the local/vm builder legs AND the builders themselves (C4).

- **ONE RPC** on the existing E3b ExecutorService reverse channel (the same broker F2 stands up):
  `RunBuildStep(BuildStepRequest{step_json: spec.InstallStepView, opts_json: EmitOpts}) ‚Üí BuildStepReply{reverse_ops_json, error}`
  (charly/plugin/proto/plugin.proto + regen; SDK `Executor.RunBuildStep` client). The plugin, walking the
  plan, dials it for `BuilderStep`/`LocalPkgInstallStep`; the host owns the engine, the plugin owns the walk.
- **Thin host handler** (plugin_executor_reverse.go: `RunBuildStep` ‚Üí `stepFromView` ‚Üí switch): `*LocalPkgInstallStep`
  ‚Üí the existing `execLocalPkgInstall` (makepkg + `transferAndInstallPkgs`); `*BuilderStep` ‚Üí the new
  `runVenueBuilderStep` (charly/builder_venue.go) ‚Äî **EXTRACTED (R3) from VmDeployTarget.execBuilder/
  execHomeArtifactBuilder; the VM target now delegates to it in 2 lines** ‚Äî driving the existing
  `BuilderRun`/`EnsureImagePresent`/`buildDepPkgsOnHost`/`transferAndInstallPkgs`; any other kind ‚Üí loud error.
  Zero build-engine reimplementation. The host build-engine context is threaded via `InvokeWithExecutor(‚Ä¶, build)`.
- The plugin folds the step's recorded `Reverse()` ops into its DeployReply (record-and-replay teardown).
- **R2 fix in-tree:** `validate.go` now accepts a `localpkg:`-only candy as install content (a real gap the F3
  witness candy surfaced).

R10 (fully tested and validated): `charly check run check-exampledeploy` PASS run 2026.180.1152 ‚Äî the external
plugin drove `RunBuildStep` and the host built + installed a real localpkg (`charly-f3-witness` via makepkg +
`pacman -U`) on a fresh-rebuild re-verify, then the reverse op removed it (`pacman -R`), zero residue;
`go test ./...` green incl. `TestRunBuildStep_Dispatch` (Builder‚Üíbuilder fn, LocalPkgInstall‚ÜíexecLocalPkgInstall,
non-build‚Üíreject, malformed‚Üíerror). (The BuilderStep arm rides the identical RPC + is dispatch-unit-tested + its
fn is exercised by the VM beds; its full F3 E2E lands with the local/vm cutovers, which deploy a home-artifact
builder on a disposable bed rather than polluting the operator host's real ~/.cargo/~/.npm-global/~/.pixi.)

### 2026-06-29 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: F2 ‚Äî the executable deploy channel (serializable per-step InstallPlan IR on the wire + PutFile reverse RPC)

The foundation that lets an EXTERNAL out-of-process deploy plugin walk + EXECUTE an InstallPlan's steps on a
venue and PUSH files ‚Äî the prerequisite for externalizing the local/vm deploy substrates (which the prior
android/k8s substrates did NOT need, as they don't execute InstallPlan steps). Closes the two gaps the E3b
seam left.

- **Serializable per-step IR:** `InstallPlan.Steps []InstallStep` now round-trips on the wire via ONE
  tagged-union `spec.InstallStepView` (charly/spec/deploy_wire.go ‚Äî a `Kind` discriminator + the superset of
  all 13 concrete step kinds' fields; the rich payloads Op/LocalPkg/Builder/ApkPackageSpec already live in
  `spec`). ONE converter `charly/step_view.go` (`stepToView`/`stepFromView`) bridges it; the in-proc
  DeployTargets keep walking `[]InstallStep` UNCHANGED and the wire path reconstructs the SAME concrete Go
  step type, so execute semantics ride along byte-identical (R3 ‚Äî `Scope`/`Venue`/`RequiresGate` are computed
  methods, NOT stored identity; carried as advisory fields only so an executing plugin picks sudo-vs-user
  without re-deriving). `InstallPlan.wireView()` now fills `Steps`; the stale "future cutover / provenance-only
  / Steps dropped" claims swept (R5).
- **PutFile reverse RPC:** `ExecutorService.PutFile` (charly/plugin/proto/plugin.proto + regen) ‚Äî the
  host-served handler (plugin_executor_reverse.go) delegates to the live `DeployExecutor.PutFile` (honoring
  `owner_root`); SDK `Executor.PutFile` (binary-safe proto `bytes`).
- **Latent bug fixed in passing (R1/R2, not deferred):** `spec.Matcher` had `UnmarshalJSON` but no
  `MarshalJSON`, so a zero matcher round-tripped to `{Op:"op"}`; added a symmetric `MarshalJSON` (zero‚Üínull)
  + a null short-circuit in `UnmarshalJSON`. Real matchers + baked labels byte-unchanged.
- `candy/plugin-example-deploy` now decodes the plans-with-steps, WALKS + EXECUTES the steps on the venue over
  the reverse channel (honoring each step's advisory scope) + PUSHES a file via the new PutFile ‚Äî the F2 proof.

R10 (fully tested and validated): `charly check run check-exampledeploy` PASS run 2026.180.1047 ‚Äî the external
plugin executed a real file-write step + a shell-hook step AND pushed a file, on a fresh-rebuild re-verify
(on-venue evidence: the written file, the env.d hook drop-in, the pushed file; record-and-replay teardown
left zero side-effect); `go test ./...` green incl. `TestStepView_RoundTrip` (all 13 step kinds + a coverage
gate asserting every kind has a fixture) + `TestExecutorReverseServer_PutFile`.

### 2026-06-29 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize the `k8s` deploy substrate ‚Üí candy/plugin-kube `deploy:k8s` (F1, beside `verb:kube`)

The SECOND deploy SUBSTRATE to leave charly's core (after `android`), via the now-proven F1 substrate-kind-plugin
dispatch seam. Per the operator directive "make EVERYTHING a plugin ‚Äî a user composes the binary with the plugins
it needs": a charly composed without the kube plugin does not deploy `target: k8s`; one that references plugin-kube
does. candy/plugin-kube now owns ALL Kubernetes cluster interaction (R3 ‚Äî the `kube:` probe verb, the k3s
kubeconfig-merge seam, AND the deploy `kubectl apply -k`).

- **F1 dispatch:** `"k8s": true` added to `externalizedDeploySubstrates` (`charly/provider_deploy.go`) ‚Äî the whole
  dispatch change. `checkDeployProviderBijection` now accepts k8s as in-proc-XOR-externalized; `isExternalDeploySubstrate`
  treats the CUE-kind word `k8s` as external; the prescan registers `deploy:k8s` from plugin-kube's `plugin:` block, so
  `ResolveTarget` routes `target: k8s` ‚Üí `externalDeployTarget` once plugin-kube connects (loaded-on-reference via the
  substrate kind in `deployNodePluginContext`).
- **The generator STAYS in core ‚Äî the plugin does the cluster I/O.** Unlike `deploy:android` (where the plugin DRIVES
  the device), `GenerateK8sKustomize` (`charly/k8s_generate.go`) cannot leave core: it consumes the package-main
  `Capabilities`/`BoxMetadata` type + the CUE egress gate (`#K8sObject`/`#Kustomization`) the out-of-process plugin
  cannot reach, AND it has a SECOND in-core consumer (`charly bundle from-box --target k8s`). So the host-side
  `deploy:k8s` preresolver (`charly/k8s_deploy_preresolve.go`, registered via the GENERAL `deploy_preresolve.go` hook ‚Äî
  R3 with android) resolves the image Capabilities (label-resolving the ref like the pod path ‚Äî `leafName` +
  `resolveLocalImageRef`, which the never-run in-proc target lacked) + the `kind: k8s` cluster template, RUNS the
  egress-validated `GenerateK8sKustomize`, and ships the overlay path + tree root + kubeconfig context in
  `DeployVenue.Substrate` (the new `spec.K8sDeployVenue`). candy/plugin-kube's new `deploy.go` runs
  `kubectl --context <ctx> apply -k` (the LIVE cluster I/O it owns) and returns the `kubectl delete -k` + tree-removal
  teardown op the host records to the ledger (record-and-replay). `--context` from the cluster template targets the
  cluster explicitly ‚Äî the old `K8sApply`-gated in-proc apply was never wired, so there was no behavior to preserve.
- **R5 deletes:** `charly/k8s_target.go` (`K8sDeployTarget`), `charly/unified_targets_k8s.go` (`K8sUnifiedTarget`
  Add/Del/Test/Update), `charly/plugin_deploy_k8s.go` (the `k8sTarget` builtin), `EmitOpts.K8sApply`, and
  `ErrNotSupportedOnK8s` (+ the install-plan / go / kubernetes / vm-deploy-target / build / generate / generate-source
  skill sweep). `git grep` of the removed identifiers returns only CHANGELOG. No pkg/arch change ‚Äî plugin-kube is
  loaded-on-reference, so `target: k8s` resolves project-lessly like the `kube:` verb.
- **New R10 bed `check-k8s-deploy`** (group bed; the proven sibling-member shape) + the `check-k8s-deploy-app` fixture
  box (minimal Fedora base + local pure-rpm candies, so it builds from the root project where namespace boxes do not):
  a k3s VM member (reusing `k3s-vm` + `k3s-server`) brings up a cluster + merges kubeconfig to `vm-k3s-vm`, then a
  `target: k8s` workload member deploys via the externalized substrate; the `kube:` checks assert the Deployment object
  landed (the pod is not asserted Ready ‚Äî the local box image is absent from the disposable cluster's containerd;
  image-into-cluster delivery is orthogonal to the substrate).

### 2026-06-29 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize the `android` deploy substrate ‚Üí candy/plugin-adb `deploy:android` (the F1 substrate-kind-plugin dispatch keystone)

The FIRST deploy SUBSTRATE to leave charly's core, via the new F1 substrate-kind-plugin dispatch seam ‚Äî the
keystone that lets a CUE-kind substrate word (`pod`/`local`/`k8s`/`android`/`vm`) be served by an
out-of-process plugin. Per the operator directive "make EVERYTHING a plugin ‚Äî a user builds a binary with
the plugins it needs": a charly composed without the android deploy plugin simply does not deploy android
(by design); one that bakes/references plugin-adb does.

- **F1 dispatch (GENERAL for all 5 substrates):** ONE source of truth `externalizedDeploySubstrates`
  (`charly/provider_deploy.go`, currently `{"android": true}`). `checkDeployProviderBijection` relaxed from
  "every substrate word has an in-proc DeployTargetProvider" to **in-proc XOR externalized**;

  set; the prescan already registers `deploy:<word>` from a candy `plugin:` block, so `ResolveTarget`

### 2026-06-29 ‚Äî fix(charly)!: NestedExecutor.GetFile stages the pulled file on the PARENT, not inside the leaf ‚Äî the reverse-channel container‚Üíhost pull

Surfaced by the android-emulator bed's `selkies-core-frame-not-uniform` check ‚Äî the first consumer to
exercise the container‚Üíhost reverse-channel `GetFile` green. `NestedExecutor.GetFile` baked the staging
`> tmp` redirect INSIDE `wrapWithJump`, so the staged copy was written in the LEAF container while
`Parent.GetFile` read the parent's separate filesystem ‚Üí `open ‚Ä¶: no such file or directory` on EVERY
container‚Üíhost (and VM‚Üíhost) file pull (wl screenshots, record `.cast`, any nested artifact). The captured
frame was real (a 1024√ó768 PNG) ‚Äî only the pull was broken; it had simply never been exercised green before.

The fix runs ONLY `cat <remote>` through the jump (the leaf's byte-clean stdout exits verbatim) and applies
the `>` redirect on the PARENT shell ‚Äî the `{ ‚Ä¶ }` group's stdout, closed with `}` after the heredoc
terminator's own line ‚Äî so the stage lands parent-side where `Parent.GetFile` reads it. Binary-safe (the
parent `>` is byte-level, unlike RunCapture's protobuf-string channel); recurses for multi-hop (each level
stages on its own parent). New unit test `TestNestedExecutorGetFile_StagesRedirectOnParent` asserts the
parent-side composition + a verbatim binary round-trip (fails against the pre-fix code).

R10 (fully tested and validated): `charly check run check-android-emulator-pod` PASS run 2026.180.0818 ‚Äî
the wl-screenshot binary PNG now pulls and `selkies-core-frame-not-uniform` passes; `go test ./...` green.
The android-emulator bed is the only bed that exercises the nested-`GetFile` path (per the RCA), so it plus
the binary-round-trip unit test are complete coverage.

### 2026-06-28 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize `charly vm` ‚Üí candy/plugin-vm (command:vm) ‚Äî the fourth WELDED-command externalization

Moves the `charly vm` COMMAND surface (the VM lifecycle CLI: build / create / start / stop / destroy /
console / ssh / snapshot / gpu / import / clone / cp-box / list) OUT of charly's core into the
already-out-of-tree `candy/plugin-vm`, which becomes DUAL-MODE ‚Äî `verb:libvirt` (gRPC-served, unchanged)
PLUS the new `command:vm`. The 4th WELDED-command externalization (after tmux, preempt, feature). The
`charly vm ‚Ä¶` CLI is UNCHANGED; only the registration LOCATION moved (a deleted builtin CommandProvider ‚Üí
an external command plugin dispatched via the C1.1 stdio passthrough seam).

`charly vm`'s VmCmd Run handlers are WELDED to the deepest core ‚Äî the project loader, the libvirt/qemu
backends, cloud-init, the VM deploy target, and the VmOp-resolution RPCs the plugin's own verb:libvirt
serves ‚Äî so the whole `VmCmd` tree (charly/vm.go + vm_snapshot_cmd.go) MUST STAY CORE (R3). The SOLUTION
re-homes the WHOLE in-core VmCmd tree onto ONE new hidden core command ‚Äî `charly __vm` (the sanctioned
`__cli-model`/`__preempt-status`/`__feature-list` internal-command pattern) ‚Äî and plugin-vm's `command:vm`
leg (command.go, cliMain) is a THIN FORWARDER that RAW-FORWARDS the pass-through args via
`syscall.Exec(CHARLY_BIN, "__vm", args‚Ä¶)`. One hidden command for the whole subtree (not one-per-leaf like
preempt/feature) because the VmCmd grammar is large + nested; raw-forwarding preserves the contract and
keeps charly's inherited stdio/TTY so `charly vm console` / `charly vm ssh` stay interactive. PLACEMENT-only
(sheds no dep ‚Äî the go-libvirt/govmm/libvirtxml stack already lived in plugin-vm).

THE PANIC RCA (a prior attempt hit `panic: duplicate command name "vm" in command "CLI"` at startup and was
reverted before diagnosis): the panic was NOT a latent dedup bug and NOT "vm is the first host-baked
verb+command plugin" (plugin-secrets is ALREADY a host-baked dual `verb:credential`+`command:secrets` plugin
and never panics). It was the plain builtin-vs-external collision: with `command:vm` declared on plugin-vm,
the prescan registers "vm" into `declaredExternalCommand` ‚Üí `collectExternalCommandPlugins()` emits a "vm"
holder, WHILE the still-registered builtin `vmCommand` (`registerDedicatedBuiltin`) ‚Üí `collectCommandPlugins()`
ALSO emits a "vm" holder; both append into `cli.Plugins` (main.go) ‚Üí two "vm" commands on the CLI root ‚Üí kong
panics at parse, for EVERY invocation. The fix IS the R5 deletion of `vmCommand`, so only the external
`command:vm` remains. Reproduced live on this branch (additive `command:vm` + vmCommand present ‚Üí panic), then
fixed (vmCommand deleted ‚Üí `charly version` / `charly box validate` exit 0).

- candy/plugin-vm: `sdk.Serve` ‚Üí `sdk.Main(&vmProvider{}, &vmMeta{}, cliMain)` (dual-mode); new command.go
  (cliMain ‚Üí execCharly ‚Üí `syscall.Exec CHARLY_BIN __vm <args‚Ä¶>`); `command:vm` added to plugin.providers
  (CLI-grammar prescan + baked `.providers`), NOT advertised in Describe (mirrors plugin-secrets).
- core: `charly/main.go` gains `VmInternal VmCmd` as the hidden `__vm` command (re-homes the whole VmCmd
  tree); the leaf-domain comment swept (vm ‚Üí EXTERNAL). pkg/arch: bakes plugin-vm in both per-plugin loops.
- R5: `charly/plugin_command_vm.go` + the `registerDedicatedBuiltin(vmCommand{})` registration DELETED;
  swept main.go (comment) + provider_command_test.go (the `vm` case dropped from
  `TestCommandProviders_NonMachineryCommands`). `git grep vmCommand|plugin_command_vm` ‚Üí CHANGELOG only.
  `TestExternalCommandExecPlan_Vm` added (the externalization gate). The deploy:vm target (`VmUnifiedTarget`)
  + kind:vm parsing stay core, untouched.

R10 (fully tested and validated): the duplicate-fix no-panic gate is proven live (`charly version` + `charly box validate`
exit 0, no panic) plus `go test ./...` green, plugin-vm `GOWORK=off go build`/`vet` clean, `charly --help`
shows `vm (out-of-process command plugin)`, `charly __vm --help` lists the re-homed VmCmd subtree. The
heavy VM live R10: **`charly check run check-charly-vm` PASS run 2026.179.0940** ‚Äî a disposable Arch-Cloud VM,
fresh rebuild: the externalized `charly vm create`/`start`/`destroy` drove a real VM through the full external
chain (command:vm plugin ‚Üí `syscall.Exec __vm` ‚Üí in-core lifecycle ‚Üí verb:libvirt RPC), including the bed
runner's OWN internal `charly vm` self-execs; deploy-add/check-live/update/cleanup all ok.

### 2026-06-28 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize `charly feature` ‚Üí candy/plugin-feature (the third WELDED-command externalization)

Moves `charly feature` (the ADE inspection verbs list/pending/validate) OUT of charly's core into the
out-of-tree COMMAND-class plugin `candy/plugin-feature` ‚Äî the 3rd WELDED-command externalization (after
tmux, preempt). The `charly feature` CLI is UNCHANGED; the implementation moved (builtin ‚Üí external, the
C1.1 stdio passthrough seam). feature was welded to the DEEPEST core ‚Äî `LoadConfig`/`ScanCandy` (the
unified loader), the `Step` plan model, and `validatePlanSteps` (SHARED with `charly box validate`, R3) ‚Äî
so all STAY core. The SOLUTION (the exact preempt precedent): the plugin shells back to NEW HIDDEN core
commands (the sanctioned `__cli-model`/`__preempt-status` pattern): `charly __feature-list` /
`__feature-pending` / `__feature-validate`, each running the in-core loader + plan-model inspection.
PLACEMENT-only (sheds no dep).

- candy/plugin-feature: new module (sdk.Main + cliMain ‚Üí kctx.Run(FeatureCmd); each leaf shell-backs to
  `CHARLY_BIN __feature-*` via syscall.Exec with arg/flag passthrough; command:feature via prescan + baked
  `.providers`).

### 2026-06-28 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize `charly preempt` ‚Üí candy/plugin-preempt (the second WELDED-command externalization)

Moves the `charly preempt` exclusive-resource preemption-lease inspector/recoverer (status /
restore) OUT of charly's core into a new OUT-OF-TREE COMMAND-class plugin candy ‚Äî the SECOND
WELDED-command externalization in the core-externalization program ("turn EVERYTHING into a plugin
incl. the welded ones"), after candy/plugin-tmux. The `charly preempt status` / `charly preempt
restore [claimant]` CLI surface is UNCHANGED; only the implementation LOCATION moved, from a builtin
CommandProvider to an external plugin dispatched via the proven C1.1 stdio passthrough seam (charly
RESOLVES the plugin binary and syscall.Exec's it in CLI mode with CHARLY_BIN stamped).

`charly preempt` was WELDED to the 1225-LOC GPU resource ARBITER (charly/preempt.go,
ResourceArbiter) which MUST STAY CORE ‚Äî it is shared by `charly vm create`
(acquireExclusiveForClaimant), `charly vm gpu`, and the check-bed runner, so the arbiter cannot move
(R3). The SOLUTION (the tmux precedent ‚Äî a plugin shells back through SANCTIONED `charly` CLI verbs,
never ad-hoc anything, R4): two NEW HIDDEN core commands expose the in-core arbiter, the SAME
`charly __cli-model` / `charly __plugin-providers` internal-command pattern ‚Äî

- `charly __preempt-status` ‚Äî `newResourceArbiter().Status()` + the active-lease table
  (renderPreemptStatus, io.Writer-split for the unit test); the verbatim former `preempt status`
  output.
- `charly __preempt-restore [claimant]` ‚Äî `reconcileStranded()` (no arg) / `ReleaseClaimant(claimant,
  true)` (with arg); the verbatim former `preempt restore` behaviour.

The plugin re-expresses each `charly preempt` leaf as a `syscall.Exec(CHARLY_BIN, "__preempt-status"/
"__preempt-restore" ‚Ä¶)` shell-back ‚Äî the dispatch seam stamps CHARLY_BIN to the dispatching charly,
so the in-core arbiter runs in the re-entered process and its stdout/stderr/exit-code flow back
through the plugin (which IS the operator's `charly preempt` process) natively. No core symbol
crosses the boundary; the arbiter logic is NOT duplicated (it stays in preempt.go, invoked ONLY by
the hidden verbs).

- candy/plugin-preempt ‚Äî new standalone Go module (go.mod + main.go/provider.go/command.go +
  schema/preempt.cue + generated params + charly.yml): `sdk.Main(&provider{}, &meta{}, cliMain)`;
  cliMain parses PreemptCmd (status / restore leaves, verbatim former-core grammar) ‚Üí kctx.Run();
  provider.Invoke returns the loud "CLI-dispatched, not gRPC" error; meta.Describe ships an empty
  capability set + the self-contained doc schema. Declares `command:preempt` (CLI prescan + baked
  `.providers`), advertises no Describe capability. ADE build-context check (`plugin: command` ‚Üí
  `true`) proves the module builds.
- charly/preempt_internal_cmd.go ‚Äî the two hidden commands (PreemptStatusInternalCmd /
  PreemptRestoreInternalCmd) registered as `__preempt-status` / `__preempt-restore` in main.go's CLI
  struct (beside `__cli-model` / `__plugin-providers`).
- charly.yml ‚Äî check-preempt-local: a disposable kind:local (host: local) R10 witness composing
  plugin-preempt; `charly preempt status` exits 0 on a fresh GPU-less host (no active leases),
  proving the externalized command + hidden-command shell-back end-to-end. `restore` (needs a live
  GPU-preemption scenario) is out of scope for the bed ‚Äî covered by the Go e2e.
- pkg/arch/PKGBUILD ‚Äî bakes plugin-preempt beside plugin-secrets/plugin-udev/plugin-tmux at
  /usr/lib/charly/plugins (build + `.providers` manifest + install), so `charly preempt` works
  project-less on a host install.
- taskfiles/Cue.yml ‚Äî candy/plugin-preempt/schema added to the cue:gen plugin-params loop.

  `registerDedicatedBuiltin(preemptCommand{})` registration; the main.go leaf-domain comment and the

  plugin_command_preempt' charly/` returns ZERO; `PreemptCmd` survives ONLY in

### 2026-06-28 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize `charly tmux` ‚Üí candy/plugin-tmux (the first WELDED-command externalization)

Moves the `charly tmux` persistent-session manager OUT of charly's core into a new OUT-OF-TREE
COMMAND-class plugin candy ‚Äî the FIRST WELDED-command externalization in the core-externalization
program ("turn EVERYTHING into a plugin incl. the welded ones"), the precedent for preempt /
feature / vm. The `charly tmux` CLI surface (shell / cmd / run / attach / list / capture / send /
kill ‚Äî the 8-leaf TmuxCmd) is UNCHANGED; only the implementation LOCATION moved, from a builtin
CommandProvider to an external plugin dispatched via the proven C1.1 stdio passthrough seam
(charly RESOLVES the plugin binary and syscall.Exec's it in CLI mode with CHARLY_BIN stamped ‚Äî the
plugin BECOMES the process with native stdio/TTY).

Unlike udev (self-contained, stdlib + x/sys/unix), `charly tmux` was WELDED to the core
venue/executor resolver: every leaf opened with `resolveCheckVenue(box, instance)`
(check_venue.go ‚Äî STAYS core, 12 callers) then ran tmux through the venue's `DeployExecutor`
(venueRun / venueCapture). The SOLUTION (no R3 violation, no ad-hoc podman, R4): the externalized
plugin RE-EXPRESSES each leaf as a shell-back through SANCTIONED `charly` CLI verbs (the CLI is the
only operational interface) ‚Äî the C1.1 stdio seam hands the plugin native stdio/TTY + CHARLY_BIN
(the dispatching charly), so the plugin re-enters that SAME binary:

- non-interactive (cmd / run / list / capture / send / kill) ‚Üí `charly cmd <box> 'tmux ‚Ä¶'` runs
  tmux on the venue's container via the existing host‚Üícontainer exec delegation. The former core
  path was `resolveCheckVenue ‚Üí ContainerChain ‚Üí <engine> exec <c> bash -c 'tmux ‚Ä¶'`; the
  shell-back is `charly cmd ‚Üí resolveContainer ‚Üí <engine> exec <c> sh -c 'tmux ‚Ä¶'` ‚Äî the SAME
  container, SAME default exec user, SAME `/tmp/tmux-<uid>/default` socket, so a session a `run`
  creates is the session a later `list`/`capture` reaches (RDD-verified live on the check-tmux-pod
  round-trip).
- interactive (shell / attach) ‚Üí `charly shell <box> -c 'tmux ‚Ä¶'` opens a real container TTY. The
  former core REQUIRED a container for shell/attach (a VM target errored with a `charly vm ssh`
  hint), so the container-scoped shell-back is faithful; the plugin owns charly's terminal, so the
  inner `charly shell` allocates `<engine> exec -it` and the TTY flows end-to-end.
- the `tmux cmd` desktop notification now fires via `charly cmd`'s OWN sanctioned completion
  notification (the `--notify`/`--no-notify` flag maps 1:1) instead of the former bespoke
  in-container gdbus call ‚Äî the CLI is the only operational interface, no re-implemented gdbus
  snippet (R3/R4). The notification text changes from "charly: sent to <session>" to "charly:
  command completed".

SCOPE NOTE (deliberate, container-scoped): the former core non-interactive leaves transparently
reached a VM / host (`.`) venue too (a side-effect of the generic resolveCheckVenue); the
`charly cmd`/`charly shell` shell-backs are container-only, so a VM/host tmux target is no longer
transparently routed (it was undocumented ‚Äî the tmux skill is exclusively container-scoped ‚Äî and
interactive shell/attach were ALREADY container-only). This matches `charly cmd`'s own scope.

- candy/plugin-tmux ‚Äî new standalone Go module (go.mod + main.go/provider.go/command.go +
  schema/tmux.cue + generated params + charly.yml): `sdk.Main(&provider{}, &meta{}, cliMain)`;
  cliMain parses TmuxCmd (the verbatim former-core leaf STRUCTS; only each Run body re-expressed as
  a shell-back) ‚Üí kctx.Run(); provider.Invoke returns the loud "CLI-dispatched, not gRPC" error;
  meta.Describe ships an empty capability set + the self-contained doc schema. The shell-quoter is
  kit.ShellQuote (imported directly, R3 ‚Äî no re-implementation). Declares `command:tmux` (CLI
  prescan + baked `.providers`), advertises no Describe capability. ADE build-context check
  (`plugin: command` ‚Üí `true`) proves the module builds.
- pkg/arch/PKGBUILD ‚Äî bakes plugin-tmux beside plugin-secrets/plugin-udev at
  /usr/lib/charly/plugins (build + `.providers` manifest + install, the per-plugin loop), so
  `charly tmux` works project-less on a host install.
- taskfiles/Cue.yml ‚Äî candy/plugin-tmux/schema added to the cue:gen plugin-params loop.
- R5 hard cutover: charly/tmux.go + charly/plugin_command_tmux.go + tmux_test.go DELETED with the
  `registerDedicatedBuiltin(tmuxCommand{})` registration; the main.go leaf-domain comment, the
  kit_aliases.go + notify.go "tmux call-site" claims, and the provider_command_test.go
  ExtractedLeafCommands case + ExtractedReachMCP assertion swept (tmux moved to the external/absent
  set beside mcp/secrets/udev). `git grep -nE 'TmuxCmd|tmuxCommand|plugin_command_tmux|execTmux|
  captureTmux|sendTmuxCommand|tmuxArgs' charly/` returns ZERO (the candy/plugin-record matches are
  that unrelated plugin's OWN tmux helpers; charly/ core is clean).
- The R10 witness BED + its bed-support BOX both live in the box/arch submodule, NOT in main:
  main owns no boxes, and a pod bed referencing a custom box is only resolvable when RUN from the
  submodule (the bed runner's `selfSuperprojectOverridePair(box/arch)` points the box's `@github`
  overthink `candy/tmux` ref at the LOCAL main working tree ‚Äî the SAME pattern box/fedora's
  check-fedora-coder-pod uses to test main's charly-mcp via the host charly, and box/arch's
  check-arch-vscode-pod uses for candy/vscode). So main carries ZERO tmux box/bed ‚Äî only the
  superproject code (candy/plugin-tmux, the charly/ deletes+sweep, taskfiles/Cue.yml, pkg/arch
  plugin bake, this CHANGELOG). The bed + box ship in the box/arch commit (its own CHANGELOG entry);
  the box bakes its tmux candy rather than using `add_candy:` (whose pod overlay was, at the time,
  BUILT but not deployed ‚Äî the separate pre-existing quirk flagged above; SINCE FIXED ‚Äî the
  add_candy-on-pod overlay now builds AND deterministically deploys via the persisted
  `resolved_image` ref; see the `check-addcandy-pod` bed). The bed's host-side check drives the
  full `charly tmux` round-trip against the deployed pod via the HOST charly under test (the baked
  plugin-tmux from pkg/arch): `run`‚Üí`list`‚Üí`capture`(RUN marker)‚Üí`send ‚Ä¶ --enter`
  (`echo TMUX-SEND-$((6*7))`)‚Üí`capture`(EXECUTED `TMUX-SEND-42`)‚Üí`kill` ‚Üí TMUX-ROUNDTRIP-OK.
