### 2026-06-28 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize `charly udev` ‚Üí candy/plugin-udev (the first externalizable-command precedent)

Moves the `charly udev` GPU-device udev-rule manager OUT of charly's core into a new OUT-OF-TREE
COMMAND-class plugin candy ‚Äî the first externalizable-command move in the core-externalization
program ("turn EVERYTHING into a plugin"). The `charly udev` CLI surface (generate / install /
remove / status) is UNCHANGED; only the implementation LOCATION moved, from a builtin
CommandProvider to an external plugin dispatched via the proven C1.1 stdio passthrough seam
(charly RESOLVES the plugin binary and syscall.Exec's it in CLI mode ‚Äî the plugin BECOMES the
process with native stdio/TTY, so the `sudo tee` / `sudo udevadm` shell-outs of install/remove
reach the real terminal).

udev was a fully SELF-CONTAINED command (stdlib + golang.org/x/sys/unix only, zero core-symbol
calls, zero shared-helper conflict ‚Äî every helper had zero callers outside udev.go), so the move
is CLEAN: a pure command-only plugin mirroring candy/plugin-example-command (no gRPC verb), not
the verb+command candy/plugin-mcp / candy/plugin-secrets. It is a PLACEMENT-only move (sheds no
dep ‚Äî x/sys/unix stays in core via devices.go/doctor.go/vm_gpu_cmd.go).

### 2026-06-28 ‚Äî fix(charly): bake_plugin: implies require: ‚Äî the baked plugin's version feeds the composing image's EffectiveVersion (#43)

Closes the S0 hash-gap (follow-up #43). A candy's `bake_plugin: <ref>` (the baked-plugin seam)
host-builds the plugin + COPYs it into the image, but did NOT pull the plugin candy's `version:`
into the composing image's **EffectiveVersion** (the `ai.opencharly.version` content-derived
label) ‚Äî only `require:` did (via `ResolveCandyOrder`'s `addTransitive`, which walks
`layer.Require`/`layer.IncludedCandy` but not `layer.BakePlugin`). So a baked-plugin change
without another layer's `version:` bump left the EffectiveVersion unchanged ‚Üí `charly clean`
retention / short-name resolution treated it as the same image ‚Üí a stale baked plugin could
escape rebuild.

- `populateCandyFromYAML` (charly/unified.go) ‚Äî the single post-parse populator shared by
  `scanCandy` (discovered) + `synthesizeInlineCandy` (inline) ‚Äî folds each `bake_plugin:` ref
  into the candy's `require:` set (deduped by `.Bare()`, the `ResolveCandyOrder` map-key form,
  so a candy declaring BOTH does not double-add; runs before `qualifyRemoteSiblingDeps` so the
  implied ref qualifies identically to an explicit require).
- R3/R5: candy/charly-mcp (the sole `bake_plugin:` consumer in the tree) declared BOTH
  `require: [plugin-mcp]` and `bake_plugin: [plugin-mcp]` ‚Äî the now-redundant explicit
  `require:` block removed.

R10 (fully tested and validated): `TestBakePluginImpliesRequire_FeedsEffectiveVersion` PASS ‚Äî
drives `populateCandyFromYAML` on a `bake_plugin`-only candy, proves the implied require + that
the baked plugin's version becomes the composing image's EffectiveVersion + bumping it bumps the
image identity + no double-add ‚Äî with a negative-proof (FAILS without the fix). `check-fedora-coder-pod`
PASS run 2026.179.0007 (10 steps, fresh-rebuild ‚Äî the bake_plugin path through build + deploy +
feature-run). `go test ./...` green; `charly box validate` clean.

### 2026-06-28 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: shed godbus ‚Äî keyring-unlock-waiter ‚Üí plugin-secrets (zero heavy deps in charly's core)

C6 of the core-externalization program ‚Äî the gocryptfs keyring-unlock-waiter (the LAST godbus
user in charly's core) moves into `candy/plugin-secrets`, shedding `github.com/godbus/dbus/v5`
ENTIRELY from `charly/go.mod` + `go.sum`. **charly's core now links ZERO heavy third-party
deps** ‚Äî completing the dep-minimization (after go-sdk / go-keyring / go-libvirt / govmm /
libvirtxml / client-go / goadb / selenium / spice).

- **The wait, via `verb:credential await-unlock`.** plugin-secrets gains `keyring_unlock_wait.go`
  ‚Äî the godbus `PropertiesChanged` subscription + a 30s backstop re-probe + a bus-unavailable
  polling fallback + `isCollectionUnlockedSignal` (beside the C2-moved `ssClient`) ‚Äî and an
  `await-unlock` method with an up-front fast-path probe that returns immediately when the
  credential is already resolvable (the common service-restart case) without touching DBus; the
  blocking subscription handles the genuinely-locked boot path.
- **Core delegates.** `pluginCredentialStore` gains `awaitUnlock` (a ctx-aware `callCtx` behind a
  `credentialAwaiter` seam); `enc.go`'s `resolveEncPassphraseForMount` delegates to it via
  `awaitKeyringUnlockViaPlugin`. The bounded `source=unavailable` retry
  (`encMountDeadline`/`encMountPollPeriod`, no godbus) STAYS in core; the mount-resolve logic +
  its 11 unit tests are unchanged.
- **Deadlock verdict** (C2 deferred godbus citing a deadlock): NOT a real deadlock ‚Äî separate
  processes, no shared lock; go-plugin v1.8.0's bare gRPC server over a local Unix socket with no
  keepalive survives the unbounded boot‚Üílogin blocking RPC; SIGTERM cancellation propagates via
  the Invoke ctx.
- **R5:** deleted `keyring_unlock_signal.go` + its test + `enc.go`'s godbus import + the three
  `waitForKeyringUnlock*` funcs + `encMountSignalBackstop`/`encMountProgressLogInterval`; swept the
  stale "godbus stays in core" comment claims; `git grep godbus charly/` returns only comments.
  Submodule (landed first): plugins (the enc + go SKILL.md doc sweep).

R10 (analysed on a live system): `TestCredentialAwaitUnlock_ExternalEndToEnd` PASS ‚Äî the
externalized `await-unlock` RPC runs out-of-process against the real baked plugin-secrets and
returns the credential. `check-k3s-vm` PASS (run 2026.178.2344) ‚Äî the `verb:credential` resolve
fresh-rebuild regression gate. `go test ./...` green; `grep godbus charly/go.mod charly/go.sum` = 0/0.
The keyring-LOCKED‚Üíunlock-with-a-real-Secret-Service bed is a noted follow-up (impractical on a
config-backend host).

### 2026-06-27 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize the secrets subsystem ‚Üí candy/plugin-secrets [verb:credential, command:secrets] (sheds go-keyring)

C2 of the core-externalization program ‚Äî the ENTIRE secrets subsystem (the credential
store backends + the `charly secrets` CLI + the GPG `.secrets` surface) moves OUT of
charly's core into `candy/plugin-secrets`, shedding `github.com/zalando/go-keyring`
ENTIRELY from `charly/go.mod` + `go.sum` (it now links only into the bundled plugin
binary). Built on C1's S0 baked-plugin seam + C1.1's stdio command seam.

- **The store, via `verb:credential`.** Moved to candy/plugin-secrets: `credential_keyring.go`
  (the go-keyring backend), `credential_config.go`, the `secret_service.go` Secret-Service
  ssClient store-CRUD, and the keyring-lock singleton. The plugin serves `verb:credential`
  (get/set/delete/list/name/resolve/health). The CORE keeps a thin `pluginCredentialStore`
  adapter (`DefaultCredentialStore()` ‚Üí it) implementing the unchanged `CredentialStore`
  interface, and `ResolveCredential` = env-check + `verb:credential resolve`; all 16 consumer
  sites (layer_secrets / secrets.go ProvisionPodmanSecrets / vnc_preresolve / config_image /
  runtime_config / the migrations / enc.go) keep using the interface. `secret_service.go`
  SPLIT: `isCollectionUnlockedSignal` stays in core (`keyring_unlock_signal.go`) for enc.go's
  unlock-waiter (C6 keeps godbus); `doctor.go`'s keyring health renders from a `verb:credential
  health` reply. Deleted `credential_store.go` (R5).
- **The CLI, via `command:secrets`** (on C1.1's stdio seam). Moved `secrets_cmd.go` +
  `secrets_gpg.go` into the plugin's `sdk.Main` cliFunc ‚Äî syscall.Exec'd, so `secrets get`
  (scriptable stdout), `secrets gpg env` (the `eval "$(‚Ä¶)"` direnv path), `secrets set` /
  `gpg edit` (TTY/$EDITOR) all work. Deleted the builtin `charly secrets` (`plugin_command_secrets.go`).
  `charly settings migrate-secrets` reparented ‚Üí `charly secrets migrate-secrets`.
- **Baked-verb discovery (S0 ‚Üí verbs).** `discoverBakedPluginWords` now registers VERB words
  (not just commands) from `.providers` manifests, with a lazy baked-verb gRPC connect on a
  ResolveVerb miss ‚Äî so a project-less HOST charly resolves `verb:credential` from the
  pkg/arch-baked `/usr/lib/charly/plugins/plugin-secrets`. New hidden `charly __plugin-providers
  <candy-dir>` emits a candy's `plugin.providers` (single source for the host bake's `.providers`,
  NOT the gRPC Describe which omits CLI-served commands). Core test seam `setDefaultCredentialStoreForTest`.
- **Submodules** (landed first): `pkg/arch` `89a9d8c..1c598a0` (bake plugin-secrets into the
  package); `plugins` `3624a57c..8d3bb716` (the R5 doc sweep).

R10: `check-k3s-vm` PASS 6/6 incl. `update` (fresh rebuild) ‚Äî the `K3S_CLUSTER_TOKEN`
`secret_require` autogen+resolve ran through the baked `/usr/lib/charly/plugins/plugin-secrets`;
`check-fedora-coder-pod` PASS (the baked-discovery generalization didn't regress `command:mcp`);
host CLI round-trips in-project + project-less; `go test ./...` green; `grep zalando/go-keyring
charly/go.mod` empty.

### 2026-06-27 ‚Äî feat(charly): stdio-passthrough command seam ‚Äî external commands `syscall.Exec` with inherited terminal stdio (restores `mcp serve --stdio`)

C1.1 of the core-externalization program ‚Äî the enabler the secrets-CLI externalization (C2) needs, and the fix for C1's `mcp serve --stdio` regression. An external COMMAND plugin (`charly <word> ‚Ä¶`) now runs as a `syscall.Exec` passthrough with the terminal's own stdin/stdout/stderr, replacing C1's gRPC `Invoke` command dispatch (which discarded the reply ‚Äî no stdout, no prompts, no `$EDITOR`).

- **Host dispatch** (`provider_command_external.go`): `dispatchExternalCommand` resolves the command word's binary via `resolveCommandPluginBinary` (baked `bakedCommandBinaries[word]` first, else project-scan ‚Üí the loader's `resolvePluginBinary`) and `syscall.Exec`s it with the raw args after the word ‚Äî charly's process is REPLACED by the plugin, so the plugin inherits stdio/TTY natively, becomes the process (the deployed `--listen` service needs no wrapper and no signal forwarding), and its exit is charly's. The child env strips the go-plugin handshake cookie (‚Üí CLI mode) and stamps `CHARLY_BIN`.
- **Dual-mode plugins** (`plugin/sdk/sdk.go`): `IsServeMode()` (handshake cookie present ‚áí gRPC serve, for the plugin's verb/kind providers) + `Main(provider, meta, cliFunc)`. A plugin binary serves gRPC when connected by the loader and runs its own CLI when `syscall.Exec`'d as a command ‚Äî same binary, two entrypoints; the verb/gRPC path is unchanged.
- **plugin-mcp**: `main()` ‚Üí `sdk.Main(‚Ä¶, cliMain)`; `cliMain` parses `serve [--listen <addr> | --stdio]`; `--stdio` restored via the go-sdk `mcp.StdioTransport` (the honest-error stub deleted); `--listen` keeps the StreamableHTTP server. `command:mcp` is dropped from the gRPC `Describe` (it's CLI-served now, not registry-resolved) but kept in the candy `plugin.providers` (drives the grammar prescan + the baked `.providers` manifest). The deployed charly-mcp service (`charly mcp serve --listen :18765`) now `syscall.Exec`s the baked plugin-mcp.
- **plugin-example-command**: dual-mode CLI (prints to real stdout); the gRPC marker-write `Invoke` deleted.
- **R5**: deleted `connectCommandPlugin`, `loadBakedPluginBinary`, `invokeCommand`, the `{"args":‚Ä¶}` Invoke marshal, the `#McpInput`/`#ExamplecommandInput` schema defs, `classCommand`, and the lazy-connect test; swept every stale reference + the obsolete stdio/Invoke/marker claims in both candy docs. `git grep` of each removed identifier is clean.

R10: `check-fedora-coder-pod` PASS 10/10 on a fresh rebuild ‚Äî the deployed `charly mcp serve --listen` (via `syscall.Exec`) serves and every mcp verb probe passes (ping / list-tools / call version / call box.list.boxes). Host proof: `charly mcp serve --stdio` returns a valid JSON-RPC `initialize` (serverInfo charly), `charly examplecommand ‚Ä¶` passes through to stdout, `--listen` binds 151 tools; `go test ./...` green.

### 2026-06-27 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize `charly mcp serve` ‚Üí candy/plugin-mcp (sheds go-sdk) + the S0 baked-plugin seam (run external plugins in a deployed container)

The first cutover of the core-externalization program (operator: "turn EVERYTHING into a plugin"). `charly mcp serve` ‚Äî the meta-command that exposes the whole charly CLI as MCP tools ‚Äî moved OUT of charly's core into `candy/plugin-mcp` as a COMMAND-class plugin, shedding `github.com/modelcontextprotocol/go-sdk` (+ google/jsonschema-go, segmentio/asm+encoding, yosida95/uritemplate, golang.org/x/oauth2) from the core binary. It is a generic whole-CLI bridge, so it can't import the package-main `CLI` tree ‚Äî instead a new hidden core seam `charly __cli-model` (cli_model_cmd.go) emits the kong command tree as `sdk.CLIModel` JSON (plugin/sdk/climodel.go), and the plugin builds its tool surface from that + drives each command by fork/exec'ing `charly <cmd>`.

- **S0 BAKED-PLUGIN SEAM (foundational).** A deployed minimal container has neither the candy source nor a go toolchain, so an external plugin its in-container charly needs at runtime (the charly-mcp service's `charly mcp serve`) must be BAKED in. New `bake_plugin:` candy field (schema/candy.cue ‚Üí spec) ‚Üí `generate.go emitBakedPlugins` host-builds the plugin binary + a `.providers` words-manifest and COPYs them into the image at `/usr/lib/charly/plugins/<leaf>` (keyed by the candy LEAF name, stable across local/@github refs ‚Äî `bakedPluginFileName`). The loader (`plugin_loader.go`): `resolvePluginBinary` prefers a baked binary over a source build; `discoverBakedPluginWords` registers a baked plugin's command words from the manifest WITHOUT connecting it (cheap); `connectCommandPlugin` lazy-connects the baked binary on dispatch. `main.go` calls `discoverBakedPluginWords()` before the command prescan. `plugin_transport.go` threads `CHARLY_BIN` (the host's os.Executable) so a command plugin calls back the SAME binary.
- **plugin-mcp.** New `command.go` (the `command:mcp` provider, routed by Class) + `serve.go` (the server ported from the deleted mcp_server.go: schema-from-CLIModel, fork/exec tool handlers, `childCharlyEnv()` strips CHARLY_PROJECT_DIR so `--repo default` never collides with the container's `CHARLY_PROJECT_DIR=/workspace`, and `__cli-model` is fetched with NO prefix so a cold-start network blip can't stickily strip the project prefix from every tool) + `schema/mcp-command.cue`/`params`. `charly.yml` advertises `[verb:mcp, command:mcp]`. `--stdio` errors honestly (the out-of-process command stdio limitation ‚Äî restored by the C1.1 follow-up).
- **R5.** Deleted mcp_server.go + plugin_command_mcp.go + their tests; repurposed the command-reflection tests (provider_command_test.go, plugin_command_udev_test.go) onto the new `buildCLIModel` seam + cli_model_cmd_test.go; swept the stale `buildMcpServer`/`mcp_server.go` comments; `mcp` dropped from the builtin-command-registration test. `go mod tidy` + a targeted go.sum prune shed the go-sdk family without the monorepo candy-require bloat.

Follow-ups opened: C1.1 (a general stdio-passthrough command seam ‚Äî host fork/execs the command plugin with inherited stdio ‚Äî to restore `mcp serve --stdio`), S0-hash-gap (make a baked plugin's content part of the composing image's EffectiveVersion so a plugin-only code change auto-invalidates the image).

R10: `check-fedora-coder-pod` PASS (10/10) on a fresh rebuild ‚Äî the deployed charly-mcp service runs `charly mcp serve` against the BAKED plugin and the mcp verb probes it: ping / list-tools / call version / **call box.list.boxes** all green (the deep RDD chased box.list.boxes through the `--repo`/`--dir` conflict ‚Üí the sticky prefix-downgrade ‚Üí the decoupling fix). `check-pod` (loader/mechanism regression) + `go test ./...` green.

### 2026-06-27 ‚Äî chore(hooks): the commit-gate recognizes .cue comment-only edits

The `pre-commit-gate.sh` comment-only detection (the `LINE_COMMENT` extension‚Üíprefix map) lacked `.cue`, so it could not certify a comment-only CUE edit as documentation ‚Äî blocking an honest `documentation reviewed` commit of a schema-comment fix (it forced either an inflated runtime tier or a deferral). Added `.cue: //` (CUE uses `//` line comments, like Go). Verified live: a comment-only `charly/schema/_common.cue` edit now commits at `documentation reviewed` (the preceding `a26ac3bf` typo-fix commit passed through the fixed gate). Operator-authorized self-modification of the gate (a guarded surface). Surfaced while landing the live-verb-migration's `_common.cue` comment-typo fix.

### 2026-06-27 ‚Äî chore(charly)!: delete the dead in-proc compiled-in-live-verb machinery + the unreachable validate_ai_artifacts feature (orphaned by the live-verb externalization); relocate the external-verb method-allowlist contract to methodspec.go

The live-verb externalization (migrations #1‚Äì#6: cdp/wl/vnc/dbus/mcp/record + the libvirt dep-shed) left ZERO compiled-in live verbs, orphaning the entire in-proc live-verb seam ‚Äî the `LiveVerbProvider` interface, the host `runCharlyVerb` subprocess dispatcher, and the `validate_ai_artifacts` AI-iteration feature whose only reader was that dispatcher. The prior cutovers RETAINED this machinery "for a future compiled-in live verb"; this cutover DELETES it. RDD confirmed each symbol's only consumers were within the dead seam itself.

- DEAD LIVE-VERB MACHINERY DELETED. `kit.LiveVerbProvider` (kit/kit.go's `CheckContext.RunCharlyVerb` hook + the interface) + the package-main `LiveVerbProvider` (provider_verb.go) + `runnerCheckContext.RunCharlyVerb` + `kitVerbLiveAdapter` + `registerCompiledDedicatedVerb` + the host `runCharlyVerb` dispatcher + `validateCharlyVerb` (validate_check.go) + the now-orphaned `validWxH` + the pluginsgen `"live"`/`NewLiveVerb` codegen branch + the schemagen `liveVerbs` slice + the `liveVerbs‚ÜíLiveVerbMethods` projection + `spec.LiveVerbMethods` (cue:gen ‚Äî vocab_gen.go) + the `checkMethodAllowlists(spec.LiveVerbMethods)` startup gate (reserved_registry.go / registry_bootstrap.go) + its test + the comment-only `verb_method_contract.go` + the ~27 dead `kit.Pos*` helpers. KEPT INTACT: `kit.CheckVerbProvider` + the in-proc Category-A verbs (file/port/http/process/‚Ä¶), the EXTERNAL verb path (runPluginVerb ‚Üí invokeVerbProvider ‚Üí Invoke), the kind/deploy/step/builder/command provider seams, and the pluginsgen verb/kind/deploy/step/builder/command shapes.
- METHOD-ALLOWLIST CONTRACT RELOCATED (NOT deleted). `kit.MethodSpec` + the six libvirt-used positional builders (`PosArtifact`/`PosKeyNameSplit`/`PosText`/`PosLibvirtQmp`/`PosCommandFields`/`PosTarget`) are the nested-CLI argv contract `candy/plugin-vm`'s libvirt verb imports ‚Äî NOT live-verb machinery ‚Äî so they moved out of the deleted `charly/plugin/kit/liveverb.go` into a new `charly/plugin/kit/methodspec.go`. `liveverb.go` is deleted.
- DEAD validate_ai_artifacts FEATURE DELETED. The flag's only reader was the unreachable `runCharlyVerb` (`if r.ValidateAiArtifacts && spec.Artifact`); `CheckEnv` never carried it to the external verbs, so it had been a no-op since the live verbs externalized. Deleted: the CUE field `validate_ai_artifacts?` (schema/deploy.cue ‚Üí cue:gen), the `Runner.ValidateAiArtifacts`/`IterStartTime` fields, the harness `RunScoringOpts` (now empty ‚Äî `RunCheckLive`/`scoreOnePodBucket` signatures simplified) + its threading in check_loop.go/check_runner_live.go/check_runner_cmd.go, and the HOST artifact-validator duplicate (`runArtifactValidators` + `assertArtifactMinDimensions`/`NotUniform`/`MinCastEvents`) + `checkRequiredFields`/`isZeroField`/`findCharlyBinary`. Artifact validation is now ALWAYS-ON in the out-of-process verb plugins via the single SDK copy `sdk.RunArtifactValidators`; its test coverage moved to `charly/plugin/sdk/artifact_test.go`. The repo's own `charly.yml` `iterate:` block dropped the now-dead `validate_ai_artifacts: true`.
- MIGRATION (intra-HEAD, NOT a HEAD bump). `drop-validate-ai-artifacts` (schema 2026.174.0051, slotted below the calver-schema stamp) strips a residual `validate_ai_artifacts` key from any `iterate:` block. RDD-confirmed the loader TOLERATES the residual key (the iterate node is not closed-validated by `#NodeDoc`), so a config carrying it still loads ‚Äî the step removes it for cleanliness; `LatestSchemaVersion()` is unchanged, so no repo-wide re-stamp. `plan-unify` no longer carries the retired flag forward.
- R5 SWEEP. `git grep` of `LiveVerbProvider`/`runCharlyVerb`/`validateCharlyVerb`/`RunCharlyVerb`/`kitVerbLiveAdapter`/`registerCompiledDedicatedVerb`/`LiveVerbMethods`/the dead `Pos*` names returns ZERO outside this CHANGELOG; the live-verb-seam references in charly/ (provider_verb/checkenv, validate_check, the schema README + _common.cue, the external-verb/appium tests) AND every candy/plugin-* plugin comment were reworded to describe the host pipeline without naming the deleted identifiers. `kit.MethodSpec` + the six live `Pos*` resolve only to methodspec.go + candy/plugin-vm.

Coverage: `go build ./...` + `go vet ./...` + `go test ./...` green (the bijection / registry / cue-reproducibility gates + the relocated SDK artifact-validator tests prove the EXTERNAL path + Category-A verbs + the libvirt nested CLI survive) + `gofmt -l` clean + `task cue:gen` idempotent + the standalone `candy/plugin-vm` `go build` (the relocated `kit.MethodSpec`/`Pos*` still satisfy the libvirt import) + `charly migrate` idempotent (strips `validate_ai_artifacts`, keeps siblings). ### 2026-06-27 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize the vnc check verb out-of-process ‚Äî pod AND vm, RFB client fully relocated (live-verb migration #4)

### 2026-06-27 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: reverse-channel RunCapture/GetFile infra + externalize the record check verb (live-verb migration #2)

The EXEC-based check verbs (record/dbus/wl) probe the live container by capturing command output / pulling artifacts ‚Äî which the E3b executor reverse channel could not do (its `RunReply` was error-only, the deploy/step legs). This cutover adds the missing legs AND externalizes `record` as the first consumer, proving the channel end-to-end.

- INFRA. `plugin.proto` `ExecutorService` gains `RunCapture(RunRequest)‚ÜíCaptureReply{stdout,stderr,exit_code,error}` + `GetFile(GetFileRequest)‚ÜíGetFileReply{content,error}` (regenerated via `task proto:gen`). `executorReverseServer` implements both (delegating to the live `DeployExecutor.RunCapture/GetFile`); `sdk.Executor` gains the client `RunCapture/GetFile`. `invokeVerbProvider` now attaches the host executor broker for external verbs (`executorInvoker.InvokeWithExecutor` with `r.Exec`), so an out-of-process exec-based check verb can call BACK against the running container. A port-based external verb (cdp/vnc/mcp/spice/kube) never dials the broker; a builtin verb never reaches here. Locked by `TestExecutorReverse_CaptureAndGetFile` (a non-zero exit rides `ExitCode`, NOT `Error`; `GetFile` reads venue files).
- RECORD EXTERNALIZED (the first consumer + the novel verb-plugin-uses-executor pattern). `charly/record.go` ‚Üí `candy/plugin-record` (main/provider/methods.go): `provider.Invoke` gets the executor via `sdk.ExecutorFromInvoke(brokerID)` (a missing broker is a hard FAIL ‚Äî record needs the live venue); the methods drive asciinema/wf-recorder via `exec.RunCapture`; `stop` pulls the `.cast`/`.mp4` via `exec.GetFile` ‚Üí `os.WriteFile(op.Artifact)` before `sdk.RunArtifactValidators`. Deleted `record.go` + the `Record RecordCmd` mount + the shim + plugin-record from `compiled_plugins`/`plugins_generated` (regenerated); record left `#OpVerb`/`liveVerbs`/`VerbCatalog` (cue:gen). BREAKING: the `charly check record` host CLI subcommand removed (declarative-only now, like mcp/spice/kube). R5: plugins submodule (11 skill files) + the charly compiled-in-verb comments (record dropped ‚Üí cdp/wl/vnc/dbus).
- COMPOSE: `require: plugin-record` in the record-authoring candies (asciinema, wf-recorder, wl-record-pixelflux) so it loads from the image closure wherever `record:` checks live.

- COMPOSE (the externalization's loading consequence ‚Äî R2). An out-of-process verb plugin loads ONLY from a checked image's candy CLOSURE (`collectReferencedPluginWords` op.Kind() then build-connects it). So every candy that AUTHORS an `mcp:` check now `require:`s plugin-mcp (the plugin-kube/k3s-server pattern): `mcp-layer`, `jupyter`, `jupyter-ml`, `marimo`, `charly-mcp`, `chrome-devtools-mcp`. Without this the baked `mcp:` checks SKIP as `unknown verb "mcp"`.

The externalized plugin HONORS the authored `mcp:` ping `timeout:` (`op.Timeout`); the in-proc path silently used a 30s flag default, masking that the authored `10s` was too short for a slow MCP server's connect+initialize (jupyter's takes >10s; list-tools/call passed at the 30s default). Every `mcp:` ping now uses `timeout: 30s` + `eventually: 90s` + `retry_interval: 3s` (the readiness-retry chrome-devtools-mcp already had): `jupyter`, `jupyter-ml`, `marimo`, `charly-mcp`, `mcp-layer`, `plugin-mcp`, `chrome-devtools-mcp`.

### 2026-06-26 ‚Äî feat(charly): thread the project defaults.readiness to out-of-process plugins via CHARLY_READINESS_* env (FU-7)

The vm shed's externalized plugins (candy/plugin-vm) poll with built-in + `CHARLY_READINESS_*` env readiness defaults only ‚Äî an out-of-process plugin cannot `LoadUnified` to read the project's `defaults.readiness`, so a project customizing it was silently ignored by the plugin's poll-gates (the operator-side stop/wait loops: `libvirt`/`vm_libvirt` StopGate, `libvirt_guest_agent` WaitCapped).

- FIX: when the host spawns an external plugin (`LocalTransport.Connect`), it threads its RESOLVED readiness (`defaults.readiness` ‚äï host env, via `loadedReadiness()`) into the plugin's spawn env as `CHARLY_READINESS_*` (`readinessPluginEnv` appended to `cmd.Env`) ‚Äî which the plugin's OWN `readinessResolve` already re-reads. So the out-of-process plugin inherits the host-resolved readiness without a project loader. Other plugins ignore the unknown env; only the vm plugin's poll-gates honor it. A resolved value that already came from a host `CHARLY_READINESS_*` env re-emits identically (no ambiguity on the duplicate key).
- R3: the readiness field set is consolidated into ONE package-level table (`readinessSpecs`) ‚Äî `readinessResolve` READS it (config/env/fallback ‚Üí resolved); `readinessPluginEnv` WRITES it (resolved ‚Üí env) ‚Äî replacing the former inline spec list, so the `CHARLY_READINESS_*` env-name set lives once in core.

Coverage: `TestReadinessPluginEnv_RoundTrips` (host-resolved ‚Üí `CHARLY_READINESS_*` ‚Üí re-resolved via `readinessResolve`, the plugin's path, == the same bounds ‚Äî fails without the emitter). R10: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` ‚Äî PASS (steps=6), run `2026.177.1438`; the vm plugin spawns with the readiness env + `libvirt-verb-dispatches` passes on a fresh rebuild (`update` + `cleanup` green). `go test ./...` green; build + gofmt + vet clean.

### 2026-06-26 ‚Äî fix(charly): reliable unpinned cloud_image cache-reuse + restore the externalized VM check-verb surface (check-arch-vm)

One cutover, several interdependent fixes for the `check-arch-vm` bed ‚Äî each surfaced, and blocking, during the previous one's R10 (R2 ‚Äî fixed in the same working tree; none alone leaves the bed green).

- **(1) Unpinned cloud_image cache-reuse (R2/R3 from the fedora-vm pin).** box/arch's `arch-vm` cloud_image uses a rolling `images/latest/` Arch URL that cannot take a static pin, so it RE-DOWNLOADED the full qcow2 on every VM build ‚Äî the every-run-re-download class that tripped Fedora-mirror 403s. `http_fetch.go`'s cache-hit gate required a pinned `expected` sha256. FIX (generic): relax to `(expected == "" || existing == expected)` ‚Äî an unpinned cloud_image is reused via its own download-computed recorded sum; pinned images keep the stronger check. Coverage `TestFetchQcow2_ReusesUnpinnedCachedImage`.
- **(2‚Äì4) Three regressions from the go-libvirt shed (v2026.177.0911)** that externalized the VM/spice/libvirt verbs to the out-of-process candy/plugin-vm + candy/plugin-spice. They surfaced only on `check-arch-vm` (the only bed with specific-domain libvirt/spice probes whose deploy name ‚âÝ vm-entity name); `check-fedora-vm` uses only `libvirt: list` (no specific-domain lookup) so it never tripped them.
  - **(2) Operator-side VM-domain-name remap (R1).** The shed dropped the deploy-name‚Üívm-entity-name remap (`uf.Bundle[name].From`) when ResolveVmTarget moved out-of-process (the plugin can't LoadUnified). The host check-runner passed `Runner.Box` (the deploy/bed name `check-arch-vm`) as the verb target, so the plugin prefixed `charly-` ‚Üí looked up the non-existent `charly-check-arch-vm` instead of the live `charly-arch`. FIX (charly core): `Runner` gains `VmName` (set in `runVm` from the already-resolved entity) + a `vmTargetName()` accessor (VmName if set, else Box); the wire field every out-of-process verb reads ‚Äî `snapshotCheckEnv`'s `CheckEnv.Box` ‚Äî plus `spice_preresolve.go` and `checkrun_charly_verbs.go` all read `vmTargetName()`. Pods/k8s/android leave VmName empty ‚Üí unchanged. Coverage `TestRunner_vmTargetName`.
  - **(3) SPICE tunnel misclassification.** `candy/plugin-vm/vm_target.go` set `TunnelNeeded: t.Uri != ""`, but the resolve-spice/resolve-vnc handler defaults an empty URI to the LOCAL `qemu:///session` ‚Äî so a local VM's SPICE endpoint was wrongly SSH-tunnelled to an empty target ("ssh tunnel to @:0"). FIX: `TunnelNeeded: uriNeedsTunnel(t.Uri)` (a new helper testing the remote `qemu+ssh://` SCHEME, shared by spice + vnc ‚Äî R3), matching the field's documented intent.
  - **(4) Out-of-process verb stderr not captured.** `candy/plugin-vm/provider.go`'s `captureStdout` redirected only `os.Stdout`, so a verb writing its result to stderr (guest/ping's "agent responsive") had its `stderr:` matcher see empty. FIX: `captureStdout` ‚Üí `captureOutput` captures BOTH streams; the libvirt handler threads the captured stderr into the result.
- **R1/R5 doc sweep (same origin).** The shed left stale "stays in core" prose in the spice + libvirt check skills claiming `vm_target.go` / `ResolveVmTarget` / `libvirt_cmd.go` / go-libvirt live in charly core ‚Äî they're in candy/plugin-vm now. Corrected across plugins/check/skills/{spice,libvirt}/SKILL.md.

R10: `charly -C box/arch check run check-arch-vm` ‚Äî PASS (steps=13), run `2026.177.1342`; check-live 60/60 INCLUDING the fresh-rebuild re-verification (`update` ‚Üí `check-live-rebuild`). The three formerly-failing classes pass: `libvirt=info` ‚Üí `charly-arch`, `spice=status` ‚Üí ok, `guest/ping` ‚Üí "agent responsive" (vs runs `.1109`/`.1221` which failed all 10 operator-side probes). `go test ./...` green; both modules build; gofmt + vet clean.

### 2026-06-26 ‚Äî fix(charly): restore host-side egress validation of the VM domain XML (the vm shed dropped it)

R2 immediate-next from the vmshared-dedup R10's transitional sweep (Task 7). The go-libvirt shed externalized VM create to the out-of-process candy/plugin-vm, which NO-OP'd `ValidateEgress`/`ValidateXMLEgress` (`egress_stub.go`) carrying a "DELETE this stub + move validation host-side BEFORE the R10 acceptance run" TODO that was never honored ‚Äî so the VM's rendered libvirt **domain XML was created UNCHECKED** against egress policy. (Cloud-init was unaffected ‚Äî it's egress-validated host-side when the host builds the seed ISO via `RegenerateSeedISO` ‚Üí `RenderCloudInit` ‚Üí `ValidateEgress`; only the domain XML was dropped.)

- FIX: the verb-create RPC has no reverse channel, so validation is restored via a **two-phase `ValidateOnly` create** ‚Äî the plugin renders + RETURNS the domain XML (`validate_only=true` ‚Üí `rendered_domain_xml`), the host runs the real `charly/egress.go` `ValidateXMLEgress`, and only then issues the create call. The out-of-process plugin must NOT carry the egress subsystem (the design the stub's TODO intended). `vmCreateReq` gains `ValidateOnly`; the create reply gains `rendered_domain_xml`; `runVmSpecCreate` (core) does render‚Üívalidate‚Üícreate. QEMU returns no XML (its cloud-init is already host-validated), so its validate pass is a no-op gate.
- Removed the misleading inline no-op `ValidateXMLEgress` from the plugin's `libvirt_yaml_bridge.go` (the host validates now) + the now-unused `egress_stub.go` `ValidateXMLEgress`. `egress_stub.go`'s `ValidateEgress` stays (the plugin's defer-to-host `vmshared.ValidateEgress` hook wiring) with a corrected comment.
- R5/Task-7 sweep: removed the stale "Phase-A/Phase-B" transitional comments across `candy/plugin-vm` (`egress_stub`, `vm_phaseA_shims`, `provider`, `vm_create_spec`) ‚Äî they framed DONE host-side work (boot-autostart prereqs, the ssh-config alias, the wired lifecycle/display ops) as pending phases.
- R3: documented decision to keep `vm_phaseA_shims.go`'s trivial host-detection trio (`libvirtSessionURI` + `qemuSystemBinary` + `startLibvirtUserSession`, ~13 lines) as a per-module copy of core's `charly/vm.go` ‚Äî below the bar for exporting trivia across the module boundary; the substantial shared VM code already lives in `vmshared`.
- Tracked follow-up (docs/status.md FU-7, minor): the host's project-configured `defaults.readiness` is not yet threaded through the create RPC ‚Äî the plugin polls with built-in + `CHARLY_READINESS_*` env defaults only.

R10: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` ‚Äî PASS (steps=6), run `2026.177.1052`; the vm-create step's two-phase egress-validating create passed (the host `ValidateXMLEgress`-gated the rendered domain XML before create); `libvirt-verb-dispatches` + `LOCALPKG-RPM-AUTORESOLVE-OK` green. Coverage: `TestVmCreate_HostEgressValidatesReturnedDomainXML` (the host decode+gate REJECTS a policy-violating domain XML, ACCEPTS a valid one, SKIPS QEMU's no-XML) ‚Äî fails without the fix. `go test ./...` green; both modules build; gofmt + go vet clean.

### 2026-06-26 ‚Äî refactor(charly): extract shared VM code into charly/vmshared ‚Äî kill the vm-shed's 3,444-line cross-module duplication (R3)

R2 immediate-next from the go-libvirt shed (earlier today). That cutover externalized the VM subsystem into the out-of-process candy/plugin-vm, but because a separate Go module cannot import charly's `package main`, it COPIED 17 byte-identical VM / libvirt / cloud-init / qemu / ovmf / ssh files (3,444 lines) into the plugin instead of sharing them ‚Äî a large R3 violation surfaced by the post-land R5/R3 self-test (and confirmed plugin-vm-specific: zero duplication across the other 40 plugin candies).

- FIX: the 17 files now live ONCE in a new importable package `github.com/overthinkos/overthink/charly/vmshared` (package vmshared), consumed by BOTH the charly core and the candy/plugin-vm module (the latter via its existing `replace ‚Ä¶ => ../../charly`).
- The cluster was not fully self-contained: several files call backends with DIFFERENT impls per module (the 7 snapshot backends ‚Äî core RPCs the plugin vs the plugin's go-libvirt impl; CUE egress validation ‚Äî core's real validator vs the plugin's no-op). These are wired as 10 injection seams in `charly/vmshared/hooks.go` (swappable vars), populated per-module in each consumer's `vmshared_aliases.go` `init()`, following the codebase's existing swappable-var idiom (`var InspectContainer`). Behavior is preserved exactly.
- Type/var aliases in `charly/vmshared_aliases.go` + `candy/plugin-vm/vmshared_aliases.go` keep existing call sites compiling unchanged. OVMF path-table parsing became `sync.OnceValue` so the embedded-defaults hook runs at first use (after the consumer injects it), not during vmshared package-init.
- Also fixed 6 gofmt deviations the shed left behind (check_cmd.go, checkspec.go, vm_plugin_client.go + the plugin's libvirt.go, provider.go, vm_create_spec.go) ‚Äî R1 zero-warnings.
- Bumps the box/fedora pointer to include the `fedora-vm` checksum pin (the bed-flakiness fix this cutover's R10 surfaced ‚Äî see box/fedora CHANGELOG).

R10: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` ‚Äî PASS (steps=6), run `2026.177.0948`, all 6 steps ok; LOCALPKG-RPM-AUTORESOLVE-OK + libvirt-verb-dispatches both PASS (the dedup'd plugin builds + dispatches the verb live). Unit gates: `go test ./...` green (core + the new charly/vmshared); `candy/plugin-vm` builds (GOWORK=off); `go vet` clean both modules; zero byte-identical .go files remain between charly/ and candy/plugin-vm/.

### 2026-06-26 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: shed go-libvirt + govmm + libvirtxml ‚Äî VM subsystem externalized to the out-of-process candy/plugin-vm

The largest single dependency shed of the core-externalization program. Charly's ENTIRE VM subsystem ‚Äî the `libvirt` check verb, the `charly vm` lifecycle (create/start/stop/destroy/list/import/snapshot), and the libvirt/qemu/cloud-init/OVMF renderers ‚Äî moved OUT of charly's core into the OUT-OF-PROCESS plugin `candy/plugin-vm` (go-plugin gRPC). `github.com/digitalocean/go-libvirt`, `github.com/kata-containers/govmm`, and `libvirt.org/go/libvirtxml` are GONE from `charly/go.mod` + `go.sum`.

- ARCHITECTURE: the plugin owns the go-libvirt/govmm impl and takes ALL project-dependent data from the host (it never loads charly.yml). Core's consumers RPC it through the single choke point `invokeVmPluginEnv` (charly/vm_plugin_client.go): the lifecycle (`runVmSpecCreate` ‚Üí create op; startVM/stopVM/destroy/list; runCleanOrphans), snapshot internal+external (vm_snapshot_client.go), qemu-QMP shutdown (vm_qemu_client.go), import (domain-xml/list-all-domains), and the spice/vnc/ssh/status/preempt display+state resolvers. Pure-host helpers (libvirtSessionSocket, killQemuByPID, the cloud-init seed, OVMF path resolution, CollectLibvirtSnippets, writeJSON) stay core in vm_host_helpers.go / vm_create_spec.go.
- REGISTRATION: `candy/plugin-libvirt` (the former compiled-in libvirt live-verb candy) DELETED + removed from `compiled_plugins`; `candy/plugin-vm` is EXTERNAL (discovered by loadProjectPlugins). `libvirt` reclassified from a compiled-in verb to an EXTERNAL-CHARLY-VERB like kube/adb/spice: removed from `#OpVerb` (schema/_common.cue), schemagen `liveVerbs`, and `VerbCatalog` (checkspec.go); vocab_gen.go + cue_types_gen.go regenerated.
- PLUGIN REACHABILITY (the load-bearing wiring, found + fixed on the disposable bed across three RCAs): the external libvirt plugin registers only at `loadProjectPlugins` time, which the `charly vm` lifecycle + status/preempt/ssh/vnc/spice paths and the check runner did NOT reach. Fixed with ONE shared `vmPluginCandyRef()` ("@"+DefaultProjectRepo+"/candy/plugin-vm") pulled via `ResolveOpts.ExtraCandyRefs` (its documented host-side-plugin purpose) in both load paths: `ensureVmPluginConnected` (a sync.Once lazy build-connect, falling back to the canonical ref when a `box/<distro>` project's closure lacks the plugin) and the check runner. The check runner's load-scope also now surfaces each plan step's verb discriminator (`deployNodePluginContext` op.Kind()), so a bed's `libvirt: list` step reaches the loader (it was SKIPPing as "unknown verb").
- DELETED from core: vm_libvirt.go, vm_qemu.go, vm_target.go, vm_snapshot_libvirt.go, vm_snapshot_internal.go, libvirt_cmd.go, libvirt_ops.go, libvirt_guest_agent.go, libvirt_yaml_bridge.go + InjectLibvirtXML (libvirt.go) + runVmSpecCreateLibvirt/Qemu (vm_create_spec.go) + the core `charly check libvirt` CLI field (it nests via the external plugin, like kube/adb). The VM-rendering unit tests moved to candy/plugin-vm.

R10: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` (disposable Fedora Cloud VM bed) ‚Äî GREEN on a fresh rebuild. vm-create dispatched the create op through the external plugin; the `libvirt-verb-dispatches` check RAN-and-PASSED (`libvirt: list` through candy/plugin-vm listed the live host domain `charly-fedora-vm running`); the fresh-`charly update` rebuild gate passed; the VM was destroyed on cleanup. `go test ./...` green (core + candy/plugin-vm). Residual bed warnings are documented-external (xorriso's ISO-9660 complaint about cloud-init's mandatory lowercase `cidata` volid; dnf's expected `--dev-local-pkg` OpenPGP skip; a guest systemd drop-in warning) ‚Äî none charly-emitted, all pre-existing.

### 2026-06-26 ‚Äî fix(traefik): the traefik-acme-storage-resolved check was inverted by `${HOME}` matcher substitution

RCA'd (R1) when it surfaced as the sole FAIL during an unrelated candy-config R10 (`check-fedora-test-pod`). The check `traefik-acme-storage-resolved` asserted `not_contains: "${HOME}"` to prove the build-time `${HOME}`‚Üíreal-home `sed` (traefik-step-3) worked. But the plan runner VARIABLE-SUBSTITUTES `${HOME}` in the matcher value itself ‚Üí `not_contains: "/home/user"`. The correctly-resolved file contains `storage: /home/user/.traefik/...`, so the substituted matcher `not_contains "/home/user"` FAILS ‚Äî i.e. the check inverted: it passed only when the substitution had NOT happened. The author intended `${HOME}` as a LITERAL; the runner treats it as a variable.

- FIX: removed the broken `not_contains: "${HOME}"` matcher. The positive `matches: "storage: /home/"` already fully proves resolution ‚Äî an unsubstituted file would read `storage: ${HOME}/...` and FAIL that match ‚Äî so no coverage is lost. Reworded the check description to match (R5).
- SWEEP (R1/R5, claim-keyed): `grep -F` across every `candy/*/charly.yml` plan confirms this was the ONLY check asserting a literal `${...}` in a matcher ‚Äî a one-off, not a class.

Verified: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-test-pod` ‚Äî GREEN (exit 0, 10/10 steps); `traefik-acme-storage-resolved` PASSES in all four phases (check-image / check-live / feature-run / feature-run-rebuild), through the fresh-rebuild gate.

### 2026-06-26 ‚Äî fix(charly): cloud-init readiness gate hung ALL VM check-live beds (run `sudo cloud-init status`)

RCA'd (R1) during the libvirt live-verb relocation's R10 (the cutover below): `SSHExecutor.WaitForCloudInit` polled `cloud-init status` as the NON-ROOT ssh user. On Fedora 43 / cloud-init 25.2 / Python 3.14 that crashes with `PermissionError` reading the root-only `/run/cloud-init/cloud.cfg` ‚Üí stderr suppressed (`2>/dev/null`), exit swallowed (`|| true`) ‚Üí blank stdout ‚Üí the poll (no "running"/"done" token) treated blank as "keep polling" ‚Üí `runVm` (check_cmd.go) passes `context.Background()` with only a 30-min absolute cap ‚Üí a **30-minute SILENT HANG of every VM check-live**, then SIGKILL (exit 255). The deploy path tolerated the same crash (logs + continues); only check-live's `runVm` hard-waited.

- FIX: the gate runs `sudo cloud-init status` (RDD-proven on a live Fedora 43 guest: non-root ‚Üí `PermissionError` rc=1; `sudo` ‚Üí `status: done` rc=0; charly-managed guests have passwordless sudo). cloud-init had actually settled long ago (root: `status: done`, finished ~15s after boot) ‚Äî the gate was waiting forever for a guest that was already done.
- R5/R1 doc sweep: the gate's comments claimed it runs `cloud-init status --wait` (stale ‚Äî it polls non-wait status) ‚Äî corrected in deploy_executor_ssh.go, check_bed_run.go, check_cmd.go.
- Bed coverage: a `libvirt: list` check (`libvirt-verb-dispatches`) added to check-fedora-vm's plan (box/fedora) ‚Äî gives the relocated libvirt live-verb (candy/plugin-libvirt) its dedicated VM-bed proof, dispatching through the candy ‚Üí cc.RunCharlyVerb ‚Üí host `charly check libvirt list`.
- R2 bug fix surfaced by that new check: `libvirt: list` lacked `SkipBox` in the allowlist (candy/plugin-libvirt), so runCharlyVerb appended the deploy name as a positional and `charly check libvirt list` (which takes `[flags]` only ‚Äî it's host-side, lists ALL session domains) rejected it (`unexpected argument`). PRE-EXISTING (the package-main allowlist had the same latent gap ‚Äî `list` was the only libvirt method never exercised by a bed; the other methods take `<vm>` = the image positional correctly). Fixed: `SkipBox: true` on `list`.

Verified: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` ‚Äî check-live now COMPLETES (was a 30-min SIGKILL hang); the `libvirt: list` check PASSES through candy/plugin-libvirt; the localpkg-rpm-autoresolve check still passes; fresh feature-run-rebuild leg green.

### 2026-06-25 ‚Äî refactor(charly): live-verb dispatch contract (MethodSpec + posArgs) ‚Üí importable kit

STEP 0 of relocating the seven live-container verbs (cdp/wl/vnc/dbus/mcp/record/libvirt) into candies: the verb-dispatch CONTRACT types now live in the importable kit, so a future live-verb CANDY can author its method allowlist without importing charly's package main.

- NEW `charly/plugin/kit/liveverb.go`: `kit.MethodSpec` (the per-method dispatch spec ‚Äî `Path`/`Required`/`PosArgs`/`Artifact`/`SkipBox`, exported fields) + the ~37 `kit.PosX` positional-arg builders (`PosTab`‚Ä¶`PosLibvirtQmp`, reading `*spec.Op`) ‚Äî the single shared source.
- DELETED from `charly/checkrun_charly_verbs.go`: the package-main `methodSpec` type + the duplicate posArgs library (‚àí318 lines). `runCharlyVerb` now consumes `map[string]kit.MethodSpec` directly; the host-side dispatch framework (the `runCharlyVerb` subprocess dispatcher, the artifact validators, `resolveCheckApk`, `findCharlyBinary`, the `artifactValidatableMethods` allowlist) STAYS in package main.
- The seven `plugin_verb_<verb>.go` allowlists + `provider_verb.go`'s `LiveVerbProvider.Methods()` + `validate_check.go` + the `validate_ai` test now reference `kit.MethodSpec` / `kit.PosX` ‚Äî one source of truth (R3), no duplication.
- No behavior change (a pure type relocation). The next step (per-verb candy relocation) adds `kit.LiveVerbProvider` + a `CheckContext.RunCharlyVerb` delegation hook so a candy verb authors its allowlist and the host runs the dispatch.

Verified: `go test ./...` (the `runCharlyVerb` framework + dispatch tests pass with the kit types), `task build:charly`, `charly -C box/fedora check run check-pod`.

### 2026-06-25 ‚Äî feat(charly): the host-engine kit ‚Äî relocate the `port` check verb into a compiled-in candy

`charly/plugin/kit`: the importable contract a HOST-COUPLED check verb implements to run IN-PROCESS against
the live check engine ‚Äî so a verb whose logic needs the running `*Runner` (exec-in-container, host TCP dial,
the HTTP client) can live in its OWN candy module. First relocation on it: the `port` verb ‚Üí `candy/plugin-port`.
The enabler for moving the remaining ~25 host-coupled check verbs/kinds out of charly's module.

- `kit`: `CheckContext` interface (Exec/Mode/HTTPClient/DialTimeout/Box/Instance/Distros) + `Executor` (the
  `DeployExecutor` RunCapture+Kind subset) + `Result`/`Status` + `CheckVerbProvider{RunVerb(ctx, CheckContext, *spec.Op)}`.
  Imports only stdlib + `charly/spec`.
- `check_kit_adapter.go`: `runnerCheckContext` (*Runner ‚Üí kit.CheckContext), `kitVerbAdapter` (kit provider ‚Üí
  package-main `CheckVerbProvider`, converting `kit.Result`‚Üí`CheckResult`), `registerCompiledCheckVerb`
  (concats the candy's raw schema FS via `schemaconcat` + registers through `RegisterBuiltinPluginUnit`).
  Host-coupled candies are COMPILED-IN-ONLY (the live CheckContext can't cross a process boundary).
- `pluginsgen` detects the kit shape (candy exports `NewCheckVerb`) ‚Üí emits `registerCompiledCheckVerb` vs
  `registerCompiledPlugin` (the pb dual-placement path).
- `candy/plugin-port`: `NewCheckVerb` + the moved `runPort`/`dialPort` logic (on `kit.CheckContext`) +
  `SchemaFS`/`InputDefs`; `compiled_plugins` += `plugin-port`; `cue:gen` loop += `candy/plugin-port/schema`.
- DELETED `charly/plugin/builtins/port/` + `charly/plugin_port.go` + the now-dead `r.runPort`/`r.dialPort` +
  the unused `net` import in checkrun.go (R5).
- R10: `go test ./...` PASS; `task build:charly` OK; `charly check run check-pod` PASS (steps=10) ‚Äî the bed's
  `:18794` port check now dispatches the compiled-in kit candy through `runnerCheckContext`.

### 2026-06-25 ‚Äî feat(charly): charly.yml-selectable compiled-in plugin candies (the in-proc placement of a candy)

A plugin candy can now be COMPILED INTO the charly binary, selected per-charly-build by a new additive
`compiled_plugins:` directive in charly.yml ‚Äî the in-proc placement of an out-of-tree candy, the dual of the
existing out-of-process gRPC path. Anything not selected still loads out-of-process when referenced (the
placements COEXIST). First step of the program to relocate ALL plugins into candies.

- `compiled_plugins:` added to `#NodeDoc` (`charly/schema/node.cue`, regenerated `DocDirectives` via
  `task cue:gen`) + the embedded `charly/charly.yml`. `pluginsgen` (`charly/internal/pluginsgen`, run by
  `task build:charly` before `go build`, `GOWORK=off`, stdlib+yaml only) reads it and emits
  `charly/plugins_generated.go` (one `registerCompiledPlugin` per candy) + the repo-root `go.work` (a
  `use ./candy/<name>` per candy). Both COMMITTED + reproducibility-gated (`TestPluginsGenReproducible`);
  `go.work` / `go.work.sum` un-ignored.
- `InProcServedTransport` + `inprocProvider` + `registerCompiledPlugin` (`charly/plugin_inproc.go`): a
  compiled-in candy's pb provider is driven IN-PROCESS ‚Äî `Describe` ‚Üí the SAME `buildUnit` capability-lift +
  `loadBuiltinPluginUnits` schema gate an external goes through; each capability wrapped in an `inprocProvider`
  (the in-proc twin of `grpcProvider`, origin `"builtin"`). Dispatch is registry-routed, transport-invisible.
- Coexist switch (`pluginAlreadyConnected`): a word registered origin `"builtin"` (compiled in) SKIPS the
  out-of-process host build instead of colliding. New `originBuiltin` const is the single source.
- `buildPluginBinary` now builds with `GOWORK=off` (the out-of-process build is standalone in the candy's own
  module, never the repo workspace) and targets `./cmd/serve` when present.
- Reference: `candy/plugin-example-external` relocated to the dual-placement shape (importable root package +
  `cmd/serve` shim) + added to `compiled_plugins` ‚Äî now BOTH the compiled-in AND the out-of-process example
  (check renamed `externalprobe-out-of-proc` ‚Üí `externalprobe-dispatches`, placement-agnostic).
- R10: `go test ./...` PASS; `task build:charly` (installs via the new pluginsgen path) OK; `charly check run
  check-pod` PASS (steps=10), testing LOCAL candies ‚Äî exercises the compiled-in `externalprobe` dispatch, the
  coexist skip, and `GOWORK=off` host-builds of the out-of-process examplestep/examplebuilder plugins.

### 2026-06-24 ‚Äî feat(charly): command class out-of-process ‚Äî an external command plugin contributes a `charly <word>` CLI subcommand

The LAST builtin‚Üíexternal class: a candy declaring `plugin: providers: [command:<word>]` now contributes a
`charly <word>` CLI subcommand served OUT-OF-PROCESS. All six provider classes (kind/verb/deploy/step/builder/
command) are now external-capable, placement-agnostic.

The chicken-and-egg (the command WORD must be in the Kong grammar to parse `charly <word>`, but connecting the
provider needs the project dir ‚Äî itself a Kong flag) is solved by a prescan mirroring `plugin_prescan.go`'s
deploy-substrate recognition:

- `plugin_command_prescan.go` `prescanProjectCommandWords` (called in main BEFORE `kong.Parse`) byte-gated-reads
  the project's discovered candy manifests + registers each declared external COMMAND word
  (`declaredExternalCommand`; `prescanPluginManifest` now registers `ClassDeployTarget` AND `ClassCommand`).
  `projectDirPreParse` / `scanDirFlag` resolve the project dir pre-parse.
- `collectExternalCommandPlugins` builds a Kong grammar holder for each prescanned word (provider UNconnected),
  so `charly <word>` parses; `dispatchExternalCommand` LAZY-connects on actual invocation (`connectCommandPlugin`
  ‚Üí `loadProjectPlugins` scoped to the one word) then `Invoke(OpRun, {args})`. The host build + gRPC connect is
  paid ONLY when the command runs, never on every charly call. A project with no command plugins registers
  nothing (the grammar is byte-for-byte the builtin set).
- `candy/plugin-example-command` (the example: `Invoke(OpRun)` writes a marker from its args).
- `TestCommandPrescan_RegisterAndCollect` + `TestDispatchExternalCommand_LazyConnect` + `TestScanDirFlag` + the
  existing `TestExternalCommandSeam_*` (now word-keyed).

R10: `charly examplecommand <marker> hello` live ‚Äî the plugin connected over gRPC + wrote the marker (args
joined); `charly --help` lists `examplecommand` (prescan‚Üígrammar). `check-local` PASS (the prescan-at-startup
regression ‚Äî it runs on every charly invocation in a project dir). Fresh-rebuild re-verified.

### 2026-06-24 ‚Äî perf(charly): loadProjectPlugins scopes to plan-referenced plugins (no longer host-builds every external plugin)

`loadProjectPlugins` now host-builds + connects ONLY the out-of-tree plugin candies whose declared providers are
REFERENCED by the work at hand ‚Äî instead of every external plugin candy in the scanned set ‚Äî shrinking the
build-time exec surface + cost. All 3 callers (build `NewGenerator`, deploy `loadDeployPlugins`, check
`attachCheckRunnerContext`) collect the COMPLETE reference set (candy + box plan plugin verbs, `external_builder`
fields, deploy substrate, inline/flattened bed-plan verbs, `add_candy`) via `collectReferencedPluginWords`;
class-agnostic word matching errs toward INCLUDE (over-load safe ‚Äî NO under-load). Builtins (`init()`-registered)
are unaffected.

- `plugin_loader.go` `collectReferencedPluginWords` + `pluginProvidesReferencedWord`; `loadProjectPlugins(ctx,
  candies, refs)`. `deployNodePluginContext` replaces `deployAddCandyRefs` (R3 ‚Äî one bed-node resolve returns
  add_candy + the substrate/inline plugin words). `generate.go` / `deploy_add_shared.go` / `check_cmd.go` compute
  + pass the reference set. NO CUE schema change, NO HEAD bump.
- Unit tests `TestCollectReferencedPluginWords_Scoping` + `_ClassAgnostic`.

R10 (cross-cutting ‚Üí multi-bed fan-out, proving NO under-load): `check-pod` PASS 10/10 (build ‚Äî external
step+builder plugins loaded + executed), `check-local` PASS 4/4 (deploy verb-as-step plugin loaded),
`check-exampledeploy` PASS 4/4 (external deploy substrate plugin loaded); all zero warnings.

### 2026-06-24 ‚Äî feat(charly): step deploy-execute ‚Äî an external verb-as-step runs at DEPLOY via the reverse channel (OpExecute)

The deploy-context half of the verb/step leg: a `run: plugin: <verb>` step whose verb is an external
grpcProvider now EXECUTES at DEPLOY (local/vm target, where the install runs on the target, not baked) via the
E3b ExecutorService reverse channel ‚Äî the deploy counterpart of the build-context `OpEmit`-into-the-Containerfile.
So the verb/step class is external-capable at BUILD (`OpEmit`) AND DEPLOY (`OpExecute`), placement-agnostic.

- `compileActOp` (install_build.go) routes a `plugin:` verb whose provider is an `executorInvoker`
  (`InvokeWithExecutor`, satisfied only by `*grpcProvider`) to the new `ExternalPluginStep` IR kind
  (install_plan.go, `StepKindExternalPlugin`; registered in `allStepKinds`, provider_step.go). A builtin
  `ProvisionActor` / `command` keep their existing path ‚Äî the `executorInvoker` discriminator mirrors the
  build-context `BuildEmitter` marker (R3).
- `plugin_step_external.go`: `externalPluginStepProvider` ‚Äî `EmitOCI` reuses `emitPluginFragment` (build/pod-overlay
  venue); `EmitLocal`/`EmitVM` call `executeExternalPluginStep` ‚Üí `InvokeWithExecutor(OpExecute)` over the reverse
  channel (the plugin runs its deploy-context effect on the target via the live `DeployExecutor`), decode
  `spec.DeployReply`, and RECORD its `ReverseOp`s to the ledger so `bundle del` replays them (record-and-replay,
  R3). `spec.DeployReply`/`ReverseOp` reused verbatim; NO new wire type, NO CUE schema change, NO HEAD bump.
- `candy/plugin-example-step` extended to handle `OpExecute` (writes a host-venue probe marker, returns a removing
  reverse op) + `candy/examplestep-deploy-consumer` (a deploy-context `run: plugin: examplestep` step).

R10: `charly check run check-local` PASS 4/4, zero warnings; `examplestep-deploy-marker` PASS (the verb-as-step
executed at local deploy, the `OpExecute` marker present over the reverse channel); `update` re-applied
idempotently; `cleanup` (bundle del) replayed the reverse op (host clean). Go e2e
`TestExternalPluginStep_ReverseChannelEndToEnd` proves the full `OpExecute` + reverse-op replay.

### 2026-06-24 ‚Äî feat(charly): build-time plugin execution ‚Äî an external plugin's OpEmit bakes a Containerfile fragment at image build (placement-agnostic, builtin OR external)

The build-time half of the EVERY-KIND-IS-A-PLUGIN program: a `run:` plugin verb step now EXECUTES at image
build, so an out-of-tree plugin candy is host-built, connected out-of-process, and its `OpEmit` Invoked during
`charly box build` ‚Äî the returned Containerfile FRAGMENT spliced verbatim into the generated Containerfile.
Placement-agnostic above the registry: a plugin works identically whether compiled into `charly` (builtin) OR
dynamically loaded as an external candy, at BOTH deploy and image-build time ‚Äî the foundation for migrating every
internal/builtin plugin external in future cutovers.

- **Build-time connect seam** (`generate.go` `NewGenerator`): `loadProjectPlugins` connects the project's
  out-of-tree plugin candies during image generation, so an external step/verb provider registers + is dialable
  at build. A builtin is already registered via `init()`; only an external is host-built + connected here.
- **Placement-agnostic emit** (`tasks.go` `emitTasks` + `emitPluginFragment`): a `plugin:` verb that is a builtin
  `ProvisionActor` renders its act shell in-proc (the zero-JSON fast path); any other resolved provider (an
  external `grpcProvider`, or a builtin `BuildEmitter`) renders its fragment via `Invoke(OpEmit)` ‚Äî in-proc for a
  builtin, over go-plugin gRPC for an external ‚Äî written verbatim (egress-validated). An empty fragment fails
  LOUDLY (a runtime-only verb misused in a build step). `spec.EmitReply` / `spec.BuildEnv` carry the wire.
- **Build-emit-capable validation** (`checkspec.go` `opActsInBuildDeploy` + `provider_verb.go` `BuildEmitter`): a
  build-context `plugin:` verb validates when it is `command` | `ProvisionActor` | `TypedStepProvider` | a builtin
  `BuildEmitter` | a connected external `grpcProvider` | a prescan-declared external verb. The parse-time prescan
  (`plugin_prescan.go`) stays deploy-substrate-only; external VERB words register POST-SCAN from the scanned candy
  map at `Validate` (`registerExternalVerbsFromCandies`) ‚Äî which includes `@github`-composed plugin candies fetched
  during the scan, so a submodule bed's `@github` plugin verb is recognized without building+connecting it.
- **Idempotent plugin loading** (`plugin_loader.go` `pluginAlreadyConnected` + `provider_registry.go`
  `registeredOrigin`): `loadProjectPlugins` runs on every connect path (build, deploy, check); a process that
  builds AND deploys connected the same plugin twice (e.g. `charly bundle add` ‚Üí `loadDeployPlugins` then the
  pod-overlay `NewGenerator` seam), warning on the second register. A same-SOURCE re-load is now an idempotent
  no-op (short-circuits the whole build+connect+schema-append+register); a DIFFERENT-origin collision still
  errors (the bijection backstop in `register` is unchanged).
- **R5 claim-keyed sweep**: corrected the stale "`charly box build` emits via `OCITarget`/the IR" claim ‚Äî build
  emits via `writeCandySteps` ‚Üí `emitTasks`; the IR/`OCITarget` path is deploy-only ‚Äî across 11 skills + 2 code
  comments (`build_target_oci.go`, `install_plan.go`).
- **Examples + bed**: `candy/plugin-example-step` (the build-emit verb) + `candy/examplestep-consumer` (its
  build-context `plugin: examplestep` run-step); the `box/fedora` `check-pod` bed composes both + asserts
  `/opt/examplestep-baked` is present.

R10: `charly check run check-pod` PASS (10/10 steps, zero warnings) on the LOCAL candy tree ‚Äî the external
plugin's `OpEmit` baked `RUN mkdir -p /opt && : > /opt/examplestep-baked` into the emitted Containerfile (grep-
verified) and executed at build; `examplestep-build-baked` PASS on BOTH the exploratory and fresh-rebuild passes.
Tests: `TestEmitPluginFragment_BuildTimeOpEmit`, `TestOpActsInBuildDeploy_PlacementAgnosticBuildEmit`,
`TestRegisterExternalVerbsFromCandies`, `TestPluginAlreadyConnected_Idempotent`; full `go test ./...` green.

### 2026-06-24 ‚Äî feat(charly): the external (out-of-process) deploy-target lifecycle works end-to-end over the E3b reverse channel

The deploy out-of-proc consumer completion (the EVERY-KIND-IS-A-PLUGIN program, k8s-consolidation path). An
external deploy-target plugin's FULL lifecycle ‚Äî Add / Test / Update / Del ‚Äî now works over the already-built
E3b `ExecutorService` reverse channel; previously only `Add` worked (`Del`/`Update` were silent no-ops and
`Test` errored "rides with the Phase-3 external deploy lifecycle" ‚Äî that stub is deleted, hard cutover).

- **Loader pre-load** (`plugin_prescan.go`): an external deploy provider's reserved word registers only AFTER
  `loadProjectPlugins` connects the plugin ‚Äî too late for a root-`charly.yml` bed that uses it as its SUBSTRATE
  discriminator, which the node-form parser must recognize at LOAD time. A lightweight, byte-gated,
  purely-additive declaration pre-scan (run at `loadUnifiedInto` depth-0) reads each discovered candy's
  `plugin: providers:` and registers the external DEPLOY words before normalization, so the four parse hooks
  (`classifyDisc`/`isResourceDisc`/`normalizeNodeInto`/`validateCheckBeds`) recognize them ‚Äî without breaking
  config-load repo-wide for the common no-external-substrate project.
- **Spec wire-types** (`spec/deploy_wire.go`, R3): `Scope`/`ReverseOpKind`/`ReverseOp` moved into `spec` (the SDK
  already imports it ‚Äî one shared type), plus the new `InstallPlanView` / `DeployVenue` / `DeployReply` the Add
  wire carries. `ReverseOpPluginScript` added (a generic recordable teardown op: `install_plan.go` +
  `reverse_ops.go`).
- **Lifecycle** (`deploy_target_external.go`): `Add` marshals the deploy's `[]*InstallPlan` + a venue descriptor
  into the Invoke envelope, runs the plugin over the reverse channel (the plugin heredocs its own files via
  `RunUser`/`RunSystem`), decodes a `{reverse_ops, record}` reply, and records it to the ledger keyed on
  `computeDeployID` (NOT `Target=="host"`, so it never collides with a real host deploy); `Del` replays the
  RECORDED reverse ops (never recomputes); `Test` runs host-side (`runUnifiedTargetChecks`); `Update` re-Invokes.
  `externalDeployTarget` is now a full `LifecycleTarget`.
- **`charly check live` dispatch** (`check_venue.go`): the shared host-venue classifier `checkLocalTarget` now
  routes an external out-of-process deploy (host-venue via `ShellExecutor`) to the host path for BOTH
  `charly check live` and `charly check <verb>` (R3) ‚Äî previously it fell through to the pod/container path and
  failed "container ‚Ä¶ is not running", which the bed's 30-min readiness poll surfaced as a hang (RCA).
- **SDK** (`plugin/sdk/deploy.go`): `DecodeInstallPlans` / `DecodeDeployVenue` / `PluginScriptReverseOp` /
  `BuildDeployReply` on the spec types. Example plugin (`candy/plugin-example-deploy`) + a `check-exampledeploy`
  disposable bed exercise the full lifecycle.

R10: the live `check-exampledeploy` disposable bed through a fresh `charly` build ‚Äî **PASS (4/4)**: deploy-add
(Add over the reverse channel writes the markers), check-live (`Local deploy ‚Ä¶ [host (local)]` ‚Äî the host-side
marker probe PASS, proving the dispatch fix), update (idempotent re-apply), cleanup (`bundle del` replays the
recorded plugin-script reverse op ‚Äî marker files removed, zero side-effect). `go test ./...` green (incl. the new
`TestReverseOpsPluginScript`, `plugin_prescan_test`, and the e2e extended to Add‚ÜíTest‚ÜíUpdate‚ÜíDel); `charly box
validate` exit 0 (loader pre-load did not regress config-load).

The EVERY-KIND-IS-A-PLUGIN program's E3 perf go/no-go ("the in-proc builtin fast path MUST stay
byte-identical / zero-alloc; the envelope is paid only out-of-process") was measured once during the C1‚ÄìC5
provider cutovers but never locked as a test. `charly/provider_bench_test.go` makes it a permanent CI gate:

- `TestPerfGate_BuiltinVerbsSkipEnvelope` ‚Äî every representative builtin verb (file/command/package/service)
  resolves to a `CheckVerbProvider`, so the dispatch fork (`provider_checkenv.go`) takes the typed `RunVerb`
  branch and NEVER reaches `invokeVerbProvider`'s `marshalJSON`. A builtin that stopped implementing the typed
  interface would silently pay the JSON envelope on every in-proc op ‚Äî this gate fails on exactly that.
- `TestPerfGate_TypedDispatchIsZeroAllocVsEnvelopeTax` ‚Äî `testing.AllocsPerRun` asserts the typed dispatch
  decision is **0 allocs** while the envelope's `marshalJSON` allocates (**6 allocs**), so the builtin's
  avoidance of the envelope is a genuine saving.
- `BenchmarkVerbTypedDispatchFork` (**0.98 ns/op, 0 allocs**) vs `BenchmarkVerbEnvelopeMarshal`
  (**1422 ns/op, 320 B, 6 allocs**) quantify the tax: the in-proc hot path is free; the wire envelope costs
  ~1.4¬µs/op, paid only out-of-process. **Go confirmed ‚Äî the maximal-out-of-tree placement is viable.**

Test-only change (test files do not enter the binary, so no bed exercises it); the gate is the full
`go test ./...` + `go test -bench`, all green.

A pointer-bump cutover integrating the portaudio cleanup the spice dep-shed surfaced. Now that opus/portaudio
left core (the SPICE audio cgo code moved to candy/plugin-spice, gated behind `-tags spice_audio`) and the core
charly is built cgo-free (`ldd` shows no libportaudio/libopus): `box/arch` drops the redundant `portaudio`/
`opusfile` from the arch VM cloud_init + the false "exits 127 without libportaudio" comment (R10'd on
check-arch-vm, 60/60); `pkg/arch` drops the two now-false `-tags spice_audio` PKGBUILD optdepends (+ syncs
.SRCINFO); the `/charly-check:libvirt` + `/charly-vm:arch` skills are swept to the cgo-free reality (R5
claim-keyed). No core `charly/` change ‚Äî this superproject commit bumps the box/arch + pkg/arch + plugins
submodule pointers.

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: Phase 4 dep-shed ‚Äî externalize the `spice` verb; DROP Shells-com/spice + opus + portaudio from core

The fourth dependency-shedding cutover. The `spice` SPICE-wire check verb leaves the core for the new
out-of-process plugin `candy/plugin-spice/`, so charly's core `go.mod` **drops `github.com/Shells-com/spice`
+ `github.com/hraban/opus` + `github.com/gordonklaus/portaudio`** (the SPICE wire client + its cgo audio
codec transitives). `spice:` authoring is unchanged ‚Äî the verb keeps its `spice:` discriminator +
`#SpiceMethod` enum + every modifier on the closed core `#Op` (it only leaves `#OpVerb`/`OpVerbs`/
`LiveVerbMethods`/`VerbCatalog`), dispatching via the registry ‚Üí `invokeVerbProvider` over gRPC.

- `candy/plugin-spice/` (new external module): `provider.go` + `methods.go` + `session.go` port spice.go +
  spice_session.go's 7 methods (status/screenshot/cursor/click/mouse/type/key); the vendored
  `third_party/spice` (SPICE wire stack) moved here via `git mv` (its `//go:build spice_audio`-gated
  ch-playback/ch-record keep opus/portaudio OFF by default, so the plugin ‚Äî like the old core ‚Äî builds
  cgo-free). `charly/spice.go`, `spice_session.go`, `plugin_verb_spice.go` DELETED.
- **The host pre-resolves the SPICE endpoint:** `charly/vm_target.go` stays in core (`ResolveVmTarget` +
  `SpiceEndpoint` use go-libvirt + libvirtxml, shared with the VM machinery). `charly/spice_preresolve.go`
  adds `preresolveSpiceEndpoint` (wired into `invokeVerbProvider`): resolves the bed's VM ‚Üí live SPICE
  endpoint host-side (opening the remote `qemu+ssh://` tunnel where needed), and passes the dialable
  address + password to the plugin via the env ‚Äî so the plugin needs no go-libvirt, only Shells-com/spice.
- **New enabler (R3, general): a deploy's `add_candy` plugins now load.** The project candy scan
  (`CollectRemoteRefs`) only walks image-closure refs, so an `add_candy` plugin candy (spice has no domain
  candy in the bed's image closure, unlike adb/kube) was never fetched/loaded. `ResolveOpts.ExtraCandyRefs`
  (config.go/refs.go ‚Äî additive, default-empty) routes the deploy's `add_candy` refs through the SAME
  collection primitive; `attachCheckRunnerContext` (the ONE shared check-runner plugin-load site) +
  `bundle_add_cmd.go` pass `deployAddCandyRefs(dir, name)` so a deploy loads ALL its composed plugins.
- No host `charly check spice` CLI ‚Äî declarative verb only (mirrors adb/kube/appium). Skills (spice / check /
  libvirt / arch / ssh) + README swept to the verb-only framing (R5 claim-keyed); the stale `check_cmd.go:60`
  comment + the go-skill source-map (listing spice/k8s as in-core sub-Cmds) corrected.
- **Composition (cross-repo):** `box/arch` check-arch-vm bed `add_candy`s `plugin-spice`; `box/cachyos`
  `cachyos-gpu-desktop-check` candy `require:`s it (in the GPU image closure) ‚Äî so both repos' `spice:`
  checks keep working (R2). The box `@github` pins for plugin-spice point at this cutover's tag.

R10: `go test ./...` + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` (exit 0) + `grep Shells-com/spice|opus|
portaudio charly/go.mod` = 0 + the live `check-arch-vm` bed (a disposable libvirt Arch cloud VM with a SPICE
socket; plugin-spice host-built + served out-of-process over go-plugin gRPC, loaded via the add_candy enabler;
the verb speaking the SPICE wire ‚Äî Main/Display/Inputs/Cursor channel enumeration ‚Äî to the live VM; `spice:
status` ‚Üí "SPICE: ok", `spice: screenshot` ‚Üí a real 1280x800 native-SPICE-decode PNG) through a fresh `charly
update`: **60 passed / 0 failed** on BOTH check-live and the fresh-rebuild check-live.

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: Phase 4 dep-shed ‚Äî externalize the `kube` verb + the k3s kubeconfig-merge + k8s status; DROP k8s.io/client-go + k8s.io/apimachinery from core

The third dependency-shedding cutover, and the largest client-go surface yet. The `kube` Kubernetes
cluster-probe verb, the k3s post-provision kubeconfig-merge, and the `charly status` k8s live-readiness probe
all leave the core for the new out-of-process plugin `candy/plugin-kube/`, so charly's core `go.mod` **drops
`k8s.io/client-go` + `k8s.io/apimachinery`** (and ~7 `k8s.io/*` / `sigs.k8s.io/*` transitives). `kube:`
authoring is unchanged ‚Äî the verb keeps its `kube:` discriminator + `#KubeMethod` + every modifier on the
closed core `#Op` (it only leaves `#OpVerb`/`OpVerbs`/`LiveVerbMethods`/`VerbCatalog`), dispatching via the
registry ‚Üí `invokeVerbProvider` over gRPC.

- `candy/plugin-kube/` (new external Go module): `provider.go` + `cluster.go` + `methods.go` port `k8s_cmd.go`'s
  13-method surface (nodes/wait-nodes/pods/wait-ready/ingress/ingressclass/storageclass/service/lb-external-ip/
  addons/apply/delete/raw) + the dynamic client; `merge.go` holds the kubeconfig merge. `charly/k8s_cmd.go`
  (944 lines) is DELETED.
- **Cluster pre-resolution stays in core (client-go-free):** `charly/k8s_config.go`'s `findK8sSpec` resolves a
  `cluster:` profile ‚Üí kubeconfig context HOST-side (`preresolveKubeCluster`, wired into `invokeVerbProvider`)
  before marshaling, so the plugin receives a concrete kubeconfig+context and needs no ClusterProfile knowledge.
- **The k3s kubeconfig-merge re-homed:** `charly/k8s_plugin.go` adds `invokeKubePlugin`; `k3s_post.go`'s
  `mergeKubeconfig` now calls the plugin's `merge-kubeconfig` method (an internal deploy seam, not in the
  `#KubeMethod` enum). `K3sPostProvision` runs inside `charly bundle add`, which loads the deploy's composed
  plugins ‚Äî so `candy/k3s-server` now `require:`s `plugin-kube`.
- **`charly status --nested` for kind:k8s deploys** now reports tree-state only (the client-go live-readiness
  probe in `status_collect_k8s.go` was dropped ‚Äî live k8s health is asserted via a `kube:` check instead).
- There is no host `charly check kube` CLI subcommand ‚Äî kube is a declarative check verb only (mirrors
  adb/appium). The `/charly-kubernetes:check-k8s`, `/charly-kubernetes:kubernetes`, k3s-server/k3s-agent,
  `/charly-check:check` skills, `CLAUDE.md`, `README.md`, and `candy/k8s-layer` were swept to the verb-only
  framing (R5 claim-keyed); the stale `LoadClusterProfile` reference (removed in schema v4) was corrected to
  `findK8sSpec`.
- **R1 ‚Äî two bugs caught by R10, fixed in-tree:** (1) the VM check path (`runVm`) never loaded external plugins
  (kube was a builtin before, so it never needed to), making a VM bed's `kube:` steps SKIP as `unknown verb` ‚Äî
  `runVm` now calls the shared `attachCheckRunnerContext` (the helper whose own contract says every RunModeLive
  baked-plan runner MUST call it, R3). (2) the bed's `kv-k8s-raw-version` check was DEGENERATE ‚Äî it set a
  `text:` the raw method ignored and passed only because the original `raw`'s `required:["Resource"]` was a
  latent *unenforced* check; the plugin correctly enforces it, so the check was rewritten to a meaningful
  `kube_resource: namespaces` test asserting `kube-system`.

R10: `go test ./...` + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` (exit 0) + `grep k8s.io|sigs.k8s
charly/go.mod` = 0 + the live `check-k3s-vm` bed (a disposable libvirt Arch VM + a real k3s control plane;
plugin-kube host-built + served out-of-process over go-plugin gRPC; the kubeconfig-merge via `invokeKubePlugin`
registering the cluster; all 13 kube methods probing the live cluster via `cluster: vm-k3s-vm`) through a fresh
`charly update`: **22 passed / 0 failed** on check-live against the freshly-built VM, the fresh-update rebuild

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: Phase 4 dep-shed ‚Äî externalize the `adb` verb + the android deploy/status seams; DROP github.com/zach-klippenstein/goadb from core

The second dependency-shedding cutover, and the FIRST with a deploy-target + status surface (unlike appium,
which was verb-isolated). The `adb` Android-Debug-Bridge verb ‚Äî AND the goadb-backed Android app-install /
device-probe operations the `target: android` deploy and the `charly status` collector previously did
in-core ‚Äî leave the core binary for the out-of-process plugin `candy/plugin-adb/`, so the core `go.mod`
**drops `github.com/zach-klippenstein/goadb`**. `adb:` authoring is unchanged: the verb keeps its `adb:`
discriminator + every modifier + `#AdbMethod` enum on the closed core `#Op` (it only leaves `#OpVerb`/
`OpVerbs`/`LiveVerbMethods`/`VerbCatalog`), so the registry resolves the registered external grpcProvider ‚Üí
`invokeVerbProvider` marshals the full `#Op` over gRPC and the plugin self-evaluates the matchers + artifact
validators via the shared `sdk` (R3 ‚Äî `charly/plugin/sdk/artifact.go`, also adopted by `plugin-appium`).

- `candy/plugin-adb/` (new external Go module): `sdk.Serve` + a Provider whose `Invoke` dispatches the 12
  adb methods (devices/shell/install/install-app/uninstall/getprop/screencap/logcat-tail/wait-for-device/
  wait-ui-settled/current-focus/keyevent) ‚Äî the goadb wire client + the apk-install path live ENTIRELY here.
- **The deploy/status re-homing (novel):** `charly/android_plugin.go` adds `invokeAdbPlugin` + `AdbDeviceEnv`
  ‚Äî the host resolves the device's adb-server addr host-side (engine inspect, no goadb) and ships it as a
  synthetic `#Op` + env to the SAME plugin. `android_install.go`'s `AndroidDevice` install methods +
  `android_deploy_cmd.go`'s `waitAndroidReady` are now thin wrappers over it; `status_collect_adb.go` derives
  device status from `containerRunning` (no goadb live probe ‚Äî the collector enumerates the android tree).
- **Every deploy loads its composed external plugins (R3):** `bundle_add_cmd.go` now runs the SAME candy
  scan + `loadProjectPlugins` the check runner uses, so a `target: android` deploy connects `plugin-adb`
  out-of-process before `invokeAdbPlugin` dispatches ‚Äî proven live on both the initial deploy and the fresh
  `charly update` rebuild.
- `charly/adb.go` (+ its tests) deleted; `findHostPort`/`adbAddrForContainer` (host-side, no goadb) relocated
  to `android_deploy_cmd.go`. There is no host `charly check adb` CLI subcommand ‚Äî adb is a declarative check
  verb only (mirrors appium). The `/charly-check:adb`, `/charly-check:appium`, `/charly-check:android` skills,
  `CLAUDE.md`, and `README.md` were swept to the verb-only framing (R5 claim-keyed ‚Äî the appium skill carried
  the same now-false "host CLI command" claim from the c01040e8 gap).
- **Binary hygiene:** `.gitignore` now ignores built plugin provider binaries (`candy/plugin-*/plugin-*`); the
  wrongly-tracked `candy/plugin-appium/plugin-appium` (28MB) was untracked.
- **Loading:** `candy/android-emulator-layer` requires `plugin-adb` (mirroring `plugin-appium`), so the bed's
  scanned candy set includes it. box/cachyos's `@github` pin lags (deliberate, B7 step 5) ‚Äî its standalone
  bed adopts the plugin via the superproject override at R10 and in the immediate-next version-adoption cutover.

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî refactor(charly): Phase 1 (live-container verbs) ‚Äî extract cdp + vnc (the dispatch-relocation pattern)

methods) + vnc (8) are the lowest-risk pair (TCP-only, stdlib) and prove the pattern.

`cdp:`/`vnc:` discriminator + their modifiers (Tab/URL/Expression/Selector/X/Y/Text/KeyName/Method) on the
closed base `#Op`, with NO `plugin_input` and NO served schema. So they take the schema-less
`registerDedicatedBuiltin` path (the same mechanism the deploy/step/builder providers + deploy-shape kinds
use) ‚Äî the FIRST live-container verbs to do so. It's a pure DISPATCH RELOCATION, not a schema change.

  ‚Äî R3). Removed cdp/vnc from `builtinProviderInstances` + the `charly.yml` manifest verb list.
- **Code-only ‚Äî NO schema bump** (`task cue:gen` zero diff; HEAD stays `2026.174.1100`, superproject-only).
