### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî refactor(charly): Phase 2 deploy-shape ‚Äî extract group/pod/vm/k8s/local/android into dedicated KindProviders

The hardest heavy-kind batch: the 6 deploy-shape kinds leave the core `kind_builtins.go` (which now hosts
ONLY `candy`) for dedicated builtin `KindProvider`s. **Design resolved by the code (RDD-proved on `group`
first):** unlike the tier-1 leaf kinds (distro/builder/‚Ä¶), these CANNOT use the JSON Invoke envelope ‚Äî
they recurse over the `genericNode` member tree (pod members, vm‚Üík8s nesting, resource siblings) and land
in the TYPED core maps (`uf.Bundle`/`uf.Pod`/`uf.VM`/`uf.K8s`/`uf.Local`/`uf.Android`) every deploy/check
consumer reads, neither of which survives serialization. So they stay **in-proc `KindProvider`s with typed
`DecodeNode`**, registered via `registerDedicatedBuiltin`, and the recursion helpers (`buildBundleNodeInto`,
`buildStandaloneResource`, `buildBundleNode`, `resourceChildren`) **stay in CORE** (byte-identical, only
relocated). External out-of-proc is correctly deferred to the ExecutorService enabler ‚Äî placement stays a
build choice.

- `plugin_group.go` (groupKind) + `plugin_substrate.go` (the parameterized `standaloneKind{word,def}` +
  `isDeployShape`, with 5 thin `registerDedicatedBuiltin` registrations for pod/vm/k8s/local/android).
  Removed group/standalone/isDeployShape from `kind_builtins.go`, the 6 from `builtinProviderInstances`,
  and the 6 words from the `charly.yml` `providers:` manifest (now `kind: [candy]`).
- **Code-only ‚Äî NO schema bump** (the authored keywords + core `#Pod`/`#Vm`/‚Ä¶ defs are unchanged; HEAD
  stays `2026.174.1100`, no box re-stamp ‚Äî superproject-only). `checkKindProviderBijection` still proves
  each is registered.

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. the recursion/nesting gates ‚Äî `TestBuildBundleNode_Structure`, `TestOverlay
RoundTrip_GroupMembersSurvive`, `TestDeployNestedPodsInGuest_*`, `TestNestedExecutor_ThreeLevelNesting`,
`TestAndroid*`, `TestVm/PodUnifiedTarget` ‚Äî + bijection/corpus) + `task build:charly` + `charly box
validate` exit 0 (root + box/fedora/cachyos/arch) + `charly box generate` (gen=0) + the multi-bed gate:
check-pod (pod), check-cross-pod-cdp (group), check-local (local), check-k3s-vm (vm + vm‚Üík8s nesting),
check-android-emulator-pod (android + pod‚Üíandroid nesting).

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî refactor(charly): Phase 2 tier-1 ‚Äî extract distro/builder/init/resource/target into KindProvider plugins

The first heavy-kind batch: the 5 build-vocabulary / cross-ref kinds leave the core `kind_builtins.go`
typed `DecodeNode` for dedicated `KindProvider` plugin units, mirroring the clean-tier precedent
(agent/module/sidecar/package-group). **Code-only ‚Äî NO schema bump:** extracting a kind leaves the
authored keyword (`distro:`/`builder:`/‚Ä¶) unchanged (the plugin decodes it), so it's a CUE-internal vocab
change (`#Node` arms / `KindWords`), not an authored wire-key change ‚Äî no `MigrationStep`, HEAD stays
`2026.174.1100`, no box re-stamp (this is a superproject-only cutover).

- Per kind: `charly/plugin/builtins/<kind>/` (self-contained `#<Kind>Input` + plugin.go + params) +
  `plugin_<kind>.go` (`KindProvider`, Invoke‚ÜíOpLoad ‚Üí decode into the core `spec.<Kind>` ‚Üí land in
  `uf.PluginKinds["<kind>"]`). The core `#<Kind>` defs stay in `schema/` (still generate the `spec.<Kind>`
  consumer types ‚Äî zero consumer-type churn). Removed the 5 typed `*Kind` structs, the 5 `cue_kind_*.go`
  registrations, the `UnifiedFile.{Distro,Builder,Init,Resource,Target}` fields, the 5 `mergeXMap`
  funcs (subsumed by `mergePluginKindsMap`), and the manifest entries.
- Consumer rerouting (the real work): `Distros()`/`Builders()`/`Inits()`/`Resources()` accessors (a shared
  `decodePluginKindMap[T]` over `uf.PluginKinds`) replace every typed-field reader ‚Äî the generator's
  `Project{Distro,Builder,Init}Config`, preempt/vm GPU arbitration, the migrate default-vocab compare.
  `target` has zero core readers (Calamares importers deferred) ‚Üí no accessor (dead code, R5); its body
  rests in `PluginKinds["target"]`.
- **RCA fix (R1):** `distro` is BOTH a plugin kind AND a candy package-surface data key; `classifyDisc`
  checked `dataKeySet` before the plugin `ResolveKind`, mis-classing a top-level `distro:` node as `"data"`
  (dropping the non-deployable-kind child gate). Fixed: a registered plugin KIND now wins over a homonymous
  data key for a TOP-LEVEL node (the `asChild` data-sense path unchanged); only `distro` collides.

R10: `go test ./...` (charly + spec + the reserved-word bijection gates + CUE corpus/closedness) + `task
build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 (root + box/fedora) + `charly box generate` (gen=0, proving
the box build reads distro/builder/init vocab through the new accessors) + check-pod.

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: extract the `file` verb ‚Äî the LAST verb leaves `#Op` + schema HEAD ‚Üí 2026.174.1100

The final verb extraction ‚Äî **every check/state-provision verb is now a plugin** (`#OpVerb` is empty of
the legacy probe/act verbs). `file` is a shell-act state-provision verb (RDD corrected an initial
mis-scoping as pure-check): `fileVerb.RenderProvisionScript` is a RUNTIME file-creation act (touch+chmod),
distinct from the BUILD-time COPY of `write:`/`copy:`, so it's preserved ‚Äî `fileVerb` implements
`CheckVerbProvider` (RunVerb ‚Üí runFile) AND `ProvisionActor`, mirroring unix_group/user/mount/kernel-param.

- **Shared-field discipline:** `mode` is read by copy/write at deploy (`deploy_target_{local,vm}.go`), so
  it STAYS on `#Op` and is reproduced in `#FileInput` (the gid-between-unix_group-and-user pattern). Only
  the 7 file-exclusive fields (`file`/`exists`/`owner`/`group_of`/`filetype`/`contains`/`sha256`) leave `#Op`.
- **Third silent-regression caught (R5):** `contains` carries a bare-scalar **contains-default** (6 live
  candies rely on it ‚Äî qemu-guest-agent, docker-ce, waybar-labwc, ‚Ä¶); the generic `decodeMatcherList`
  (equals-default) would have silently flipped them to exact-equality. Added a dedicated `decodeContainsList`
  codec to preserve the semantic, and ‚Äî `file` being its last user ‚Äî fully removed the orphaned base
  `#ContainsList`/`ContainsList`/`expandContainsListNode` (CUE def, spec type, normalizer, tests + the stale
  refs in the `matching` plugin schema). `git grep '#ContainsList'` over `charly/` is clean.

The state-provision MigrationStep extended with file (check: AND run:); `calver-schema` + `LatestSchema
Version` `2026.174.0900` ‚Üí `2026.174.1100`; cascaded across all 6 repos (B7); 181 main candies migrated.
(No @github version-adoption needed; all 5 boxes' standalone validate stayed exit 0.)

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. `TestRunner_FileVerb` + its bare-scalar-contains subtest, `TestDecodeContains
List`, the migrator check+run file cases, `TestEmitTasks_PluginAct_File` proving the migrated `plugin:
file` renders with zero "unknown verb" via the REAL box-build emit path, `TestCollectDescriptions_Bakes
PluginFileCheck`) + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 (root + all 5 boxes standalone) +
check-pod, whose check-live runs the migrated `plugin: file` checks.

per-verb skip-filter ‚Äî so it STAYS on `#Op`. `resolvePackageName` (the distro-aware name resolver) stays
shared. The dead `case StepKindSystemPackages` in compileActOp (read the removed `Op.Package`) is deleted.

**R5 completion the extraction enables:** `package`/`service` were the ONLY `VerbSpec.LowersTo` users, and
service's lowering already moved into its provider ‚Äî so `LowersTo` is now fully dead. Removed the struct
field, the 4th positional on every `VerbCatalog` entry, and simplified `ActsInBuildDeploy` to
`installVerbs[verb]`. Removed `package` from `#Op`/`VerbCatalog`/`spec.OpVerbs`/`builtinProviderInstances`/
the manifest.

`2026.174.0700` ‚Üí `2026.174.0900`; cascaded across all 6 repos (B7); 84 main candies migrated. (No @github

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: TypedStepProvider enabler + extract the `service` verb + schema HEAD ‚Üí 2026.174.0700

provider and ‚Äî if it's a `TypedStepProvider` ‚Äî `return`s `ConstructStep(...)` (the typed step, whose

only for pure-check / RenderProvisionScript plugins (command/etc.). The dead `case StepKindService
Packaged` in compileActOp (which read the now-removed `Op.Service`) is deleted (R5).

**service extracted:** `serviceVerb` implements ALL THREE ‚Äî `CheckVerbProvider` (RunVerb ‚Üí `runService`),
`TypedStepProvider` (LowersTo + ConstructStep ‚Üí `ServicePackagedStep`), and `ProvisionActor`
(RenderProvisionScript, the runtime/opt-in live-act path). **RDD correction:** `running`/`enabled` had
ZERO remaining `#Op` readers after extraction (process reads its OWN `plugin_input.running`), so all of
`service`/`running`/`enabled` moved into `#ServiceInput` and left `#Op` ‚Äî and the stale "running STAYS
in #Op" claim in `process.cue` was swept (R1 doc-divergence). Removed `service` from `#Op`/`VerbCatalog`
(its `LowersTo` now lives in the provider)/`spec.OpVerbs`/`builtinProviderInstances`/the manifest.

The state-provision MigrationStep extended with service (check: AND run:); `calver-schema` + `Latest

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: extract the `command` verb into a plugin unit (the install-task act seam) + schema HEAD ‚Üí 2026.174.0500

The hardest state-provision-tier verb. `command` is dual-natured but UNLIKE the RenderProvisionScript
verbs: its run-act is the full `emitCmd` path (the `bash <<'OVCMD'` heredoc, cache mounts, from_host
bind-mounts, BUILD_ARCH) ‚Äî un-expressible as a provision-script string. So it's install-task-like, not
state-provision-like.

- **Check side:** `commandVerb` is a CheckVerbProvider (`plugin_verb_command.go` ‚Äî named to avoid the
  CLI `plugin_command_*.go` files); RunVerb decodes `plugin_input` ‚Üí `params.CommandInput`, reads the
  matchers from the step Op.
- **Act side (Option A):** `emitTasks` (`case "plugin"`) + `renderOpCommand` get a localized `if t.Plugin
  == "command"` branch that rehydrates `Op{Command,‚Ä¶}` from `plugin_input` and falls into the existing
  `emitCmd` ‚Äî ONE shared command emitter, no duplication.
- **RDD correction:** `command` is a SHARED `#Op` modifier ‚Äî `wl`/`libvirt` read `Op.Command` as their
  argv ‚Äî so `command` STAYS in `#Op`, leaving only the `#OpVerb` union. Only `background`/`from_host`/
  `in_container` are command-exclusive (‚Üí `#CommandInput`); the matchers `stdout`/`stderr`/`exit_status`
  stay shared in `#Op`. The MigrationStep field-SPLITS accordingly (exclusive fields ‚Üí plugin_input,
  matchers stay at step level), gated by `stepHasCharlyVerb` so a `wl`/`libvirt`+command step is not
  converted.

**Validation restoration (R2, surfaced + fixed):** `collectCheckRefs` now scans `plugin_input` ‚Äî
RESTORING the `${VAR}`-in-build-scope check that the earlier http extraction silently dropped when
fields moved off `#Op`. It surfaced 4 pre-existing latent bugs (build-scope steps referencing the
runtime `${HOST_PORT}`): `candy/testapi` steps 4/5 and `candy/{kde-selkies,selkies-kde-desktop}` ‚Äî all
fixed by adding `context: [runtime]`.

`calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion` `2026.174.0300` ‚Üí `2026.174.0500`; cascaded across all 6 repos
(B7); 144 main candies + the box candies migrated.

**Cross-repo note (B7 step 5):** box/cachyos + box/fedora pin the selkies/testapi candies via `@github`
at `v2026.170.1105` (a deliberate lag). The restored check correctly flags the scope bug in those
FROZEN pinned copies ‚Äî fixed at the producer's (main) HEAD here; the consumers' standalone validate
clears when those pins adopt the fix in the immediate-next version-adoption cutover. The cutover's R10
(check-pod, assembled with the local-main override) and the boxes' assembled-context validate both pass.

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. `TestEmitTasks_PluginAct‚Ä¶` + the command field-split migrator test) + `task
build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 (root + the assembled box context) + check-pod ‚Äî whose
composed candies exercise migrated `plugin: command` check AND run-act steps, the act emitting a real
`RUN` block (verified: `unknown verb "command"`/`"plugin"` count = 0 in the generated Containerfile).

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: extract 3 shared-path state-provision verbs (user/mount/kernel-param) + schema HEAD ‚Üí 2026.174.0300

The state-provision batch on the proven act-emit enabler: `user`, `mount`, `kernel-param` each leave
the closed `#Op` into dedicated builtin plugin units that are BOTH a `CheckVerbProvider` (RunVerb ‚Üí
`runUser`/`runMount`/`runKernelParam`) AND a `ProvisionActor` (RenderProvisionScript). Each verb's
fields move into its `#<Verb>Input`:

- **user** owns `user`/`uid`/`gid`/`home`/`shell` ‚Äî and a confirmed handoff: `gid`/`uid` were held in
  `#Op` only because `runUser` read them; now that `user` leaves, NO other `#Op` verb reads them, so
  they're removed from `#Op` (unix_group's `#UnixGroupInput` already reproduces `gid` standalone).
- **mount** owns `mount`/`mount_source`/`filesystem`/`opt` (`opt` a `MatcherList`).
- **kernel-param** ‚Äî kept the hyphenated wire word (a clean EXTRACTION, not a rename; the Go package
  dir is `kernel_param` only because hyphens are illegal in Go identifiers).

**R10-caught fix (R2/R4):** the `kernel-param` CHECK shelled to `sysctl`, absent in the minimal check-pod
image (exit 127). Hardened `runKernelParam` to read `/proc/sys/<dotted-key-as-slash-path>` directly via
`cat` inside the target (kernel params are netns-scoped ‚Äî the target's `/proc/sys` is the source of
truth) ‚Äî `sysctl -n k` ‚â° `/proc/sys/k`, so the value is identical with ZERO external dependency. The
`run:` ACT keeps `sysctl -w` (a deploy/runtime context). The value `MatcherList` is preserved.

**Surfaced + flagged (R2, separable ‚Üí its own follow-up):** the `groups` field in `#Op` is now DEAD
(no runtime reader ‚Äî orphaned by the unix_group cutover whose `#UnixGroupInput` reproduced only
`unix_group`+`gid`). Left in `#Op`, annotated, for an immediate-next cleanup cutover.

The MigrationStep `state-provision-verbs-to-plugin` extended with the 3 verbs (BOTH check: AND run:).
`calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion` `2026.174.0100` ‚Üí `2026.174.0300`; cascaded across all 6 repos
(B7).

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. per-verb emit-path tests + `TestRunner_KernelParam` reading `/proc/sys` +
the migration test) + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 across all 6 repos (every
root at `2026.174.0300`) + check-pod ‚Äî `check-user-present` (root via getent), `check-mount-present`

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: act-emit enabler for state-provision verbs + extract unix_group + schema HEAD ‚Üí 2026.174.0100

Opens the STATE-PROVISION verb tier (verbs that are BOTH a check-probe AND a run-act that lowers to an
install-plan step). The enabler is the act-side analogue of the runPluginVerb check enabler.

**The act-emit enabler (the missing half):** a state-provision verb's runtime act (`ProvisionActor.
RenderProvisionScript`) was already plugin-ready, but the install-plan EMIT paths
(`compileActOp`/`renderOpCommand`/`emitTasks`) switched on `Op.File`/`Op.Command`/‚Ä¶ with no Plugin
case ‚Äî so a `run: {plugin: <verb>}` step would break ("task has no supported verb"). Added ONE shared
helper `resolveProvisionScript(op, distros)` that resolves `op.Plugin` ‚Üí type-asserts `ProvisionActor`
‚Üí calls `RenderProvisionScript`, wired into all THREE emit sites: the box/OCI build's candy-walk
emitter `emitTasks` (the path `charly box generate`‚Üí`writeCandySteps` actually uses), the local/vm
deploy `renderOpCommand`, and the runtime `runProvisionAct` (which would also have broken, R2). `OpStep`
gained a `Distros` field for the context. A non-`ProvisionActor` plugin in a `run:` step errors loudly
(R4). This one seam serves all 6 shared-path state-provision verbs. (R10 caught a first attempt that
wired the OCI seam into `OCITarget.emitOp` ‚Äî used only for pod-overlay rendering, NOT the base image
build ‚Äî which a unit test masked but the check-pod bed exposed as `# unknown verb "plugin" ‚Äî skipping`;
the fix moved the single seam into `emitTasks`, the emitter both the box build AND the pod overlay
share, and deleted the divergent `emitOp` pre-conversion, R5.)

**unix_group extracted** (the cleanest first ‚Äî build-safe `groupadd`, no reversals): its `unixGroup
Verb` is registered as a plugin unit that is BOTH a `CheckVerbProvider` (RunVerb ‚Üí `runUnixGroup`) AND
a `ProvisionActor` (RenderProvisionScript ‚Üí groupadd). **Key catch:** `gid` is SHARED (`runUser` reads
`Op.GID`), so `gid` stays in `#Op`; `#UnixGroupInput` reproduces it standalone. Removed the
`unix_group` discriminator from `#Op`/`VerbCatalog`/`spec.OpVerbs`/`builtinProviderInstances`/the
manifest.

A dedicated MigrationStep `state-provision-verbs-to-plugin` (@ `2026.174.0050`) converts BOTH a
`check:` AND a `run:` step's `unix_group:` ‚Üí `plugin: unix_group` (the goss migrator only handled
`check:` ‚Äî wrong for a dual-natured verb). `calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion` `2026.173.2300` ‚Üí
`2026.174.0100`; cascaded across all 6 repos (B7).

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. `TestRenderOpCommand_PluginAct_UnixGroup` (local/vm), `TestEmitOp_Plugin
Act_UnixGroup_OCI` (build), `‚Ä¶NotActCapable` (the loud error), + the migration test) + `task build:
charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 across all 6 repos (every root at `2026.174.0100`) + check-pod ‚Äî
whose composed `check-stack-layer` candy emits the `run: plugin: unix_group` **groupadd at image
build** (the act-emit enabler end-to-end), then the `check: plugin: unix_group` step verifies the group
exists at runtime. 5 submodule pointers bumped.

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: externalize the observe verbs http/interface/addr into plugin units + schema HEAD ‚Üí 2026.173.2300

Observe-verb wave 2 (after process/port/dns): `http`, `interface`, `addr` leave the closed `#Op`/
`spec.OpVerbs` into dedicated builtin plugin units (`plugin: <verb>` + `plugin_input`), reusing their
existing `runHTTP`/`runInterface`/`runAddr` impls. `http`'s `body`/`header` matchers ride the shared
`MatcherList` JSON codec (R3), the matching pattern.

**RDD refinements:** (1) `method`/`request_body` (shared with cdp/dbus/libvirt) + `timeout` (a general
per-step modifier read by `probeNeverHang`) STAY in `#Op` ‚Äî only http-exclusive fields leave. (2) R5
orphan cleanup: once `interface`/`addr` leave, `addrs` (dns already extracted) and `reachable` (port
already extracted) have no remaining `#Op` consumer ‚Äî both removed from `#Op`.

**R2/R3 latent-bug fix (surfaced + fixed in-scope):** `opExpandVars`/`collectHostRefs` only walked
`#Op` `StringFields`, so `${HOST_PORT:N}`/`${VAR}`/`${HOST:member}` inside a migrated step's
`plugin_input` was never expanded ‚Äî a latent break for the already-landed process/port/dns too (all 32
corpus `addr` uses are `127.0.0.1:${HOST_PORT:N}`). Added generic `plugin_input` walks
(`expandAnyVars`/`collectAnyStrings`) ‚Äî fixes http/addr AND retroactively repairs process/port/dns.
Also rewired `k8s_generate.checkToProbe` + the result-subject label to read the discriminator from
`plugin_input` via a generic `pluginInputStr` helper (else K8s httpGet/tcpSocket probes + report
subjects vanished for migrated steps).

**`command` recategorized (RDD, NOT scope-narrowing):** `command` is dual-natured ‚Äî `check: command:`
is a probe BUT `run: command:` lowers via `compileActOp` to a generic `OpStep` emitted as a
Containerfile `RUN` (`emitCmd`), so removing `Op.Command` from `#Op` breaks the build exactly like
package/service. It is a STATE-PROVISION verb (420 corpus uses, ~97 act steps) ‚Äî extracted later with
file/package/service via the check-verb + step-provider composition, not here.

One generalized MigrationStep `goss-verbs-to-plugin` (extended `gossVerbFields` with http/interface/
addr); `calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion` `2026.173.1742` ‚Üí `2026.173.2300`; cascaded across all

### 2026-06-23 ‚Äî feat(charly): externalize the `sidecar` kind into a plugin unit (Phase 2 ‚Äî Cutover B2; clean-tier kinds complete)

The last clean-tier kind, and the payoff for the name-keyed override enabler. `sidecar` leaves the

(`runPluginKind` ‚Üí `#SidecarInput`) on every `LoadUnified`. The explicit `mergeSidecarMap` in

complex tailscale (cap_add + env + volume + secret) round-trips end-to-end through `#SidecarInput`.

`#Sidecar` stays in `schema/` for the canonical `spec.Sidecar`/`SidecarDef` (`cue_types_gen.go`
byte-identical ‚Äî zero deploy-consumer type churn). Removed `sidecarKind`/`cue_kind_sidecar.go`/`uf.
Sidecar`/`mergeSidecarMap` + from `#Node`/`_reservedNode`/`builtinProviderInstances`/the `kind:`
manifest; `vocab_gen.go` drops `sidecar` from `KindWords`. **The clean-tier kinds (package-group,
module, agent, sidecar) are now all externalized.**

**MAIN-ONLY**: authoring (`sidecar:`) unchanged ‚Äî no `#Node` version bump, no MigrationStep, no
cascade. `charly box validate` exit 0 at root AND box/fedora (both parse the embedded tailscale

### 2026-06-22 ‚Äî feat(charly): generalize the plugin-kind mechanism ‚Äî name-keyed storage + root-wins override (kind enabler)

The foundational enabler for externalizing name-keyed, overridable kinds (RDD-surfaced when scoping
the agent/sidecar extraction: the shared `uf.PluginKinds` was a NAMELESS append-list ‚Äî fine for
package-group, whose `uf.Group` had zero readers, but agent's iterate catalog and sidecar's
overridable embedded `tailscale` are name-keyed, root-wins consumers the append-list silently breaks).

- **Name threading:** the node name (the node key) is threaded into the STORAGE KEY in `runPlugin
  Kind`, NOT into the validated body ‚Äî `assembleEntityBody` is untouched, so the body stays nameless
  and `#<Kind>Input` + the self-contained-schema property are unchanged. (No `Operation`/proto field
  added ‚Äî that would be a wire cascade + dead data; the host has `gn.name` locally at the store site.)
- **Name-keyed storage:** `UnifiedFile.PluginKinds` `map[string][]json.RawMessage` ‚Üí
  `map[string]map[string]json.RawMessage` (kind ‚Üí name ‚Üí body), mirroring the `uf.Agent`/`uf.Sidecar`
  shape the consumers need.
- **Root-wins override merge:** `mergePluginKindsMap` rewritten from append ‚Üí name-keyed override,
  byte-identical to `mergeSidecarMap`/`mergeAgentMap` (per kind, an existing root/project entry for a
  name is preserved; the embedded/import source fills only absent names) ‚Äî this is what lets a
  project's `tailscale` sidecar override the embedded one once sidecar externalizes (Cutover B).

package-group's plugin needed no change (it decodes the nameless body); its tests + the external
`e3kind` test updated to the name-keyed form. The override is dormant until a name-keyed kind extracts
(Cutover B: agent/module/sidecar).

**MAIN-ONLY**: the name is the node KEY (not authored) ‚Äî no schema/`#<Kind>Input` change, no `#Node`
change, no MigrationStep, no version bump, no cascade (zero codegen drift; `charly box validate` exit
0 at the unchanged schema version).

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. the new `TestMergePluginKindsMap_NameKeyedOverride` + `TestLoadUnified_
PluginKindNameOverride` ‚Äî two docs, same name ‚Üí root wins ‚Äî plus the updated package-group/e3kind
tests) + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 + check-pod (loader/merge no-regression ‚Äî
`mergePluginKindsMap` runs on every load).

### 2026-06-22 ‚Äî feat(charly): externalize the 15-command deploy-lifecycle group into CommandProviders

The deploy-lifecycle command bulk: `start, stop, status, restart, update, remove, logs, shell, cmd,
cp, volume, service, config, bundle, reap-orphans` leave the hardcoded `var cli struct{‚Ä¶}` in
`main.go` and become dedicated `<name>Command` CommandProviders (`plugin_command_<name>.go`), each
`KongCommand()` returning the existing `<Name>Cmd` Kong struct verbatim. **The key insight: the Run
handlers ‚Äî and the core deploy/bundle machinery they call (LoadBundleConfig, the deploy targets) ‚Äî
are untouched; only the CLI registration location moves off the struct, so "coupling in the Run
handler" is not a blocker.** They self-register via `registerDedicatedBuiltin` and arrive through
`cli.Plugins`; the MCP surface auto-picks them up.

**Coupling audit (per-command `cli.<Field>` grep):** the ONLY command field read outside Kong
dispatch is `cli.Check.Plugins` (nested-command plugins) ‚Äî so `check`, `feature`, `vm` are deferred
(large harness/domain commands; `check` has the real `cli.Check.Plugins` coupling). All 15
deploy-lifecycle commands are clean leaf moves. `reap-orphans` uses the safe filename
`plugin_command_reap_orphans.go` (underscore) with `Reserved()` returning the hyphenated CLI word.
Machinery (box/candy/clean/doctor/migrate/settings/version/__plugin) stays hardcoded.

**MAIN-ONLY**: zero codegen drift, no schema change, no version bump. GOOS-trap check: all 22
`plugin_command_*.go` compile into the linux build.

`udev.install`/`udev.remove`) from the MCP tools. Fixed by wiring `collectCommandPlugins()` into both
`mcp_server.go` `kong.New` sites (model build + tool-run parser) + the `buildTestKong` helper ‚Äî so a
plugin command's tools survive in the MCP surface identically to a hardcoded one.

### 2026-06-22 ‚Äî feat(charly): extract 3 schema-less IR providers (deploy-target/builder/step) into dedicated plugin files (Phase 3 pattern proof)

Proves the IR-provider ‚Üí dedicated-plugin pattern with the cleanest candidate of each of the three
schema-less provider categories: `localTarget` (deploy:local), `cargoBuilder` (builder:cargo),
`rebootStepProvider` (step:Reboot). Each moves out of the shared `builtinProviderInstances` slice +
the `charly.yml` providers manifest into its OWN dedicated file (`plugin_deploy_local.go` /
`plugin_builder_cargo.go` / `plugin_step_reboot.go`) ‚Äî the externalizable property ‚Äî while dispatch
stays IDENTICAL through `providerRegistry.Resolve{Deploy,Step,Builder}` (pure registration-location
refactor, zero behavior change).

**RDD finding (the mechanism):** unlike verb/kind plugin units, IR providers carry NO authored input
‚Üí NO schema, so a schema-less `RegisterBuiltinPluginUnit` is correctly REJECTED (`registerPluginUnit
Schema` hard-rejects an empty `CueSource` ‚Äî that path is exclusively for schema-carrying authored
plugins). The dedicated mechanism: each provider self-registers via a package-var initializer
(`var _ = registerDedicatedBuiltin(localTarget{})`) which runs BEFORE any `init()`, so the bootstrap
bijection gates observe it without the file-name ordering race the shared-slice init deliberately
avoids ‚Äî strictly more robust than an `init()`. This is the template for the Phase-3 bulk (the other
4 deploy targets, 11 steps, 3 builders).

**MAIN-ONLY** (no schema/corpus/cascade): no `schema/*.cue` edit, no `#Node`/`#Op` change, zero
codegen drift, no version bump. The per-class bijection gates (`checkDeployProviderBijection`,
`checkStepProviderBijection`) + `TestProviderManifest_EnforcedBijection` stay green (3 removed from
both manifest and slice).

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. the new `TestDedicatedProviders_ResolveAndDispatch` asserting each
resolves + dispatches + is absent from the shared slice/manifest, + the bijection gates that panic
the suite on a registration-ordering regression) + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0
+ check-pod (registry-init + build-pipeline no-regression on the fresh binary).

### 2026-06-22 ‚Äî feat(charly): extract the `package-group` KIND into a plugin unit (first Phase-2 kind extraction) + fix the kind‚Üíplugin loader scaffolding

The FIRST kind extraction, proving the kind‚Üíplugin pattern end-to-end through the real loader. The
zero-corpus `package-group` kind leaves the closed core into a dedicated builtin plugin unit
(`charly/plugin/builtins/package-group/` + `plugin_package_group.go`): its `#Group` schema moves
into the plugin's self-contained `#PackageGroupInput` .cue, and dispatch changes from the typed
`KindProvider.DecodeNode` to the generic plugin path (`normalizeNodeInto` ‚Üí `runPluginKind` ‚Üí
`Invoke(OpLoad)`, validated against the served schema, stored in `uf.PluginKinds["package-group"]`).
The authored form is UNCHANGED (`kind:` stays `kind:`) ‚Äî kind extraction, unlike verb extraction,
needs no MigrationStep authoring rewrite.

**Zero-corpus ‚Üí in-place, MAIN-ONLY, no version bump, no 6-repo cascade** (the EDGE-INHERIT cutover-C
precedent): no file authors `package-group:`, so the new schema accepts the whole corpus at the
unchanged `version: 2026.173.1742` ‚Äî `charly box validate` exit 0 confirms it.

**Two loader-scaffolding bugs found via RDD + fixed in-scope (R1/R2):** (1) `mergeUnified` never
merged `PluginKinds`, so EVERY plugin-kind entity (incl. the existing external `e3kind` path) was
silently dropped on every load ‚Äî added `mergePluginKindsMap` (append-merge). (2) `loadBuiltinPlugin
Units()` ran only on the check/deploy paths, not `LoadUnified`, so `runPluginKind`'s load-time schema
validation would fail "schema not loaded" ‚Äî added an idempotent gate in `runPluginKind`. Both were
masked because the E3 kind-plugin scaffolding had only ever been tested by calling `normalizeNodeInto`
directly, bypassing the real loader.

**R5:** `uf.Group` had NO downstream reader (decoded + merged, never consumed ‚Äî no Calamares generator
exists yet); removed `uf.Group`, `mergeGroupMap`, and the dead `GroupSpec` aliases. `spec.Group` stays
as the canonical entity type the plugin decodes into.

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. the new `plugin_package_group_test.go` driving a `package-group:` doc
through `LoadUnified` into `uf.PluginKinds` + the load-time schema-gate rejection test) + `task
build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 + check-pod (loader no-regression on the fresh binary).

### 2026-06-22 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: extract the observe-only goss verbs (process/port/dns) into plugin units + schema HEAD ‚Üí 2026.173.1742

The first BATCH of execution-needing goss verbs extracted into dedicated builtin plugin units
(via the runPluginVerb executor enabler ‚Äî each keeps its live `*Runner`): **process, port,
dns**. Each leaves the closed `#Op`/`spec.OpVerbs`, becomes `plugin: <verb>` + `plugin_input`,
and reuses its existing `runX` impl (RunVerb decodes plugin_input ‚Üí the typed `params.<Verb>
Input` ‚Üí `runProcess`/`runPort`/`runDNS`). Shared fields stay in `#Op`, referenced standalone
in the plugin schemas (`reachable` port‚Üîaddr, `addrs` dns‚Üîinterface). Added the R3 shared
`decodePluginInput` helper.

One generalized MigrationStep `goss-verbs-to-plugin` (@ `2026.173.1741`, replacing the
single-verb `process-to-plugin`) drives a `gossVerbFields` set: a `check:` step carrying
`process:`/`port:`/`dns:` ‚Üí `plugin: <verb>` + `plugin_input` (isStepNode-gated, so a box's
published `port:` and a candy's install `package:`/`service:` lists are NEVER touched;
idempotent). `calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion` `2026.173.1616` ‚Üí `2026.173.1742`;
re-stamped + cascaded across all 6 repos (B7).

**Architectural finding (R1, RDD-surfaced):** the state-provision goss verbs
(file/package/service/user/unix_group/kernel_param/mount) are NOT extractable into the
check-only `CheckVerbProvider` plugin model ‚Äî they additionally carry a `RenderProvisionScript`
act form AND lower to install-plan steps (the package-install/service-enable timeline baked
into Containerfiles + every deploy). The plugin model has no act/install-lowering half, so
extracting them would silently drop `run: package:`/`run: service:` provisioning (a masked
regression). They stay base `#Op` verbs pending a plugin-model decision. The remaining
observe-only goss verbs (command/http/interface/addr) are batch-2.

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. `TestMigrateGossVerbsToPlugin` + converted `TestRunner_{Port,DNS,
Process}Plugin` + the bijection/schema-splice gates) + `task build:charly` + `charly box
validate` exit 0 across all 6 repos (every root at `2026.173.1742`) + check-pod (`plugin: port`
via the migrated check-stack-layer + the new `plugin: dns` step, live). 5 submodule pointers
bumped.

### 2026-06-22 ‚Äî feat(charly): runPluginVerb dispatches CheckVerbProvider plugin units via RunVerb (executor enabler)

The `plugin: <verb>` dispatch (`runPluginVerb`) now type-checks the resolved provider: a
`CheckVerbProvider` plugin unit is dispatched via `RunVerb` (keeping the live `*Runner`), and
only an OUT-OF-PROCESS provider falls through to the serialized `Invoke` envelope. This
unblocks extracting the execution-needing goss verbs (`file`/`port`/`command`/‚Ä¶) ‚Äî which call
`r.Exec` and need the `*Runner` ‚Äî into builtin plugin units (the next Phase-1 step), the way
`matching` (pure, Invoke-based) already extracted.

Adds the canonical `examplerunverb` builtin plugin unit (a `CheckVerbProvider`, mirroring
`exampleprobe`'s Invoke form ‚Äî the in-proc-RunVerb analogue) + `TestRunPluginVerb_CheckVerb
ProviderKeepsRunner`, which proves `RunVerb` ran (not the `Invoke` stub) by reading `r.Mode`
off the live `*Runner` ‚Äî a value unreachable across the Invoke wire. Additive / dormant until
a goss verb extracts.

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. the new test + the builtin-schema-splice + reserved-word gates) +
`task build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 (root + box/fedora) + check-pod (the new
`check-runverb-plugin` step exercises the path live on the fresh rebuild). box/fedora pointer
bumped.

commit removed `matching` from the closed `#Op` but did not raise the schema version ‚Äî the

(`@ 2026.173.1615`, just before `calver-schema`) that auto-migrates an external config's
`matching:` check steps to `plugin: matching` + `plugin_input:` (`check:`+`matching:` ‚Üí
convert; an `agent-check:` step's vestigial `matching:`/`contains:` ‚Üí strip; idempotent,
`isStepNode`-gated, comment-preserving), and bumps `calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion`
`2026.172.0006` ‚Üí `2026.173.1616`. `gateSchemaVersion` now routes any un-migrated config
through `charly migrate`.

Every versioned file re-stamped to the new HEAD: the superproject root `charly.yml`, the Go
test fixtures + `testdata/` + the embedded `charly/charly.yml`, the per-host overlay
(`~/.config/charly/charly.yml`), and ‚Äî via `charly migrate` per repo ‚Äî all five

### 2026-06-22 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: extract the `matching` check verb into a dedicated built-in plugin unit (Phase-1 verb extraction)

The `matching` check verb is the FIRST verb extracted from the built-in `#Op`/`spec.OpVerbs`
set into a dedicated built-in PLUGIN UNIT (`charly/plugin/builtins/matching/`, mirroring
exampleprobe) ‚Äî the canonical Phase-1 "every verb is a plugin" pattern. The verb leaves the
closed `#Op` schema entirely; it is now authored as `plugin: matching` + `plugin_input:
{matching: <v>, contains: <matchers>}`, dispatched through the provider registry / Invoke
envelope, using the SDK-shared `sdk.MatchAll`.

Removed: `matching?: _` from `#Op` + `"matching"` from the `#OpVerb` union
(schema/_common.cue), the `Op.Matching` `Kind()` arm (spec/charly_methods.go), `matchingVerb`
(verb_builtins.go), `runMatching` (checkrun_verbs.go), the `matchingVerb{}` instance
(registry_bootstrap.go), `matching` from the `providers.verb` manifest (charly.yml), the
`VerbCatalog["matching"]` entry (checkspec.go), and a stale `cue_schema.go` comment (R5).
`task cue:gen` regenerated spec.

Cross-repo authoring migration (the verb left the shared `#Op`, so every authored site moves
in lockstep): the 2 real `box/arch` `check:` steps (`ah-matching-list`, `matching-smoke`) ‚Üí
`plugin: matching` (matcher forms verbatim); the 2 vestigial root-`charly.yml` `agent-check:`
steps (`kv-matching`, `default-step-9`) had their IGNORED `matching:`/`contains:` Op fields
stripped ‚Äî the agent grader reads only the step prose (`buildGraderPrompt`), so those fields
never executed. box/arch + box/fedora pointers bumped.

gengotypes note: `cue exp gengotypes` v0.16.1 degrades the `#MatchingInput.contains` matcher
disjunction to `any`, so `matchingProvider.Invoke` decodes the typed `Matching` from the
generated struct and re-decodes `contains` through the shared `MatcherList` JSON codec (R3) ‚Äî
no hand-written matcher type.

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. `TestRunner_MatchingPlugin` exercising the full `runPluginVerb ‚Üí
validate plugin_input against #MatchingInput ‚Üí Invoke ‚Üí MatchAll` path, the reserved-word
bijection gates, and the builtin schema-splice gate) + `task build:charly` + `charly box
validate` exit 0 across superproject + box/arch + box/fedora + check-pod (the disposable bed's
new `check-matching-plugin` step exercises the plugin verb live on the fresh rebuild).

### 2026-06-22 ‚Äî refactor(charly): goss matchers ‚Üí the plugin SDK (the Phase-1 verb-extraction prerequisite)

The 5 pure goss-matcher functions (`matchAll`/`matchOne`/`matchNumeric`/`matchValueString`/
`matchValueStrings`, formerly in `package main` charly/checkrun.go) move into the plugin SDK
(`charly/plugin/sdk/matchers.go`) as `MatchAll`/`MatchValueString`/`MatchValueStrings`
(exported) + `matchOne`/`matchNumeric` (SDK-internal), with `type Matcher = spec.Matcher`
re-exported so an out-of-process verb plugin reaches the matcher contract through the SDK
ALONE. This is the prerequisite for extracting ANY check verb: external verb plugins cannot
import `package main`, so the single shared matcher implementation (core goss verbs AND
future external verb plugins ‚Äî R3) has to live in the SDK first.

The 12 core call sites (checkrun.go √ó6, checkrun_verbs.go √ó4, checkrun_charly_verbs.go √ó2)
now call `sdk.MatchAll`/`sdk.MatchValueString`. Two tests that called the now-SDK-internal
`matchOne` directly relocate from checkrun_test.go into the SDK package's matchers_test.go
(R5 ‚Äî tests live with the code). The SDK now pulls `charly/spec` (‚Üí `gopkg.in/yaml.v3`) into
its dependency closure, so the two out-of-tree example plugin modules
(`candy/plugin-example-{deploy,external}/go.mod`) gain `gopkg.in/yaml.v3 // indirect` ‚Äî an
intrinsic consequence of routing `Matcher` through the SDK.

R10: `go test ./...` (full suite incl. the new `plugin/sdk` matcher tests + the two external
plugin e2e tests that build against the new SDK closure) + `task build:charly` + check-pod
(the disposable bed's `file`/`command`/`port`/`service` goss checks exercise `sdk.MatchAll`
live on the fresh rebuild ‚Äî the moved matchers' actual consumer). The matcher operator set is
byte-for-byte unchanged; this is a pure relocation.

data item. doctor.go reads it via `parseEmbeddedDeviceDescriptions()` over the shared

Extends the external-command-plugin path to NESTED commands, so the Phase-1 dep-shed targets
`charly check kube`/`adb`/`appium` can be served out-of-process (where their client-go /
selenium will live). RDD-proven first: `kong.Plugins` embedded in a NESTED command node
injects a dynamic `reflect.StructOf` subcommand there, not only at the CLI root.

`collectExternalCommandPlugins` now returns `(topLevel, nestedByParent, table)`: a
ClassCommand provider implementing the new `NestedCommandProvider` interface
(`CommandParent() string`) nests under that parent; everything else stays top-level. The
dispatch table is keyed by the full command PATH (`commandPathKey` strips Kong's trailing
` <args>`: `"check kube <args>"` ‚Üí `"check kube"`), and main.go dispatches via that path key.
`CheckCmd` (check_cmd.go) embeds `kong.Plugins`; main sets `cli.Check.Plugins =
nestedByParent["check"]`. The dead `firstCommandWord` is removed (R5 ‚Äî replaced by
`commandPathKey`).

R10: `TestExternalCommandSeam_NestedCheckCommand` builds a `NestedCommandProvider`, nests it
under a CheckCmd-shaped parent (kong.Plugins embed + a static sibling), parses
`check examplekube nodes --wide`, asserts the path key `"check examplekube"`, and confirms
the pass-through args reach Invoke; the top-level seam test + `TestCommandSeam_PluginCommand
Injected` still pass; `go test ./...` + `task build:charly` + `charly version` + `charly check
--help` (all 36 builtin check subcommands intact ‚Äî empty nested embed is a no-op) + `charly
box validate` + check-pod (the live check-command + CLI-dispatch flow, no regression). Dormant
until a real nested command plugin registers (the kube/adb/appium extractions).

The enabler that unblocks the Phase-1 dep-shedding command extractions (`charly check kube`
‚Üí client-go, `check adb`/`appium` ‚Üí selenium, etc.): a command can now be served by an
OUT-OF-PROCESS plugin, not just a compiled-in `CommandProvider`. RDD-proven first
(`reflect.StructOf` builds a Kong-parseable command, the selected command is detectable, and
the parsed flags read back via reflection ‚Äî GO).

`collectExternalCommandPlugins` (provider_command_external.go) builds a dynamic Kong
subcommand for every ClassCommand provider that is NOT a builtin `CommandProvider`: a
`reflect.StructOf` holder with one `cmd:""` field per command whose value is a pass-through
`Args []string` (the plugin owns its own flag parsing via its `.cue`). Because
`reflect.StructOf` types have no methods, these commands carry no `Run()` for Kong's
`ctx.Run()` ‚Äî so main.go dispatches them MANUALLY after `kong.Parse`: when the selected
command's first word matches the dispatch table, `dispatchExternalCommand` forwards the
pass-through args to the provider's `Invoke` (the standard envelope); everything else runs
through `ctx.Run()` unchanged. The seam is dormant-but-tested until a real external command
plugin registers (the Phase-1+ extractions) ‚Äî mirroring E3-kind / the builtin command seam.

R10: `TestExternalCommandSeam_DynamicCommandDispatch` builds a dynamic command, parses
`examplecmd nodes --wide`, and confirms the pass-through args (flag included) reach a fake
provider's Invoke; `go test ./...` (full suite, the builtin command seam unregressed) +
`task build:charly` + `charly version` (the CLI runs with the new machinery: empty external
table ‚Üí normal dispatch) + `charly box validate` + check-pod (the live CLI-dispatch flow
exercises the new collect+table-check path with no external commands registered ‚Üí `ctx.Run()`,
no regression).

The per-distro-family OVMF firmware candidate path pairs (fedora/arch/debian √ó

`charly.yml`. Only the PATH DATA moves ‚Äî the alias‚Üífamily resolution (centos‚Üífedora,
manjaro‚Üíarch, ubuntu‚Üídebian), the secure-boot selection, and the unknown-distro union STAY
Go logic in `ovmfCandidatesForDistro`, which reads the family table (`ovmfPathTable`) via
`parseEmbeddedOvmfPaths()` over the shared `unmarshalEmbeddedDefaults` helper. `#NodeDoc`
(schema/node.cue) recognizes the directive; `task cue:gen` regenerated spec.

R10 (the resolution is exercised LIVE on real host firmware ‚Äî the correct gate, unlike a
BIOS VM bed which never touches OVMF): `TestResolveOvmfPaths_HostFirmwareResolves` runs the
exact path `charly vm create` uses ‚Äî `ResolveOvmfPaths(hostDistro, secure)` ‚Üí
`ovmfCandidatesForDistro` (now data-driven) ‚Üí `os.Stat` ‚Äî against the Arch host's real
firmware and confirms it resolves to existing `/usr/share/edk2/x64/OVMF_CODE.4m.fd` +
`OVMF_VARS.4m.fd`. `TestOvmfPathsFromEmbedded` proves `ovmfCandidatesForDistro` returns
byte-identical candidates (fedora-secure / arch-nonsecure / debian-secure / centos‚Üífedora
alias / gentoo‚Üíunion(6)). Plus `go test ./...` + `task build:charly` + `charly box
validate` (repo + box/fedora). The full UEFI VM-create boot is unchanged by construction
(byte-identical resolved paths); the live resolution against real firmware is the changed
behavior and it is verified.

Fixes a real teardown bug: `charly vm destroy`/`stop` reported success but left the
libvirt domain RUNNING, leaking the VM (surfaced when a failed disposable VM bed orphaned
its domain). Root cause in `gracefulStopDomain` (vm_libvirt.go): it early-returned on
`state != domainStateRunning` (so a paused/blocked/crashed domain got NO action), and its
running-path poll predicate was `serr != nil || state != domainStateRunning` ‚Äî which
returns "done" on a *transient* shutdown-in-progress/paused state OR a transient
`domainState` RPC error, WITHOUT forcing. `VmDestroyCmd` then called `undefineDomain` on
the still-active domain, turning it into a lingering transient running domain.

The fix: poll for `libvirt.DomainShutoff` specifically (not merely "not running"), skip the
graceful ACPI path for non-running active states, and ‚Äî the key guarantee ‚Äî
force-`destroyDomain` unless the domain actually reached SHUTOFF before the caller
undefines it. The graceful-flush-first behavior for a healthy running guest (so the
in-guest podman overlay store flushes cleanly) is preserved; the force only fires when the
graceful path did not reach SHUTOFF.

Diagnosed empirically (a direct `DomainDestroy` drove the live stray domain 1‚Üí5
running‚ÜíSHUTOFF, proving the hard kill works ‚Äî the bug was never reaching it). R10:
`TestGracefulStopDomain_ForcesActiveDomainToShutoff` creates a real transient libvirt
domain, suspends it to PAUSED (the non-running active state the old code no-op'd on), runs
`gracefulStopDomain`, and asserts SHUTOFF (fails without the fix); `go test ./...` +
`task build:charly` + the fixed binary cleaned the actual orphaned stray VM
(running‚ÜíSHUTOFF‚Üíundefined‚Üígone, verified via `virsh list --all`). Follow-up recorded
separately: `charly vm destroy --disk` on a *running* VM deletes the disk before stopping
(should stop-first); and the failed-bed partial teardown that orphaned the domain.

The second Phase-4 data-out-of-Go cutover, via the pattern the first established: the
`charly doctor` host-dependency install-hint table (binary name ‚Üí distro ID ‚Üí package
name, 19 binaries) moves from the hardcoded Go var `installHints` (distro.go) into an
`install_hints:` directive in the embedded `charly.yml`. distro.go reads it via
`parseEmbeddedInstallHints()` over the shared `unmarshalEmbeddedDefaults` helper;
`#NodeDoc` (schema/node.cue) recognizes the directive (`{[string]: {[string]: string}}`,
added to the top-level-key regex); `task cue:gen` regenerated spec. The two colon-bearing
`"AUR: yay -S ‚Ä¶"` values are YAML-quoted. `InstallHint`'s lookup/family-fallback/AUR logic
is untouched ‚Äî only the map's source changed, so its output is identical.
`TestInstallHintsFromEmbedded` proves the loaded map matches canonically (count + the
quoted AUR values + spot-checks). R10: `go test ./...` + `task build:charly` (R9) +
`charly version` (init-parse runs, no panic) + `charly doctor` (exercises InstallHint LIVE
with the data-driven map) + `charly box validate` (repo + box/fedora, exit 0) + check-pod
(no regression in the deploy flow).

### 2026-06-22 ‚Äî feat(charly): context_ignore_baseline ‚Üí the embedded charly.yml (Phase-4 data extraction)

The first Phase-4 data-out-of-Go cutover: the built-in build-context ignore baseline (the
16 VCS/binary-exclude + cache-hygiene globs that seed every image's `.containerignore` /
`.dockerignore`) moves from the hardcoded Go var `baselineContextIgnore` (generate.go) into
a `context_ignore_baseline:` directive in the embedded `charly.yml` ‚Äî data, not code.
generate.go now reads it via `parseEmbeddedContextIgnoreBaseline()` over the new shared
`unmarshalEmbeddedDefaults` helper (R3: factored from the registry-manifest reader
`parseEmbeddedProviderManifest`, which now also uses it). `#NodeDoc` (schema/node.cue)
recognizes the directive (added to the top-level-key regex, mirroring `providers:`), so a
project may override the baseline too; `task cue:gen` regenerated spec. The
